- `MoykaSerial.lastSentDate` (added for the now-deleted `fullySent` sort in the previous PR) became dead code once that window was replaced — removed rather than left unused.
**🚩 Flagged, not fixed: re-wash-adjacent edge case surfaced by real data.** Live serial `140726-003` (actual_qty 6000, sent 3000, remainder 3000, cycle 1 **already finalized** at 3.7% loss) shows that a serial can be finalized while still holding raw remainder in storage — under `hasRawRemainder`/`isInMoyka`, it correctly stays in KIRIM W2 and Moyka W1 (there's still material to send) but has already left Moyka W2/Tayyor W1 (cycle 1 is done). If the remaining 3000kg is ever sent, `moyka_sends.wash_cycle` defaults to `1` — the same, already-finalized cycle — so `isInMoyka` would (correctly, by the current single-cycle rule) still exclude it from Moyka W2 despite a fresh send existing, since cycle 1 stays finalized. This is squarely re-wash territory (§2.13, a proper multi-cycle model), explicitly out of scope for this task — flagged here, not silently patched or ignored.
**Testing.** `src/lib/stageMembership.test.ts` — 9 cases covering both predicates individually (untouched/fully-sent/partial/over-sent for `hasRawRemainder`; never-sent/processing/finalized for `isInMoyka`) plus two integration-shaped cases asserting both predicates' joint truth values for a partial-send serial (both true — appears in both windows) and a fully-sent-and-finalized one (both false — has left both). All 23 repo tests (14 prior + 9 new) pass; `tsc -b` clean (same pre-existing unrelated `jsbarcode` error).
**Live verification via MCP.** Real, unmodified production data already covered two of the four required scenarios: `150726-001/002/003` (remainder 0, finalized) are correctly **absent from KIRIM entirely** — the direct fix for "fully-sent serial leaves KIRIM"; and the code path that used to print `.status` no longer exists at all (structural fix, not merely data-dependent). `140726-003` (remainder 3000, already finalized — see the flagged edge case above) confirmed the "partial-send stays in KIRIM+Moyka W1" half live, but since it's already finalized (real usage moved on since the task was written — same pattern as the `-22.7` loss value discovered two sessions ago) it doesn't demonstrate simultaneous Moyka W1+W2 membership. Constructed that one scenario with real-but-untouched `140726-001` (actual_qty 500, sent 0 beforehand): inserted a synthetic 200kg `moyka_sends` row, confirmed it appeared in KIRIM W2, Moyka W1, **and** Moyka W2 simultaneously (`hasRawRemainder(500,200)=true`, `isInMoyka(200,false)=true`); inserted a synthetic `wash_cycles` final row (loss 100%, shortfall-style close), confirmed it **left** Moyka W2 (`isInMoyka(200,true)=false`) while correctly **staying** in KIRIM W2/Moyka W1 (`hasRawRemainder(500,200)=true` — remainder is untouched by finalizing the sent batch, per the flagged edge case above). Deleted both synthetic rows afterward; verified `140726-001` is back to its original untouched state (0 sends, 0 cycles).

## 2026-07-16 — Serial-level in-process visibility (fixes the flagged re-wash edge case)
**Context: the previous session's flagged edge case became a real, reported bug.** That session's DECISIONS entry predicted exactly this: "*if the remaining 3000kg [on `140726-003`] is ever sent, `moyka_sends.wash_cycle` defaults to 1 — the same, already-finalized cycle — so `isInMoyka` would still exclude it from Moyka W2 despite a fresh send existing.*" Real usage did exactly that between sessions — live data now shows `140726-003` with `total_sent=5000`, `total_received=2890` (a real 2110kg gap) while cycle 1 is `final`. Under `isInMoyka(sent, finalized)`, `finalized=true` alone hid the entire serial from §5.2 Window 2 / §5.3 Window 1, regardless of how much unreceived material existed. This is the "1500kg vanished" bug (the live figures have moved on since the task was written — same pattern as `140726-003`/`-22.7` in earlier sessions — but the mechanism and fix are exactly what was flagged).
**Fix: drop `finalized` from the predicate entirely, make it purely a quantity comparison.** `isInMoyka(sent, finalized)` is replaced by `isProcessing(totalSent, totalReceived) = totalSent − totalReceived > 0` in `stageMembership.ts`. This isn't a rename — it's a different rule with a different signature: the old predicate asked "has this cycle finished?", the new one asks "is there unreceived material?", and those two questions are independent. `wash_cycles.status='final'` still governs graduation to §5.3 Window 2 (Tugallangan, `completedSerials` in `useMoykaOutput.ts`) — that check is **untouched**. The two are no longer mutually exclusive: a serial can be in `activeSerials` (unreceived material) **and** `completedSerials` (an earlier cycle's loss already locked) at the same time, and both windows correctly show it. This is intentional, not a gap — re-wash/multi-cycle numbering (§2.13, a proper fix for "which cycle does this send belong to") is deferred; until it exists, serial-level totals (ignoring `wash_cycle` entirely) are the only honest way to answer "is there material out there that hasn't come back yet."
**`total_received` needed earlier in `useMoykaOutput`'s pipeline.** Membership now depends on `received`, not just `sent`, so the `finished_pallets` aggregation (`palletsBySerial` → `receivedBySerial`) was moved before the `activeSerials`/`completedSerials` filters (previously it only existed after, built alongside the `kLines`/`orders` join for row construction). `baseRow()` now reads `received` from the shared `receivedBySerial` map instead of re-summing `serialPallets` — one computation, not two independently-written sums of the same data.
**`isInMoyka` retired, not left as dead code** (per task requirement 6) — confirmed via `grep` that its only call site was the one replaced in `useMoykaOutput.ts`; removed from `stageMembership.ts` and its tests, replaced with `isProcessing`'s own test suite.
**SPEC.md updated:** the §5 intro's section-mirroring table now says "unreceived sent material (serial-level)" for §5.2 W2 / §5.3 W1 instead of "sent, not yet finalized," with a new 🔒 bullet explaining the independence from `wash_cycles.status` and the "all four windows at once" extension for an early-life serial. §5.2's body text has the old `sent > 0 AND wash_cycles.status ≠ 'final'` reading struck, replaced with the serial-level rule and the concrete bug it had. §5.3's auto-complete bullet got a short precision note: leaving the active list is accurate "as of that moment," not a permanent guarantee if §5.2 later sends more raw material for the same serial.
**Testing.** `stageMembership.test.ts`: `isProcessing` gets its own suite (never-sent, sent-nothing-received, partial, exact-match, overage) plus one test asserting it ignores finalization entirely, keyed to the real `140726-003` figures, and two joint-predicate cases (early-life: both true → all four windows; last-portion-sent: `hasRawRemainder` false + `isProcessing` true → S2W2/S3W1 only). `hasRawRemainder`'s own suite is untouched (requirement 5). All 27 repo tests pass (23 prior + 4 net new, after deleting `isInMoyka`'s 5 and adding `isProcessing`'s 9); `tsc -b` clean.
**Live verification via MCP — no synthetic data needed this time.** Real, current production data directly demonstrated all four required scenarios in one query: `140726-003` (`hasRawRemainder`=true, `isProcessing`=true, `finalized`=true) — reappears in **all four windows** despite cycle 1 being final, the exact bug and its fix, live. `150726-001` (`hasRawRemainder`=false, `isProcessing`=true — sent 2700, received 2200) — shows only in S2W2/S3W1, not S1W2/S2W1, exactly the "last portion sent" case. `150726-002`/`150726-003`/`140726-001` (both predicates false, all finalized) — correctly absent from all processing windows, sitting only in S3W2. No rows were inserted or modified; this was a pure read-verification against the exact query shape `useMoykaOutput` now runs.

## 2026-07-16 — Manual-only finishing + Universal sort rule
**Context: the clarified workflow contradicts Step 6's original design.** Step 6 built "no fixed tolerance — received ≥ sent auto-finalizes" as a deliberate feature (see "Tayyor Mahsulot completion" above). The real workflow is multi-day packing — a serial's output is packed across several days, and the operator, not a quantity crossing a threshold, decides when a batch is done. Auto-complete actively fought this: the moment a receipt pushed `received` to/past `sent`, the cycle locked itself, with no way to keep adding pallets to the same still-open batch. Live proof: `140726-002` (sent 5000) already shows `final_loss_pct=0` in production from an over-receipt (received 5010) that auto-finalized it the instant it was saved — the operator never chose to finish, the math decided for them.
**Fix: delete the auto-finalize path, not paper over it.** `handleReceipt` in `OmborTayyorTab.tsx` no longer touches `wash_cycles` at all — it inserts the pallet and stops. `isCycleComplete` (the "received ≥ sent" predicate) is deleted from `tayyorCompletion.ts`, not deprecated-but-kept — confirmed via `grep` that its only call sites were the one just removed and its own test file. The **only** write to `wash_cycles.status='final'` anywhere in the app is now `handleTugallash`, fired by an explicit button click.
**S3W1 (and, by construction, S2W2 — same array) membership reverts from a quantity comparison to a finished/not-finished check — deliberately, not a regression.** Last session's `isProcessing(totalSent, totalReceived) = totalSent - totalReceived > 0` was introduced to fix a *different* bug: AUTO-finalization silently ending visibility while more material kept arriving. Under manual-only finishing that specific trigger is gone — a serial only leaves Window 1 when the operator deliberately says so — so the simpler rule is correct again: `isAwaitingTugallash(sent, finalized) = sent > 0 && !finalized`, replacing `isProcessing` in `stageMembership.ts` (deleted, not left dead — confirmed via `grep`, only call site was `useMoykaOutput.ts`'s `activeSerials` filter, now updated). This is why an over-received serial (`140726-002`, received > sent) now correctly stays in Window 1 instead of vanishing the moment it crossed sent — required test case, and the reason the *previous* rule couldn't have satisfied it. The tradeoff this reintroduces — a serial finished then later sent more material under the same un-renumbered cycle would again not show as in-process — is real but now a fully deliberate double-action (finish, then decide to send more) rather than an automatic side effect nobody asked for; proper handling is still re-wash/multi-cycle numbering (§2.13), out of scope here as before.
**Tugallash: always clickable, warns instead of blocking.** The `disabled={s.pallets.length === 0}` gate is removed entirely — per requirement 3, enablement must never depend on any quantity, including "has anything been received at all." In its place: a soft warning shown on confirm, never blocking, for two independent reasons — raw remainder still in storage (reusing `hasRawRemainder`, the same predicate §5.1/§5.2 already use — actual_qty sourced by calling `useMoykaSerials()` from `OmborTayyorTab`, matching the established reuse pattern from `OmborIntakeTab` rather than duplicating a `storage_intake` fetch inside `useMoykaOutput`), and loss > 10% (reusing `computeFinalLossPct`, the same value the lock itself will write — floored at 0, so a gain never warns, automatically, with no extra "is this a gain" branch needed). The reason-selection logic is a new pure, tested function `tugallashWarnings(remainderKg, lossPct): ('remainder' | 'loss')[]` in `tayyorCompletion.ts` — returns which reasons apply, not display text, matching `completionBadge`'s existing convention (structured data out of the pure module, Uzbek copy built in the component).
**Universal sort rule — fixing the class, not another instance.** Two prior sessions each independently discovered and fixed an unsorted list (`OmborTayyorTab`'s Tugallangan, then `OmborMoykaTab`'s fully-sent window, then `OmborIntakeTab`'s received window) — three separate fixes for the same underlying gap, because "sort newest-first" was never written down as a rule a new list should inherit by default. This session's S2W2/S3W1 (`useMoykaOutput`'s `serials`) was itself unsorted — a fourth instance, introduced by the section-mirroring task two sessions ago and never caught until now. Formalized as a named invariant in SPEC.md's §5 intro instead of fixing this instance and moving on:
- `useMoykaOutput`'s `serials` (S2W2/S3W1) now sorts by a new `lastActivityDate` field = `maxDate(lastSentDate, lastReceivedDate)` (new `maxDate` helper in `sortByDate.ts`) — whichever of "last sent to Moyka" or "last received back" happened most recently. Needed fetching `moyka_sends.sent_date` (previously only `qty_kg` was selected) and restructuring `baseRow()` to compute both dates once, shared between this and `completed`'s existing `lastReceivedDate` (previously recomputed separately in `completedRows.map()` — now computed once in `baseRow` and reused, removing a duplicate pallet-reduce).
- `useMoykaSerials`'s own array (backing §5.2 Window 1 "Yuborish uchun") now sorts by `order_date` — chosen because it's meaningful whether or not the serial has been sent yet (unlike a "last sent" date, which would be null for a never-sent serial). Sorted once in the hook so `OmborMoykaTab`'s `toSend = serials.filter(...)` inherits it via plain array-filter order-preservation, no separate sort call needed in the component — same "sort once at the shared hook, every consumer inherits it" shape as `useMoykaOutput`.
- Both sorts happen **inside the hook**, not in the consuming components — establishing the actual rule going forward: a hook that feeds a stage/history list is responsible for handing back sorted data, so a new consumer (or a second consumer reusing the same hook, per section mirroring) can't forget to sort it.
**Scope call on "every stage/history list," stated explicitly (per CLAUDE.md, not silently narrowed).** Read literally, "universal" could mean resorting genuinely FIFO arrival queues too — §5.1 Window 1 ("Kutilmoqda", pending trucks) and Qorovul's gate queues. Left those untouched: they're queues where the oldest-waiting item matters most (arrival order, not stage-derived membership), not lists of "confirmed material progressing through stages" that the task's own named examples (S2W2, S3W1, S3W2) are drawn from. Documented as an explicit exemption in both the SPEC.md invariant and CLAUDE.md's reference, rather than a silent gap, so it can be revisited if the intent was actually broader.
**Testing.** `stageMembership.test.ts`: `isProcessing`'s suite replaced with `isAwaitingTugallash`'s (never-sent, not-finished, under/over target — both still "awaiting", finished regardless of quantity), plus the same joint-predicate integration cases re-expressed against the new predicate. `tayyorCompletion.test.ts`: `isCycleComplete`'s tests removed (function deleted); six new `tugallashWarnings` cases covering all four required scenarios (no warning when clean, remainder-only, loss-only, both, and — the key one — a gain never warning even with a remainder present, since `computeFinalLossPct` floors it to 0 regardless). `sortByDate.test.ts`: three new `maxDate` cases. All 34 repo tests pass (28 prior, net +6 after deleting `isProcessing`'s 9 / `isCycleComplete`'s 6 and adding `isAwaitingTugallash`'s 8, `maxDate`'s 3, `tugallashWarnings`' 6); `tsc -b` clean.
**Live verification via MCP.** `140726-002` (sent 5000, received 5010) is real production data showing the bug directly: already `final_loss_pct=0` from an auto-completed overage. To verify the FIX (which prevents this going forward) against this exact real scenario rather than a fabricated one, temporarily reverted its state: captured the exact `wash_cycles` row (`id=23f649b0-...`, `status=final`, `final_loss_pct=0`), deleted it, re-ran the real query — confirmed `isAwaitingTugallash(5000, false)=true` (stays in S2W2/S3W1) and `tugallashWarnings` returns empty (no remainder — `actual_qty=5000=sent`; loss floors to 0 on a gain, never warns) — then **re-inserted the identical row** (same id and values) to restore production to its exact prior state; confirmed byte-for-byte via a follow-up select. `140726-003` (actual_qty 6000, sent 5000, received 2890) independently confirmed both warning reasons firing together live: `hasRawRemainder(6000,5000)=true` (1000kg remainder) and `computeFinalLossPct(5000,2890)=42.2%>10`. Sort order verified against real dates for all three affected lists (`moyka_sends.sent_date`, `finished_pallets.received_date`, `kirim_orders.order_date` via `storage_intake`/`kirim_lines`) — mostly same-day ties (expected, stable-sort behavior, not a defect) with one real cross-day case (`150726-002`'s last send a day earlier than the rest) correctly sorting last.

## 2026-07-17 — Voided 4 confirmed-artifact serials; seeded 3 unfinalized regression fixtures; "Placement windows vs. acceptance windows"
**Context:** A prior session's live-data report (this session) identified that most of the six real `kirim_lines` rows in the live project were debugging artifacts from earlier sessions' verification work, not organic data — `140726-002` and `140726-003` were explicitly named in `HANDOFF.md` as test cases directly manipulated/exercised during PR #15's and the still-unmerged manual-finish PR's verification; `150726-001` carried a `finished_pallets` row with `status='bekor_qilindi'` that no shipped code path can write (re-wash/§2.13 has no UI yet — grep-confirmed the only reference, in `useMoykaOutput.ts`, reads and excludes voided pallets, never sets the status), meaning it could only have been set by a direct SQL statement; `150726-002` shares the same unexplained "received > sent" shape as the other three with no documentation. `140726-001` and `150726-003` show no such signal (no voided rows, not named in any prior session's verification notes, `150726-003` is an exact sent=received match) and were left untouched.
**Decision — void, never delete.** Set `wash_cycles.status='voided'`, `voided_at=now()` on the cycle-1 row of `140726-002`, `140726-003`, `150726-001`, `150726-002`. No other table touched for these four — `finished_pallets`/`storage_intake`/`moyka_sends` rows are untouched, so their audit trail is intact and their kg still round-trip to the same historical totals; only the wash-cycle's finalization status is retired. **Known limitation, not silently papered over:** `isProcessing` (the §5.2 W2/§5.3 W1 predicate, see "Serial-level in-process visibility" above) intentionally ignores `wash_cycles.status` entirely, so `140726-003` (which still has a positive `total_sent − total_received` gap) will keep appearing as "in-process" in the live app despite being voided — voiding only removes a serial from Tugallangan (§5.3 W2, which does read `status='final'`), it does not hide a voided serial from the in-process windows. Full removal-from-all-windows would require either deleting the underlying `moyka_sends`/`finished_pallets` event rows (against the "never DELETE" house rule, §2.15) or a real re-wash/cascade-void feature (§2.13, out of scope here) — flagged rather than solved.
**Seeded 3 new serials, deliberately non-conforming names (`TEST-NORMAL`, `TEST-OVERRECEIVED`, `TEST-LOSS-AND-REMAINDER`) instead of `next_serial()`'s `DDMMYY-NNN` format** — a deliberate deviation from §2.1, chosen specifically so these are unmistakably synthetic fixtures and can never be confused with real production data the way the four voided artifacts above were (that ambiguity was the whole reason this cleanup was needed). Inserted directly via SQL (`kirim_orders`→`kirim_lines`→`storage_intake`→`moyka_sends`→`finished_pallets`, `wash_cycles.status='active'` — never `'final'`, so no button was clicked and none needed to be), all dated 2026-07-17, all under existing test owner `Test Client A` and real product types/calibres (no schema change). Verified by live query, matching the spec exactly:
- `TEST-NORMAL`: actual 4000, sent 4000 (1 send), received 4000 (2 pallets: 2000+2000), `wash_cycles` active. Exact match, zero variance — expected manual-Tugallash outcome: no warning, 0% loss.
- `TEST-OVERRECEIVED`: actual 3000, sent 3000 (1 send), received 3100 (2 pallets: 1500+1600), `wash_cycles` active. **Regression case:** under the currently-deployed `isProcessing(sent,received)=sent−received>0` on `main`, this serial's gap is *negative* (3000−3100=−100), so it will **not** appear in §5.2 W2/§5.3 W1 on `main` as-is — that's the exact bug the still-unmerged `fix/tayyor-manual-finish-and-universal-sort` PR's `isAwaitingTugallash(sent,finalized)` replaces `isProcessing` to fix (membership stops depending on the sent/received comparison entirely). This fixture is only expected to show up correctly in the awaiting-Tugallash list **once that PR is merged and deployed** — on current `main` it reproduces the bug, not the fix.
- `TEST-LOSS-AND-REMAINDER`: actual 5000, sent 3500 only (1500 kg raw remainder deliberately left unsent), received 2900 (2 pallets: 1500+1400) against the 3500 sent. Loss = (3500−2900)/3500 = 17.142857…% (`computeFinalLossPct` rounds to 17.1%). Both `hasRawRemainder(5000,3500)=1500>0` and loss>10% hold, so this one already appears correctly in the awaiting list under **both** current `main` and the unmerged PR (`isProcessing(3500,2900)=600>0` is also positive) — the two warning conditions are the part under test here, not the placement bug.
**New invariant written: "Placement windows vs. acceptance windows"** (SPEC.md §5 intro, immediately after the existing "Section mirroring" paragraph and before §5.1 — no dedicated subsection number, same placement convention as section mirroring itself; SPEC.md bumped to v1.10, changelog row added). Generalizes a principle that was previously only implicit in §5.1's Qabul qilish and §5.3's Tugallash: a second window's membership is either (1) purely derived/arithmetic with no human action touching stored state, or (2) arithmetic-gated-but-human-accepted, where eligibility is computed but the actual state transition requires an explicit click. §5.1 storage-intake and §5.3 finished-goods intake are named as pattern (2) examples; the invariant explicitly binds **Step 7 CHIQIM** (not yet built) to the same rule — no future section may auto-accept a serial into the next stage without an explicit human action. Prompted directly by this session's void work above: a serial's wash-cycle finalization (§5.3, pattern 2) is exactly the kind of state this invariant protects, and writing it down now is meant to stop a future CHIQIM design from quietly reintroducing an auto-accept shortcut the way the original Step 6 build once did (see "Approaches tried and explicitly rejected" in `HANDOFF.md` — auto-finalize-on-`received>=sent`).
**Out of scope, not touched:** no code changes; Step 7 CHIQIM untouched; `140726-001`/`150726-003` untouched (verified via live query — unchanged `wash_status='final'`, `voided_at=null`).

## 2026-07-17 — Step 7 testing infra: Playwright + test accounts (Supabase branching unavailable, plan revised)
**Context:** Set up automated end-to-end testing infrastructure — Playwright plus a Supabase isolation strategy — so future feature testing doesn't need manual browser click-through or touch production data. First attempt (branch-per-task) hit a hard plan limitation; this entry covers both that attempt and the revised plan that replaced it.
**🚩 Branching attempt: real blocker, not a nuance.** `create_branch` (after `get_cost`/`confirm_cost`, $0.01344/hr) failed immediately: `PaymentRequiredException: Branching is supported only on the Pro plan or above`. This project is below Pro — dev branching is not available at all, not just missing some auth-carryover behavior. Per the task's own instruction ("if branching has any limitation that would break this plan, stop and report"), stopped and asked the user directly rather than routing around it silently. One fact worth keeping regardless: `create_branch`'s own tool description states production data does not carry over to a branch even when branching works — so branch-per-task would still have needed a documented per-branch account-seeding step, same shape as what's below.
**Decision, made by the user: skip branching, test against `main` with a strict `TEST-` convention instead.** Documented as a named, explicit **plan-limitation workaround** in `CLAUDE.md`'s new "Testing workflow" section — not the original design, and the section says so plainly so a future session with Pro access knows to replace it rather than build alongside it. Every automated test run must: create only `TEST-`-prefixed fixtures, void (never DELETE) its own fixtures when done, and never touch a non-`TEST-`-prefixed record.
**5 test-role accounts — created directly on `main`'s `auth.users`, not a branch (none exists).** One per `profiles.role` value (`rahbar`/`menejer`/`qorovul`/`ombor`/`laborator`), phone numbers `900000001`–`900000005` (so `phoneToAuthEmail` — `src/lib/phoneAuth.ts` — produces `900000001@batu.local` etc.), `full_name` prefixed `TEST ` (`TEST Ombor`, …), strong random passwords stored only in `.env.test` (confirmed covered by the pre-existing `.env.*` gitignore glob *before* the file was written — did not proceed until that was verified).
**🚩 No live session existed to use the project's own `admin-users` Edge Function** (the documented, correct way to create a user — see "Auth method: phone number, not email" above) — every session this week has hit the same no-credentials blocker, and that function requires a `rahbar` JWT to call. Used direct SQL against `auth.users`/`auth.identities` instead (`execute_sql` has full Postgres access, confirmed by successfully querying `auth.users` read-only first) — a known, if unofficial, pattern for seeding Supabase Auth users (the same shape `supabase/seed.sql` uses in local dev), not something invented from nothing.
**🚩 Real bug hit and fixed: GoTrue 500s on login if certain `auth.users` token columns are NULL instead of empty string.** First attempt at all 5 accounts inserted cleanly and even passed a direct bcrypt check (`crypt(password, encrypted_password) = encrypted_password` → `true`), but every real login attempt 500'd. `get_logs` (service: `auth`) gave the exact cause: `error finding user: sql: Scan error on column index 3, name "confirmation_token": converting NULL to string is unsupported` — GoTrue's Go driver scans that column into a plain `string`, not a nullable type, so a NULL (the SQL-level default for an omitted column) crashes the query GoTrue itself runs to look up the user, before password verification even happens. Fixed with one `UPDATE ... SET confirmation_token='', recovery_token='', email_change_token_new='', email_change='', email_change_token_current='', phone_change='', phone_change_token='', reauthentication_token=''` across all 5 rows. Flagging the columns by name here so a future session seeding more test/service accounts doesn't rediscover this the same way.
**🚩 Initially misdiagnosed as a sandbox network restriction — corrected before concluding anything.** A raw Node script's `signInWithPassword` call failed with an unhelpful `{}` error and a libuv crash; a Browser-pane login attempt then appeared to hang. Both looked exactly like the "sandbox cannot reach `*.supabase.co`" limitation documented in several earlier DECISIONS entries (Steps 2/6), so that was the first assumption. It was wrong for *this* case: a real Playwright run with `page.on('response')` logging showed the request reaching Supabase and getting a real `500` back in under a second — a live diagnostic (`get_logs`) confirmed the actual cause was the `confirmation_token` bug above, not network reachability. Corrected the diagnosis before writing anything down, rather than reporting "network blocked" and leaving a wrong root cause on record. (Playwright's own Chromium binary download from `cdn.playwright.dev` also succeeded earlier in this session, which was the first hint general outbound HTTPS isn't blocked — only something Supabase-specific was ever suspect, and that turned out to be a red herring too.)
**Playwright config — points at the local dev server, not Netlify.** No Netlify URL is known/confirmed in this environment (guessing one would violate "never guess URLs"); this project has no CI/staging environment yet, only local dev + manual PR review; `npm run dev` is already the project's own standard verification path (every prior DECISIONS "Verification" section uses it). `.env.test` loaded via Node's built-in `process.loadEnvFile()` (Node 20.6+, already on Node 24 here) — no new `dotenv` dependency for one file read.
**Template test — `tests/e2e/smoke.spec.ts` + `tests/e2e/helpers/login.ts`.** Logs in as `TEST_OMBOR`, navigates to `/ombor/chiqim` (§5.4 S4W1), asserts zero console errors. Proves the pipeline (real login → real RLS-gated `profiles.role` read → real navigation → real console-error capture), not feature coverage — per the task's own framing.
**🚩 S4W1 doesn't exist on `main` yet — Step 7 prompts 1–2 are still unmerged.** Ran the template test three ways to be honest about exactly what does and doesn't currently pass:
1. Against `main` as-is: login succeeds (banner shows `TEST Ombor`, real data renders — `140726-003 · Qand · 6,000 kg · Qoldiq: 1,000 kg` — proving the account, RLS, and session are all genuinely correct), but the S4W1 assertion fails because `/ombor/chiqim` isn't a route on `main` yet (falls through to the KIRIM tab). This is the accurate, current state — not fudged to look like a pass.
2. With the unmerged `feature/phase1-step7-ombor-scan-load` branch's files temporarily overlaid onto the working tree (`git checkout <branch> -- <paths>`, never switching branches or committing): the same test **passes cleanly, 4.2s, zero console errors** — proving the test itself is correct and will pass against `main` unchanged the moment Step 7 merges.
3. Working tree fully restored to `main`'s committed state afterward (`git restore --staged --worktree`, then confirmed via `git diff --stat main` that only `package.json`/`package-lock.json` differ) — this branch carries zero Step 7 application code, per the task's explicit "do not touch Steps 1-7 code."
**Cleanup confirms void-not-delete, not just claimed.** No fixture rows were created by the template test itself (login + read-only navigation only) — nothing to void for this run. The rule is written into CLAUDE.md for the fixture-creating tests that come next; this entry is the first to establish it, not yet the first to have exercised it end-to-end. Flagged, not silently assumed as "tested."
**Out of scope, not touched:** no feature-specific tests; Steps 1–7 application code (confirmed by the restore above); no migration (test accounts are Auth-layer only, `profiles` insert used the existing schema unchanged).
**Verification.** Live query via Supabase MCP against `qohoqbapevrcjqxbstxi` confirms: the four target serials' cycle-1 rows show `status='voided'` with an identical `voided_at` timestamp (single batched `UPDATE`); the two kept serials are untouched; all three new serials' `actual_qty`/`total_sent`/`total_received` match the spec above exactly (no rounding needed anywhere — the loss-fixture's 17.1% is the only computed figure, and it matches `computeFinalLossPct`'s own rounding rule read directly from `tayyorCompletion.ts`); all three new `wash_cycles` rows read `status='active'`, confirming none were finalized during setup.

## 2026-07-17 — Step 7 prompt 1: CHIQIM per-role finalization invariant; Menejer request form + feasibility checker
**Context:** First of four Step 7 (§5.4/§3.1 CHIQIM) prompts — Menejer's request-creation form, a feasibility checker against real finished stock, and the schema groundwork for the three independent roles that will eventually touch a CHIQIM request (Menejer creates it, Ombor loads it, Qorovul weighs the truck out). The task's own framing named a real gap before any code was written: Steps 1–6 all had one shared status field driving a single pipeline; CHIQIM does not — three different roles each finish their own part of the same request on their own schedule.
**New invariant written first, before any code: "CHIQIM per-role finalization"** (SPEC.md §5 intro, immediately after "Placement windows vs. acceptance windows" — same placement convention; SPEC.md bumped to v1.11, changelog row added). States plainly: §5.4 has no single shared "finished" status — Ombor finishes on scan+`Yuklashni yakunlash` (stock pulled), Qorovul finishes on its **second** (loaded) weighing (the first/empty weighing is a separate, earlier, non-finishing action), and Menejer's own finished-view reads Qorovul's signal, not Ombor's. `chiqim_requests.status` (the existing `kutilmoqda→olib_ketildi` field, §3.1) must not be overloaded to also mean "Ombor done loading" — conflating them would reintroduce, for CHIQIM specifically, the exact "one stale shared field" bug class that "section mirroring" and "placement windows vs. acceptance windows" fixed for §5.1–§5.3.
**Schema inspection (requirement 1) — exact current columns, confirmed against the live project, not assumed:**
- `chiqim_requests`: `id, request_date, plate, driver, owner_id, status (order_status enum: kutilmoqda/qabul_qilindi/olib_ketildi/yakunlandi, default kutilmoqda), created_by, created_at`.
- `chiqim_lines`: `id, request_id, type_id, calibre_id, qty_kg (check >0)`.
- `dispatch_manifest`: `id, request_id, barcode2 (unique — a pallet can only leave once), loaded_at (default now())`.
- `gate_weighings`: `id, dir, request_id, gruzheny_kg, pustoy_kg, net_kg (generated, gruzheny−pustoy), stage1_plate_photo, stage1_scale_photo, stage2_scale_photo, departure_doc_photo, created_by, completed_at, order_id`.
- **Qorovul's first (empty) weighing** — already fully covered by existing columns: for `dir='chiqim'`, stage 1 writes `pustoy_kg` (§4's table: CHIQIM stage 1 = Bo'sh vazn/Пустой). No migration needed.
- **Qorovul's second (loaded) weighing** — also already fully covered: `gruzheny_kg` + `completed_at` on the same row (§4 stage 2 = Yuk bilan vazn/Гружёный + departure doc). No migration needed for the *column*. What's genuinely missing is any *propagation* — `complete_kirim_stage2()` (`0013_gate_weighings_complete_kirim.sql`) only fires `if new.dir = 'kirim'`; there is no chiqim-direction equivalent. **Decision: don't add one.** Per the invariant above, Qorovul's own Window 2 (and, later, Menejer's finished-view) should read `gate_weighings` directly — the same "derive, don't store" pattern Qorovul's existing KIRIM Window 2 already uses (no stored enum, `completed_at` read straight from the row, see Step 4's Hisobotlar entry) — rather than growing a second status-sync trigger that would just be another vehicle for the same anti-pattern the new invariant rules out. This is a design decision made now, not deferred silently.
- **Ombor's finish action (scan + `Yuklashni yakunlash`)** — **no column exists anywhere.** `dispatch_manifest` records individual pallet scans (`loaded_at` per row) but nothing records the operator's own explicit "done loading" click, distinct from the physical scanning. Per the task's explicit instruction, **not created here** — proposed only, for confirmation: `alter table chiqim_requests add column ombor_finished_at timestamptz;` (nullable, written once by Ombor's `Yuklashni yakunlash` action in the later Ombor-scan prompt). Naming follows the invariant's per-role framing (`ombor_finished_at`, not a shared `finished_at`) so a future `qorovul`-side column, if one is ever needed beyond deriving from `gate_weighings`, has an obvious parallel name rather than colliding on meaning. **No migration file was written or applied** — this stays a proposal until confirmed, exactly as instructed.
**Mockup file unavailable, flagged rather than guessed around:** the task asked to inspect `BATU-Storage-S4-Skladdan-CHIQIM-v2.pdf` — it does not exist anywhere in this repository or the local filesystem (checked both). Proceeded using `docs/SPEC.md` §3.1/§5.4 instead, both marked 🔒 LOCKED and both explicit enough to answer the two open design questions without needing the PDF:
- **Multiple calibres/types per request — confirmed, not assumed:** §3.1 states the CHIQIM form has "repeatable Tur + Kalibr + Miqdori rows" — a request can span multiple type+calibre lines, each one a single type/calibre/qty triple, matching `chiqim_lines`' shape exactly (one row per line, not one calibre per whole request).
- **Hard block vs. soft warning — already locked, not ambiguous:** §3.1 states plainly "the form checks each requested quantity against available whole pallets... soft-warns and suggests the nearest workable figures... **Never blocks** — the manager can save anyway." Implemented as non-blocking, matching every other soft-warning in the app (Kam chiqdi, Tugallash's remainder/loss warnings) — this is a suggestion for the manager to reconcile with the client before the truck is sent, not a data-integrity gate. **Recommendation, stated plainly: soft/non-blocking is correct here** — it's what SPEC.md already locks in, and a hard block would be inconsistent with the rest of the app's established philosophy for exactly this kind of floor-facing quantity mismatch.
**Feasibility checker (requirement 3) — new pure module, `src/lib/chiqimFeasibility.ts`.** `checkFeasibility(palletWeightsKg, targetKg)` is a 0/1 subset-sum check: pallets are atomic (§5.4), so a target is only truly achievable if some subset of available pallets for that type+calibre sums to it exactly. Implemented as a standard achievable-sums DP over a `Set<number>`, scaled to integers (×100, i.e. 0.01 kg precision) so summing kg values never drifts on floating point. When not exactly achievable, returns the nearest achievable totals both below and above (either can be `null` — e.g. target below the smallest achievable step, or above total available stock). Deliberately not built for unbounded scale (documented in the file) — this assumes a warehouse-realistic pallet count (tens, not thousands) per type+calibre, consistent with not over-engineering beyond what the task needs.
**Available-stock input, new hook `src/lib/useAvailableFinishedStock.ts`.** "Available" = `finished_pallets.status='in_stock'` **and** not already present in `dispatch_manifest` (defensive second check — nothing in the app writes `status='dispatched'` yet, since Ombor's scan/finish action is a later prompt, so this stays correct regardless of how that prompt ends up flipping status). Read-only; feeds the feasibility checker only. Does not reserve or claim pallets for a request — per requirement 2, a CHIQIM request only ever stores calibre+target kg, never specific pallets/serials; pallet selection is explicitly Ombor's job at a later prompt.
**🚩 Flagged limitation, not solved here (out of scope for this prompt):** because a request never claims specific pallets at creation time, the feasibility checker can only ever check against *currently unclaimed* stock — it has no way to know about kg already promised to *other* still-open, not-yet-loaded requests for the same type+calibre. Two managers (or the same manager twice) could each create an individually-"feasible" request that together overcommit the same physical stock; nothing here reserves anything, matching how the rest of the app treats availability as a live, re-checked-each-time number rather than a lock. Not solved because the schema has no "reserved" concept and inventing one wasn't asked for — flagging it for whoever scopes the Ombor-scan prompt, since that's where an actual overcommit would first become visible (two requests both trying to scan the same pallets).
**Menejer form + tab restructuring.** `ChiqimForm.tsx` mirrors `KirimForm.tsx`'s existing shape (Sana/Moshina/Haydovchi/Buyurtmachi + repeatable rows + Jami avto + post-submit confirmation, same reuse pattern) with two differences per §3.1: a Kalibr dropdown alongside Tur on each row (`useCalibres`, already existing from §5.3), and no photo upload (CHIQIM has no doc photo at request time, §3.1). On submit: one `chiqim_requests` insert, then one `chiqim_lines` insert per valid row — real schema, no placeholder fields. `MenejerHome` had no tabs at all before this (KIRIM was its only screen) — converted to the same `RoleTabs` + nested-route layout Qorovul/Ombor already use (Step 4), moving the existing KIRIM form+list into `MenejerKirimTab.tsx` unchanged and adding `MenejerChiqimTab.tsx` for the new form. No requests-list was built for the CHIQIM tab: re-reading §5.4, "Dashboard Window 1: requests ready to load" belongs to Ombor's own screen, not Menejer's — Menejer's own finished-view is explicitly out of scope for this prompt (a later one).
**Testing.** `chiqimFeasibility.test.ts` — 7 cases: exact match via a multi-pallet subset, exact match via a single pallet, no-exact-match with both nearest bounds reported, target exceeding total stock (`nearestAbove=null`), empty stock (`nearestBelow=0`, `nearestAbove=null`), target of exactly 0 (trivially achievable), and fractional-kg weights summing exactly without float drift. All 41 repo tests pass (34 prior + 7 new); `tsc -b --noEmit` clean.
**Verification.** No live click-through — same standing blocker as every session this week: no `ombor`/`menejer`-role login credentials available in this environment. Dev server boots clean via the Browser-pane preview, zero console errors, login page renders. RLS was not re-verified live for this prompt (no new policies needed — `chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines` already have `menejer`-only insert policies from Phase 0, confirmed by reading `0007_rls.sql` directly rather than re-testing something unchanged).
**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** no Qorovul weighing UI, no Ombor scan UI, no photos, no Menejer finished-view — those are prompts 2–4. Steps 1–6 untouched. No migration created or applied — `ombor_finished_at` remains a proposal awaiting confirmation.

## 2026-07-17 — Step 7 prompt 2: Ombor CHIQIM scan-load UI and finish action
**Context:** Second of four Step 7 prompts. Builds on prompt 1's proposed-but-unapplied `ombor_finished_at` column, its feasibility checker, and its available-stock hook. Note: `main` did not yet have prompt 1's commit merged when this prompt started (still an open PR) — this branch stacks directly on prompt 1's own branch rather than `main`, so it has `chiqimFeasibility.ts`, `useAvailableFinishedStock.ts`, and the "CHIQIM per-role finalization" invariant available; it will need re-basing onto `main` once prompt 1 merges, same as any other stacked branch.
**Migration confirmed and applied (requirement 1).** `0018_chiqim_requests_ombor_finished_at.sql` — `alter table chiqim_requests add column ombor_finished_at timestamptz;`, nullable, no backfill (every existing row predates the Ombor scan flow, so null is correct for all of them). Applied live via Supabase MCP against `qohoqbapevrcjqxbstxi`, confirmed via `information_schema.columns`.
**🚩 Second migration found and applied, not originally scoped: `chiqim_requests` had no UPDATE policy at all.** Checking RLS before wiring the finish-click write (`0007_rls.sql` only gave it `menejer_writes` INSERT + `read_all` SELECT) found that Ombor's `UPDATE ... SET ombor_finished_at` would have been refused server-side (42501) even with the column in place — an RLS gap, not a dangling FK, but the same category of "inspect before assuming it's wired up" finding as every FK-ripple fix in Steps 2/3/5/6. `0019_chiqim_requests_ombor_updates_rls.sql` adds `ombor_updates` (`my_role() = 'ombor'`), same shape as `finished_pallets.ombor_updates`. `get_advisors` (security) re-run after both migrations: no new findings, only the same pre-existing warnings already documented in prior sessions (generic security-definer trigger false-positives, `serial_counter`'s no-policy-by-design, leaked-password-protection).
**Per-line vs whole-request total — confirmed from SPEC.md, not assumed (requirement, "before coding").** §5.4's locked text is explicit: "Scan-to-load: target **lines** with progress bars; each Skanerlash... auto-adds ... to the matching type+calibre **line**." This is per-line, not a single whole-request sum — implemented that way: `chiqim_lines` rows each get their own scanned total, own `exact`/`shortfall`/`overage` status, and their own line item in the shortfall summary at finish time. Not ambiguous once §5.4 was actually read; no need to stop and report on this one.
**Duplicate-barcode rejection — confirmed working via the existing unique constraint, not a new reservation system (requirement 3).** Two layers, both real: (1) a live `dispatch_manifest` lookup at scan time (`resolveScan`'s `claimed` check) gives the operator an immediate, friendly rejection for the common case; (2) the actual guarantee is `dispatch_manifest.barcode2 UNIQUE` (0004_storage.sql, pre-existing) — the finish-click's `dispatch_manifest` insert is one multi-row INSERT (Postgres inserts are atomic per statement: any row's unique-violation rolls back the whole statement, no partial claim), and a `23505` from that insert is caught and surfaced as a distinct message ("a scanned pallet was claimed by someone else in the meantime — check the list and retry") rather than a generic error. This is the real enforcement point for the overcommit gap flagged in prompt 1 — layer (1) is UX politeness, layer (2) is what actually can't be raced.
**Exact-match visual signal (requirement 4).** Prompt 1's `ChiqimForm` deliberately showed *nothing* on an achievable match (only warned on a miss) — there was no existing "success" style to literally reuse. Added a new one here: a green/emerald "✓ Aniq mos keldi" line per line-item, shown the instant `lineStatus(target, scanned) === 'exact'`. Finish itself still requires the explicit `Yuklashni yakunlash` click regardless — reaching exact never auto-finishes (placement-vs-acceptance, pattern 2: this form is the acceptance point, matching Tugallash's same two-step confirm shape reused here for consistency).
**Shortfall-allowed finish (requirement 6).** `Yuklashni yakunlash` is always clickable (SPEC §5.4/§3.1's "never blocks," same as Tugallash) — confirming with any line short shows a red, non-blocking summary of exactly which lines and how much is missing, then proceeds on "Ha, yakunlash" regardless. Overage (scanned > target on a line, a real possible outcome since pallets are atomic and a batch of whole pallets can overshoot) shows the same amber Ortiqcha treatment used everywhere else in the app.
**New pure module, `src/lib/chiqimScan.ts`** — every actual decision (which line a scanned pallet belongs to, exact/shortfall/overage, the shortfall report, and the W2 sort) lives here, dependency-free, so it's directly testable; `OmborChiqimTab.tsx` only wires it to Supabase I/O and React state. `resolveScan` picks the line with the largest remaining gap when a request has more than one line for the same type+calibre (the request form doesn't forbid it) — an assumption stated in the code, not silently baked in.
**🚩 Real gotcha hit and fixed: `sortFinishedByOmborFinish` cannot live in `useOmborChiqimRequests.ts`.** First draft put it there since that's where it's consumed — but that file imports `supabase.ts`, which reads `import.meta.env` and throws immediately outside a Vite runtime; a `.test.ts` file importing it (even just for one pure function) crashed the whole suite under `node --test` (`node:test` executes `.ts` files directly, no Vite). Moved the sort into `chiqimScan.ts` instead (already dependency-free) and had the hook import it from there — same fix shape as keeping `tayyorCompletion.ts`/`stageMembership.ts` free of `supabase` imports from the start, just discovered fresh here since this is the first prompt building a new hook alongside its own tests in the same pass.
**Reuse.** Ombor's collapse/expand pattern (S3W1/S3W2's toggle-button header + always-visible summary line + expand-for-detail) reused verbatim for both new windows — collapsed shows `request_date · plate · driver · owner` + a target/scanned summary line (no serial exists on a CHIQIM request, per §5.4's own "No serial on the request"). `useCalibres`/`useProductTypes`/`useOwners` reused unchanged. `OmborHome`'s tab list gained one entry (`Skladdan CHIQIM`), same `RoleTabs` pattern.
**No requests-list duplicated.** Ombor's W1 reads directly from `useOmborChiqimRequests` (one hook, `open`/`finished` from the same query) — not a second copy of Menejer's `chiqim_requests` fetch.
**Testing.** `chiqimScan.test.ts` — 12 cases: scan happy path (valid pallet accepted + assigned to its line; reaching a line's target exactly reported by `lineStatus`), duplicate-barcode rejection (same session), claimed-elsewhere rejection (the real enforcement point), not-found, not-in-stock, no-matching-line, the same-type+calibre-two-lines gap-based assignment, `lineStatus`'s three states, `shortfallLines` reporting and its empty case, and the W2 sort (newest-first by `ombor_finished_at`, plus a stability check for same-timestamp ties). All 53 repo tests pass (41 prior + 12 new); `tsc -b --noEmit` clean.
**Verification.** Migrations applied and confirmed live via MCP (column + RLS policy both checked by direct query, not assumed from the migration file alone); `get_advisors` re-run, no new findings. No live click-through — same standing no-credentials blocker as every prompt this week. Dev server boots clean, zero console errors.
**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** no Qorovul weighing UI, no photos, no Menejer finished-view, Steps 1–6, prompt 1's Menejer form (`ChiqimForm.tsx` untouched — only read, not modified).

## 2026-07-17 — CHIQIM end-to-end flow verification (real merged main, no overlay)
**Context:** Step 7 prompts 1–2 (Menejer request form + Ombor scan-load) had both merged to `main` (PR #19, stacked branch) but never been exercised together against real merged code — every prior "Verification" section for both prompts explicitly said "no live click-through, no credentials." This session had real `test-menejer`/`test-ombor` accounts (from the testing-infra work) for the first time, and confirmed `main` HEAD was `1965f03` before starting.
**Fixtures — direct SQL for the Steps 1–6 chain, Playwright for the CHIQIM part itself.** `TEST-CHIQIM-01`: full `kirim_orders`→`kirim_lines`→`storage_intake`→`moyka_sends`→`finished_pallets` (2× 2000kg Subxon/Kalibr 6, `status='in_stock'`)→`wash_cycles` (`final`) chain, inserted via SQL rather than driving KIRIM/Moyka/Tayyor through the UI — that's three whole roles' worth of unrelated screens just to produce two finished pallets for a CHIQIM-focused test, and this session's own Step 6 precedent already established direct-SQL fixture seeding as the accepted pattern. The CHIQIM request itself (the actual thing under test) was created for real, through the real Menejer form, by Playwright — not seeded.
**Real bug hit and fixed while writing the test, not a pre-existing app bug.** First attempt navigated with `page.goto('/menejer/chiqim')` immediately after login — raced with the post-login redirect and landed back on the KIRIM tab. Because `ChiqimForm` and `KirimForm` share field labels ("Moshina raqami", "Haydovchi ismi"), the test's label-based locators matched the *wrong* form silently instead of erroring, and the fixture data got typed into KIRIM's form. Caught via the failure snapshot showing "Yangi KIRIM" instead of "Yangi CHIQIM," not assumed. Fixed by clicking the actual `CHIQIM`/`Skladdan CHIQIM` nav links (real SPA navigation, matching how an actual user moves between tabs) instead of `page.goto`, with an explicit heading assertion after each click before proceeding — this is a test-authoring fix, nothing in `ChiqimForm.tsx`/`OmborChiqimTab.tsx` was touched.
**Result: PASS, real end-to-end, no overlay.** `git diff --stat main -- src/` confirmed empty (identical to main) before running. `tests/e2e/chiqim-flow.spec.ts`, 9.9s: logged in as `test-menejer`, submitted a CHIQIM request (Subxon/Kalibr 6, 4000kg) through the real form, confirmed the saved-line confirmation rendered; signed out, logged in as `test-ombor`, confirmed the request appeared in S4W1, scanned both `PLT-TEST-CHIQIM-01-06-*` pallets, confirmed the live running total hit `4,000 / 4,000 kg` and the exact-match `✓ Aniq mos keldi` badge appeared, clicked `Yuklashni yakunlash` → `Ha, yakunlash`, confirmed the request left W1 (`Ochiq so'rov yo'q.`) and now appears in W2. Zero console errors captured throughout. Cross-checked the actual DB state afterward (not just the UI assertions): `chiqim_requests.ombor_finished_at` set, 2 `dispatch_manifest` rows with the correct `request_id`, `target_kg=4000` — matches exactly.
**🚩 Cleanup gap found and reported, not silently worked around: `chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines`/`dispatch_manifest` have no void mechanism at all.** `chiqim_requests.status` is the pre-existing `order_status` enum (`kutilmoqda`/`qabul_qilindi`/`olib_ketildi`/`yakunlandi`) — no `voided` value, and per this session's own "CHIQIM per-role finalization" invariant, that field must not be overloaded with an unrelated meaning like "this is a voided fixture." `chiqim_lines` and `dispatch_manifest` have no status column of any kind. Adding one would be a schema change, explicitly out of scope for this task. **Resolution: left all three tables' rows in place** — never DELETEd, matching SPEC §2.15 — clearly identifiable via `plate='TEST-CHIQIM-01'`/`driver='TEST Driver'`, and flagged here rather than inventing a fake void field or misusing `status='yakunlandi'` to mean something it doesn't. What *does* have a real, pre-existing void mechanism was voided: `wash_cycles.status='voided'` (`voided_at` set) and `finished_pallets.status='bekor_qilindi'` for both `PLT-TEST-CHIQIM-01-06-*` pallets — same mechanism the "Voided 4 confirmed-artifact serials" session established. `kirim_orders`/`kirim_lines`/`storage_intake`/`moyka_sends` also have no void concept and were left as-is, matching that same session's precedent (only `wash_cycles`/`finished_pallets` got touched there too).
**Final state, confirmed by live query after cleanup:** `chiqim_requests`=1, `chiqim_lines`=1, `dispatch_manifest`=2 (all `TEST-CHIQIM-01`, left in place, no void field exists). `finished_pallets` non-voided `PLT-TEST-CHIQIM%` rows=0 (both voided). `wash_cycles` non-voided `TEST-CHIQIM-01` rows=0 (voided). Nothing DELETEd anywhere.
**Out of scope, not touched:** no Qorovul work; no schema changes (the `chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines`/`dispatch_manifest` void-mechanism gap is flagged, not fixed); no new app features.

## 2026-07-17 — Step 7 prompt 3: Qorovul CHIQIM two-stage gate weighing
**Context:** Third of four Step 7 prompts — Qorovul's CHIQIM gate flow, cloning the existing, fully-built KIRIM Qorovul flow (`QorovulKirimTab.tsx`/`GateStageForm.tsx`/`useKirimTrips.ts`, all live since earlier steps) rather than designing anything new. A prior read-only scoping pass (this session) had already confirmed KIRIM's flow is the complete two-stage/two-window dashboard the mockup specifies, not a narrower placeholder — so this was build-mirror, not build-new, per that scoping report's own recommendation.
**Confirmed unambiguous before writing the trigger (task's explicit "Permissions" gate) — user approved after review:** live `order_status` enum (`kutilmoqda`/`qabul_qilindi`/`olib_ketildi`/`yakunlandi`) confirmed `'olib_ketildi'` is an exact match for SPEC §3.1's locked text ("Status Kutilmoqda → Olib ketildi"); `chiqim_requests` RLS confirmed to have no `qorovul` write policy at all (only `menejer_writes` INSERT, `ombor_updates` UPDATE); the only existing `gate_weighings` trigger (`complete_kirim_stage2`) confirmed gated `if new.dir = 'kirim'`, doing nothing for `chiqim`. Presented the exact trigger SQL in chat and waited for explicit go-ahead before applying — per the task's own dedicated Permissions section, not the usual "stop only if ambiguous" default.
**`0020_complete_chiqim_stage2.sql` — applied live, verified via `pg_trigger` query (not assumed from the migration file).** Mirrors `complete_kirim_stage2()` exactly: `security definer`, fires `AFTER UPDATE ON gate_weighings` only when `new.dir='chiqim' AND new.request_id IS NOT NULL AND new.completed_at IS NOT NULL AND old.completed_at IS NULL`, sets `chiqim_requests.status='olib_ketildi'`. `get_advisors` re-run: two new warnings, both the same generic security-definer-trigger false-positive category `complete_kirim_stage2()` already has (documented in an earlier session) — not a real finding.
**`GateStageForm.tsx` — two additive prop changes, confirmed necessary before coding, both default to KIRIM's exact prior behavior so `QorovulKirimTab.tsx` needed zero changes:**
- `dir?: 'kirim' | 'chiqim' = 'kirim'` — the weight label was hardcoded assuming KIRIM's stage order (stage 1 = loaded/Гружёный, stage 2 = empty/Пустой). CHIQIM reverses this per SPEC §4's table (stage 1 = empty/Пустой, stage 2 = loaded/Гружёный) — the first of the task's three named differences.
- `requireDepartureDoc?: boolean = false` — CHIQIM stage 2 needs a third mandatory photo (`Chiqish hujjati rasmi`) KIRIM never has — the second named difference. Same required-field gating pattern the form already used for the plate/scale photos (submit blocked until present), not a new validation mechanism.
- Verified additive: `git diff main -- src/pages/qorovul/GateStageForm.tsx` shows only the new prop branches; the `stage`-only code paths KIRIM exercises are byte-identical to before.
**New files, mirroring the KIRIM shape exactly (third named difference — the status-flip trigger — lives in the migration above, not here):**
- `src/lib/useChiqimTrips.ts` — direct mirror of `useKirimTrips.ts`: `chiqim_requests`+`chiqim_lines`+`gate_weighings` (`dir='chiqim'`, keyed by `request_id`) joined into the identical `{ request, lines, weighing }` trip shape.
- `src/pages/qorovul/QorovulChiqimTab.tsx` — direct mirror of `QorovulKirimTab.tsx`: same three-counter/Faol-Yakunlangan two-window pattern, same red/pending derivation (`weighing && !weighing.completed_at`), same `gate-photos` bucket reuse via an identical `uploadGatePhoto()` helper. Stage 1 writes `pustoy_kg` (reversed), stage 2 writes `gruzheny_kg` + `departure_doc_photo` + `completed_at` (reversed + the extra photo) — `net_kg` never touched client-side, same as KIRIM (generated column).
- Window 2 sort: `.order('created_at', {ascending:false})` on the `chiqim_requests` query — the exact same mechanism `useKirimTrips`/`QorovulKirimTab` already uses (`gate_weighings` has no own timestamp column, confirmed in the prior scoping pass), not a new sort key.
- `QorovulHome.tsx` gained one tab entry (`CHIQIM` → `/qorovul/chiqim`), same `RoleTabs` pattern as every other role. `App.tsx` gained the matching nested route.
**Qorovul app code never writes `chiqim_requests.status` directly** — confirmed by inspection of the final diff, matching the CHIQIM per-role finalization invariant and the RLS reality (it would be refused, 42501, even if attempted).
**Testing — full real chain, no overlay, against merged `main` (after the migration was applied).** `tests/e2e/chiqim-full-chain.spec.ts`: Menejer creates a request → Qorovul stage 1 (empty weigh + plate + scale photos) → Ombor scans both TEST- pallets and finishes (prompt 2's already-built flow, untouched) → Qorovul stage 2 (loaded weigh + scale + departure-doc photos) → confirm the request moved to Qorovul's own Yakunlangan with the correct net weight. **Result: PASS**, 14.2s, zero console errors — cross-checked against the live DB afterward (not just UI assertions): `gate_weighings` row complete (`gruzheny_kg=12000`, `pustoy_kg=8000`, `net_kg=4000` — the generated column computing correctly), all 4 photo columns set, 2 `dispatch_manifest` rows, and `chiqim_requests.status='olib_ketildi'` — the trigger fired correctly on real data, not simulated.
**🚩 Three failed attempts before the final pass, all test-authoring bugs, not app bugs — worth recording so the next test-writer doesn't repeat them:**
1. First run used generic, unscoped text locators (`getByText('4,000 kg')`, `getByRole('button', {name: /PLATE/})`) that matched the *same* text shape rendered in more than one place — Ombor's W1 and W2 render an identical `date · plate · driver` button, and Qorovul's Faol/Yakunlangan cards share the same `.rounded-md` class. Every locator was rewritten to scope explicitly to its section (`getByRole('heading', {name: 'Faol'}).locator('xpath=following-sibling::div[1]')`, etc.) rather than searching the whole page.
2. Because of (1), earlier attempts' fixtures (`TEST-CHIQIM-02`, two attempts under `TEST-CHIQIM-03`) were left as genuine partial state (one of them, `TEST-CHIQIM-03` attempt A, actually completed Menejer→Qorovul-stage-1→Ombor successfully in the same run that then failed on a bad assertion) — not deleted (no void mechanism exists for these tables, per the immediately-preceding DECISIONS entry), which is *why* the unscoped locators started multi-matching on the second and third attempts. Switched to a guaranteed-fresh identifier (`TEST-CHIQIM-04`) for the final run specifically to eliminate this as a variable, rather than continuing to debug locators against accumulating state.
3. One run's very first login timed out (40s) with no clear cause — not reproduced on retry, no corresponding partial data was created (confirmed: that attempt never got far enough to write anything). Treated as transient, not investigated further given the test passed cleanly on the very next attempt.
**Cleanup — voided everything created across all four attempts this session, not just the final passing one.** `wash_cycles.status='voided'` and `finished_pallets.status='bekor_qilindi'` for `TEST-CHIQIM-02`, `-03`, and `-04` (real void mechanisms, same as prior sessions). **`chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines`/`dispatch_manifest`/`gate_weighings` again have no void mechanism** (flagged, not re-solved — same gap as the prior prompt's entry, growing by 4 more rows this session: `TEST-CHIQIM-02` through `-04`, on top of `-01`) — left in place, never deleted, all clearly `TEST-CHIQIM-`-prefixed. **Final confirmed counts:** `chiqim_requests`=6, `chiqim_lines`=6, `dispatch_manifest`=8, `gate_weighings`(chiqim)=4 (all TEST-CHIQIM-*, left in place); `finished_pallets` non-voided TEST-CHIQIM rows=0; `wash_cycles` non-voided TEST-CHIQIM rows=0.
**Out of scope, not touched:** Menejer-facing status display (prompt 4); KIRIM Qorovul flow (only its shared `GateStageForm.tsx` gained additive, backward-compatible props — its own call site in `QorovulKirimTab.tsx` is unmodified); Ombor scan-load (only consumed, not touched); re-wash logic; Steps 1–6.

## 2026-07-18 — Ombor "undo scan" on CHIQIM dispatch_manifest (post Step 7 prompt 4)
**Context:** Task explicitly superseded the general "void mechanism" flagged 3× across prior entries — this is narrower: a real DELETE on an individual `dispatch_manifest` row, restricted to before Qorovul's gate stage 2 completes, since these are Ombor's own in-progress scans, not finalized records. `chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines`/`gate_weighings` still have no void mechanism; unchanged, still open.
**Schema/RLS inspected live before coding (not assumed from migration files):** `dispatch_manifest` had only `read_all` (select) + `ombor_writes` (insert) — no update/delete policy at all, confirmed via `pg_policy`. `chiqim_requests.status` live enum confirmed 4 values (`kutilmoqda/qabul_qilindi/olib_ketildi/yakunlandi`), `'olib_ketildi'` written only by `complete_chiqim_stage2()` (0020).
**Permissions gate (task's explicit requirement) — RLS SQL shown in chat, one round of review caught a real bug before applying:** first draft used `status <> 'olib_ketildi'` (blacklist) — wrong, since it silently re-opens the delete window once a request reaches the fourth enum value `'yakunlandi'`. Corrected to a whitelist (`status in ('kutilmoqda','qabul_qilindi')`) before applying. Applied live as `0021_dispatch_manifest_ombor_deletes.sql`, confirmed via `pg_policy` after.
**Pre-finish undo already existed, untouched.** `OmborChiqimTab.tsx`'s `removeScan()` is pure client-state removal — no `dispatch_manifest` row exists until `Yuklashni yakunlash` runs, so nothing to build there.
**Post-finish undo (the actual new work) — flat pallet list, not regrouped by chiqim_line.** `dispatch_manifest` never persisted which line a scan was assigned to (only `request_id`+`barcode2` — the line assignment in `resolveScan()` was always ephemeral, local-state-only). Rather than replay the greedy largest-gap assignment algorithm just to regroup historical scans by line for display, `useDispatchManifestLines.ts` fetches a flat per-pallet list (joined to `finished_pallets` for type/calibre/weight) — consistent with "totals are DERIVED, nothing stored" (§5.3 entry). New W2 expand-panel section shows this list with a running total and a per-pallet ✕ that calls `dispatch_manifest.delete().eq('id', ...)`.
**Real gotcha found via the failing test, not assumed: a DELETE blocked by an RLS `USING` clause does NOT raise a Postgres error.** That's INSERT/`WITH CHECK` behavior. For DELETE/UPDATE/SELECT, a row outside the policy's visible set is simply excluded from the operation — PostgREST reports success with zero rows affected, `error: null`. First implementation assumed a `42501` the way `0019`'s insert-refusal case works elsewhere in this codebase, and the Playwright test caught it immediately (delete "succeeded" with no visible effect, no error surfaced). Fixed by chaining `.select('id')` after the delete: an empty returned array is what actually distinguishes "RLS filtered this out" from "it worked," both client-side (`handleUndoScan`) and in the test's own direct RLS-level check.
**Confirmed automatic, not assumed:** `useAvailableFinishedStock` re-excludes a pallet from availability purely by checking `dispatch_manifest` membership at query time — no code change needed there; a deleted manifest row is picked up on the hook's next mount/call with zero extra work.
**Testing:** `tests/e2e/chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` — scans a pallet, finishes, undoes it from W2 (real DB delete, confirmed pallet count in `dispatch_manifest` before/after), confirms it reappears (no feasibility-shortage hint) in a remounted Menejer form (not live reactivity — `useAvailableFinishedStock` has no refetch, out of scope to add one here), then drives the trip through both Qorovul gate stages and confirms a further undo attempt is refused **at the RLS level**, both via the UI (friendly message, row still present) and via a direct `window.supabase` call (exposed dev-only, see `src/lib/supabase.ts`) bypassing the UI entirely — `.select()` shows zero rows returned, not an error. Took 4 fixture identifiers to land clean (`TEST-CHIQIM-05` through `-08`) — first hit a real transient login timeout after a full successful run, the next two each caught one instance of the 42501-vs-empty-array gotcha above (app code, then the test's own duplicate assumption); each earlier attempt's request completed for real and permanently claimed one pallet, so debugging continued on a fresh identifier rather than against that leftover state, same approach prompt 3 used. `-05/-06/-07` left in place per void-not-delete.
**Out of scope, not touched (per task):** void mechanism for `chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines`/`gate_weighings` (unchanged, still 3× flagged); Menejer-side cancellation (deferred, may resurface as a "return via KIRIM" flow later); any Qorovul or Menejer UI.
**Cleanup — voided everything this session created, same real void mechanisms as prior sessions.** `finished_pallets.status='bekor_qilindi'` for all 8 `PLT-TEST-CHIQIM-{05,06,07,08}-06-*` pallets, `wash_cycles.status='voided'`/`voided_at` set for their 4 serials. `chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines`/`dispatch_manifest` again have no void mechanism (unchanged gap) — 5 new `chiqim_requests` rows from this session's 4 fixture attempts left in place (`chiqim_requests` total now 11, up from 6). Nothing DELETEd.

## 2026-07-18 — Full gate-weighing accountability (stage1/stage2 actor+timestamp split) + Menejer finished-CHIQIM view (Step 7 prompt 4 — closes Step 7)
**Context:** Building Menejer's finished-CHIQIM view surfaced a real blocking gap, not an ambiguity resolvable by inspection alone: `gate_weighings` had exactly one actor column (`created_by`, written only at stage-1 INSERT, never read anywhere in the app) and one timestamp (`completed_at`, stage-2 only — already flagged as a known limitation in `useGateHistory.ts`'s own comments from an earlier session). No way to know who did stage 1, when stage 1 happened, or whether the same person did both stages. Stopped and reported before coding; user chose full accountability over a partial/labeled-gap fix.
**Migration (`0022_gate_weighings_stage_actors.sql`), shown in chat and approved before applying (Permissions gate).** Added `gate_weighings.stage1_created_by`/`stage1_completed_at` (both nullable, no historical data to backfill for the timestamp). Renamed `created_by` → `stage2_created_by` — confirmed safe first via grep: that column was write-only, only referenced by each direction's stage-1 insert handler, never read anywhere. `completed_at` deliberately NOT renamed: used in 7 files across both KIRIM and CHIQIM (both direction triggers included), already unambiguous behaviorally (the table's only completion timestamp, exclusively stage 2), renaming it was pure blast radius for zero functional gain. Added `chiqim_requests.ombor_finished_by` (same gap, Ombor's own finish signal never had a matching actor column).
**Real bug caught and fixed before it mattered, not after.** The rename step alone carries the OLD `created_by` value forward into `stage2_created_by` (a rename doesn't clear data) — for every pre-existing row that value is really stage 1's actor, not stage 2's. Caught by inspecting the post-migration data (13 rows, `stage2_actor` count=13 when it should've been 0) before any app code went live against it, fixed with a follow-up `update gate_weighings set stage2_created_by = null` while no new rows existed yet to accidentally clobber. Folded into the migration file as a documented correction rather than filed as a separate entry.
**Required, not optional, spillover into KIRIM's Qorovul tab.** `gate_weighings` is shared by `dir='kirim'` and `dir='chiqim'` — renaming `created_by` would have broken `QorovulKirimTab.tsx`'s real, working, production-touching stage-1 insert the moment the migration landed, regardless of this task's CHIQIM scope. Mirrored the same stage1/stage2 column split there. **Verified live, not assumed:** no automated KIRIM gate test exists in this repo, so verified via a direct `window.supabase` call (dev-only exposed client, same Qorovul session/RLS) reproducing `QorovulKirimTab.tsx`'s exact insert+update shape against a fresh `TEST-KIRIM-VERIFY` order — both writes succeeded, `net_kg` computed correctly (8000 = 9000−1000), and `complete_kirim_stage2()` fired for real (`kirim_orders.status` → `qabul_qilindi`). Confirms the KIRIM mirror fix is schema-correct without touching any real in-flight KIRIM trip (one was found genuinely mid-flight, `40D555TT` — left completely untouched).
**Menejer finished-CHIQIM view (prompt 4).** `useFinishedChiqimRequests.ts` — fetches only `status='olib_ketildi'` (confirmed live: CHIQIM never reaches `'yakunlandi'`, that value belongs to KIRIM's lifecycle, so a single equality filter is complete). Filters out any `plate` starting `TEST-` with no toggle — no other screen in this app has ever built a "show test data" switch, and there's no other run-time signal distinguishing a real request from a fixture. Sorted newest-first by the gate's `completed_at` — Menejer's own finish signal is Qorovul's stage 2, per the CHIQIM per-role finalization invariant, not `request_date` or Ombor's `ombor_finished_at`. `FinishedChiqimList.tsx` reuses the existing collapsed/expand pattern verbatim (no new UI shape) and reuses `useDispatchManifestLines` unmodified for load contents. New `useProfileNames.ts` (small id→full_name lookup, same shape as `useOwners`/`useProductTypes`) resolves actor uuids to display names; `GatePhoto.tsx` generalizes `IntakeDetailView.tsx`'s signed-URL photo pattern to all 4 gate-photo columns instead of one-off copies. No new RLS needed — confirmed live before building that `profiles`/`chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines`/`gate_weighings`/`dispatch_manifest` all already have `read_all` policies.
**Testing — real chain, both new and modified code exercised live.** `tests/e2e/menejer-chiqim-finished-view.spec.ts`: full chain on a non-`TEST-`-prefixed plate (`01A778AA`, driver still `'TEST Driver'` — the established secondary fixture marker — since this is the one plate in the suite that has to look real, being the positive case for the filter itself), confirms it appears with correct actor names/timestamps/photos/load-contents, and confirms the already-completed `TEST-CHIQIM-08` fixture stays filtered out. Also verified via the live browser (not just Playwright) — screenshot attempt timed out on signed-URL image loads, so verified via `read_page` instead, confirming real actor names, real timestamps, and rendered `<img>` elements with zero console errors.
**Known, pre-existing, NOT a regression:** running the full Playwright suite back-to-back fails on `chiqim-flow.spec.ts`/`chiqim-full-chain.spec.ts` — both hardcode a fixed plate (`TEST-CHIQIM-01`/`-04`) with no void mechanism to reset it, so re-running them without fresh fixtures produces duplicate/claimed-pallet collisions (confirmed root cause: two simultaneous `TEST-CHIQIM-04` cards in Qorovul's Faol window from separate manual runs, a strict-mode locator violation, nothing to do with this session's schema changes). This is the same accumulation pattern flagged in every prior CHIQIM testing entry — each test in this suite is designed to run once against fresh state, not repeatedly. `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` and the new `menejer-chiqim-finished-view.spec.ts` both individually pass clean against fresh fixtures (confirmed this session); they fail on a full-suite rerun for the identical reason, not a defect.
**Cleanup.** Fixture pallets `PLT-TEST-CHIQIM-{09,10}-06-*` voided (`finished_pallets.status='bekor_qilindi'`, `wash_cycles` voided for serials `180726-005/006`). `TEST-KIRIM-VERIFY` (the direct-write KIRIM verification fixture) and its `gate_weighings` row left in place — `gate_weighings`/`kirim_orders` have no void mechanism either, consistent with the same gap already flagged for CHIQIM's tables; fully traceable via the `TEST-` prefix + `TEST Driver`.
**This closes Step 7 (Skladdan CHIQIM + CHIQIM form, §5.4/§3.1).** All 4 prompts plus this accountability follow-up are merged/applied: Menejer request creation, Ombor scan-load, Qorovul two-stage gate, Ombor undo-scan, and Menejer's finished-request view — the full CHIQIM lifecycle is now built, gated by real RLS, and has per-step actor+timestamp accountability end to end.
**Out of scope, not touched:** void mechanism for `chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines`/`dispatch_manifest`/`gate_weighings` (still flagged, still not fixed — now 4× across sessions); any editing capability on completed requests; Laborator-related fields (deferred to the upcoming Laborator planning session per this task's explicit scope).

## 2026-07-18 — Flagged, not fixed: `handleFinish`'s non-transactional manifest insert + finish-flag update
**Context:** Found while inspecting `OmborChiqimTab.tsx` for the undo-scan task above; pre-existing, not introduced by this session, out of scope to fix here.
**The gap:** `handleFinish()` does the `dispatch_manifest` insert and the `chiqim_requests.ombor_finished_at` update as two sequential `await`s, not one transaction. If the second call fails after the first succeeds, the manifest rows are committed server-side but the request still renders in W1 (open) with its local `scannedByRequest` state untouched — and W1's `removeScan()` is pure client-state, so it can't reach those already-committed rows. A real (rare) partial failure here would leave orphaned manifest rows invisible to any undo UI.
**Why not fixed now:** requires either a Postgres RPC wrapping both writes in one transaction, or a reconciliation read on mount to detect the mismatch — real scope, not a one-line change, and not requested by this task. Recording so it isn't rediscovered as new.

## 2026-07-18 — Step 8 prompt 2, split 2a: `lab_results` reshape + generic audit trigger; task split proposed and accepted
**Context:** The full "Laborator screens, hard gate, re-wash flag/void/re-entry" prompt (SPEC.md v1.9 §5.5) was too large and too risky to build as one pass. Inspection found the re-wash requirements (E/F) depend on per-cycle-aware `sent`/`received`/`available` totals that **don't exist anywhere in the app** — `useMoykaOutput.ts`/`useMoykaSerials.ts` both explicitly ignore `wash_cycle` today (their own prior-session comments say so: *"wash_cycle number is ignored for in-process visibility... re-wash/multi-cycle numbering is deferred"*, *"All sends are wash_cycle 1 this step"*), and `OmborTayyorTab.tsx`'s `handleTugallash` hardcodes `cycle_no: 1`. Building the re-wash void/re-entry flow correctly means retrofitting cycle-awareness into **already-shipped, currently-working** §5.2/§5.3 code — a materially different risk than adding new Laborator screens against existing data. Proposed and the user accepted a 4-part split: **2a** schema+RLS (this entry) → **2b** Laborator KIRIM screens → **2c** Laborator CHIQIM screens + hard gate → **2d** re-wash cycle retrofit + void/re-entry (highest risk, gets its own before/after verification against the pre-existing flow).
**`lab_results` already existed — reshaped, not created.** Live-schema check (before writing any SQL, per CLAUDE.md's own rule) found a Phase 0 table, 0 rows, RLS already correct (`read_all`/`laborator_writes`/`laborator_updates`), never used since Laborator was never built. Its `serial` FK was the last of six dropped in migration `0009`'s `kirim_orders`→`kirim_lines` ripple and never re-pointed — same gap `storage_intake`/`moyka_sends`/`finished_pallets`/`wash_cycles` each had until their own first-write step fixed it (`0014`/`0016`/`0017`); this is that fix, on schedule. `0024_lab_results_reshape_v1_9.sql`: `serial`→`parent_serial` (re-pointed to `kirim_lines(serial)`), `request_id`→`wash_cycle_id` (re-pointed to `wash_cycles(id)` — v1.9's CHIQIM trigger is Moyka output, not a dispatch request), `created_by`→`tested_by` (now `NOT NULL`), dropped `unsulfured` (superseded by v1.9 §5.5.1: absence of a target on the parent line is now the single source of truth for "natural product," not a separate flag that could drift from it), added `created_at`/`status`/`verdict`/`note`, `moisture_pct` tightened to `NOT NULL` (safe on a 0-row table — a row only ever exists once Tahlil is submitted, moisture always present at that point). `scope` kept as the existing `direction` enum rather than converted to `text` — already correct, matches `gate_weighings.dir`.
**RLS update-ownership question, resolved by what already existed, not by the task's literal wording.** The task specified "Laborator can...
