**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` clean, `npm test` 79/79 unchanged after touching 18+ existing files and adding ~12 new ones. Live-browser-verified against both real test logins (`.env.test` phone-based accounts): as Menejer, added a client ("Sinov Mijozi QA") via the new Mijozlar screen and confirmed it appeared in the KIRIM form's Buyurtmachi dropdown with no reload needed (the new `refetch()` on `useOwners` did its job). As Rahbar, deactivated the product type "Qand qizil" and confirmed, in one pass: it disappeared from the KIRIM form's Tur dropdown (Menejer login); the Hisobot results table still printed "Qand qizil" (not a uuid) on serial `210726-008`'s historical rows; the Hisobot filter bar's own Tur dropdown still offered "Qand qizil" as a selectable filter; the serial passport for `210726-008` still printed "Qand qizil" in its Buyurtma header; and the client report for Farg'ona Eksport Guruhi still printed "Qand qizil" in both its byType breakdown and Section B quality record. Set `Sig'imi (kg/oy)` to 15000 and confirmed the Rahbar dashboard grew both a header stat ("Sig'imdan foydalanish (joriy oy): 24%") and a per-month trends column, with September correctly reading 24% (3,600/15,000 — matches §3.2.10's own raw_consumed_kg exactly); clicked Tozalash and confirmed both disappeared again, back to the exact pre-configured state. One real bug caught mid-verification and fixed: `ThresholdsSection`'s save button, first tested via a loose DOM-text-based JS selector, silently no-opped (the selector matched nothing usable) — switched to ref-based targeting via `read_page`, which is what actually caught it, and confirmed the save/clear round-trip against the database directly (not just the rendered UI) both times. Both test mutations (the deactivated type, the new client) were reverted/deactivated after verification to leave the fixture exactly as the previous phase left it, rather than leaving test debris in a dataset several other phases' verification depends on — "Qand qizil" reactivated, "Sinov Mijozi QA" deactivated (not deleted, per this task's own rule). Full Playwright suite not run, same reduced-testing rationale as every prior entry this session (would reintroduce `TEST-` debris).

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** user creation/management (stays developer-side), PDF, global i18n, the two known-failing e2e tests, any further UI polish on operational screens beyond the one-line hook-flag fix each needed.

## 2026-07-22 — e2e suite consolidation: 12 specs down to 4, self-cleaning fixtures

**Context:** The e2e suite had accumulated to 12 spec files with real overlap (several specs re-walking the same KIRIM→...→CHIQIM chain from slightly different angles) and no teardown — every run left `TEST-` debris in the shared dev database, and two specs were already failing outright after the clean-room reset (`docs/DECISIONS.md` "Clean-room reset for client-report verification") deleted the "Test Client A/B/C" owners every spec hardcoded. Reduced to 4 survivors, each justified by unique risk rather than habit, with self-cleaning teardown so the suite can run repeatedly against the shared dev database without manual cleanup.

**The 4 survivors and what each is the ONLY test covering:**
1. **`full-chain.spec.ts`** — KIRIM → gate → intake → Moyka → lab → CHIQIM → gate, single run, asserting actor/timestamp/photo data on Menejer's finished view. Subsumes `chiqim-flow`, `chiqim-full-chain`, `step9-single-product-full-chain`, `menejer-chiqim-finished-view` (including its TEST- filter negative case, via `seedFilteredFinishedRequest`), `laborator-kirim` (sulfured vs natural SO2 branching), and — as a free byproduct of an already-necessary 2-line order — `kirim-client-targets` (`target_so2_mg_kg` real `null` vs numeric) and `effective-qty.spec.ts`'s second test (multi-line reconciliation variance vs single truck-wide gate variance, neither ever showing the raw gate net).
2. **`rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts`** — fail lab, confirm pallets hidden from availability (`0 kg` feasibility), hard-block Ombor's scan with the exact refusal string, void, re-send, pass, then a real dispatch (new barcode, "✓ Aniq mos keldi") proving dispatchability is genuinely restored — not just re-enabled in the UI. Konditirskiy output from cycle 1 confirmed untouched by the void. Subsumes `rewash-full-cycle` and `laborator-chiqim-hard-gate`, merged onto the SAME serial (stronger than the originals' two-parallel-serial design — proves the full fail→void→pass→dispatch loop closes on one identity, not just that each half works in isolation).
3. **`chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts`** (kept, teardown added, no structural change) — the one test whose entire point is that a blocked DELETE returns zero rows via `.select()` rather than erroring or silently succeeding. This is enforced by the `ombor_deletes` RLS policy, not UI hiding, and historically caught a real silent-delete bug. Cannot be folded into any chain test without weakening the assertion (folding it in would test "the button doesn't appear," not "the database refuses").
4. **`report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts`** (kept, teardown added, no structural change) — the drift guard between `deriveEffectiveQty()` (TypeScript, `weightAuthority.ts`) and `report_kirim_rows` (SQL, the reporting engine's own independent re-implementation of the same derived value). Seeds all 5 branches directly (declared_pre_intake, single/multi-line provisional, multi-line final, gate-net final) and asserts both sides agree.

**Dropped outright, not folded in:** `reporting-query-engine.spec.ts` — reporting is read-only and was manually verified against a hand-computed reference dataset (`docs/DECISIONS.md` "Client report", "Yield view + Rahbar dashboard" acceptance checks) — stronger ground truth than an e2e assertion re-deriving the same numbers a second time. `smoke.spec.ts` — pure login-and-look, no assertion an actual test doesn't already make as a byproduct of logging in.

**Two known-failing specs, resolved by folding, not fixing in place:** `laborator-kirim.spec.ts` and `laborator-chiqim-hard-gate.spec.ts` were both failing post-clean-room (hardcoded "Test Client A", no longer exists). Rather than patch the owner reference and keep them as separate files, both were absorbed into survivors 1 and 2 above respectively — their actual risk (sulfured/natural SO2 branching; both-directions hard gate) is now covered by a spec that also self-cleans, instead of resurrecting two more no-teardown files.

**🔒 `effective-qty.spec.ts`'s first test — single-line provisional→gate-net auto-update, live across three screens (Ombor accept view, Menejer KIRIM list, Moyka send screen), no user action — dropped from automated coverage, NOT folded in, confirmed with the user rather than silently dropped.** None of the 4 survivors complete gate stage 2 on a single-line truck (`full-chain.spec.ts` deliberately uses a 2-line order to also cover `kirim-client-targets`/multi-line reconciliation variance; `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts` deliberately stays gate-stage-1-only throughout, matching the original `rewash-full-cycle` design). Adding a 5th spec purely to complete gate stage 2 on a single-line truck was one option offered; the user chose to drop it instead, on the basis that `weightAuthority.test.ts` (unit, kept in the 79) plus `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts`'s scenario E (gate_net_final, kept above) together cover the DERIVATION correctly — what's genuinely uncovered now is only the UI-WIRING (does a single-line truck's displayed qty actually flip from provisional to gate-net live, with no refetch, across all three screens that render it). **This is a real, accepted coverage gap, not a false one — recorded here so it isn't silently lost, and must be named as an explicit row in any future manual pre-release checklist:** *"Single-line KIRIM truck, complete gate stage 2 after intake is confirmed — confirm the displayed qty updates from the intake figure to the gate net, without a page reload, on: Ombor's own accept view, Menejer's KIRIM order list, and Moyka's send screen."* No such checklist document exists yet in this repo; this entry is that row's canonical home until one does.

**Self-cleaning teardown — the harder problem than the test-writing itself.** SPEC.md §2.15's "Never DELETE, only void" is enforced at the RLS level for operational data, confirmed via direct query: of the 11 tables in the full teardown chain (`dispatch_manifest`, `chiqim_lines`, `gate_weighings`, `chiqim_requests`, `finished_pallets`, `wash_cycles`, `moyka_sends`, `lab_results`, `storage_intake`, `kirim_lines`, `kirim_orders`), only `dispatch_manifest` has ANY delete policy at all (`ombor_deletes`, scoped to pre-gate-stage-2 status — the same policy `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` exists to verify). The other 10 have zero delete policies for any application role. A test runner therefore cannot clean up its own fixtures through the app's normal RLS-governed client at all.

**Resolved via a service-role key, confined deliberately narrowly, confirmed explicitly with the user before adding it.** `tests/e2e/helpers/teardown.ts` is a standalone Node-side `@supabase/supabase-js` client (bypasses RLS), reading `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` from `.env.test` (never committed — `.gitignore` already covered `.env.*`). Used ONLY there: never passed into `page.evaluate()` (would put it in the browser context), never imported under `src/`. Same precedent already accepted for the reporting-engine's own 96-row TEST- cleanup (`docs/DECISIONS.md` "Reporting engine cleanup") — elevated access confined to a one-off/tooling context, production RLS itself untouched. The alternative (adding real DELETE policies to production RLS to serve test cleanup) was rejected as the wrong tradeoff — it would weaken the deployed security model to serve tooling.

**Teardown is scoped strictly to each test's own generated identifiers (plates), not by TEST- prefix or time window** — `teardownFixtures({ kirimPlates, chiqimPlates })` looks up `kirim_orders`/`chiqim_requests` by exact plate match, walks the dependency chain (`dispatch_manifest`/`chiqim_lines` → `gate_weighings` → `chiqim_requests` → `finished_pallets`/`wash_cycles`/`moyka_sends`/`lab_results`/`storage_intake`/`kirim_lines` → `kirim_orders`) and runs in every spec's `test.afterEach`, so it fires even when the test itself fails partway through. `owners` was deliberately left OFF the chain — the immediately-prior Rahbar-settings task (§3.3) removed DELETE from `owners` entirely (insert/update-only, by design), and every survivor now references one existing real owner (`E2E_OWNER_NAME = 'Boysun Quritilgan Mevalar'`, picked specifically because no hand-computed reference elsewhere in the project depends on its numbers, unlike "Nukus Agro Eksport") rather than creating a throwaway one per test.

**"Test Client A/B/C" fixed as a byproduct, not the goal — every survivor's owner reference was broken by the clean-room reset independent of this task,** confirmed live before writing any test code. `fixtures.ts`'s `seedDispatchablePallets`/`seedFilteredFinishedRequest` and both new/kept specs' inline `page.evaluate()` owner lookups all now resolve `E2E_OWNER_NAME` instead of the deleted placeholder names.

**Three real bugs found on first execution, all in the new test code, not the app — fixed before the suite was considered verified:**
1. **`full-chain.spec.ts` was missing a role switch.** After the Laborator KIRIM lab-check block, the test jumped straight into clicking Ombor's "Moykaga Chiqarish" nav link while still logged in as Laborator — no such link exists for that role, so it hung for the full 150s timeout. Fixed by adding the missing logout+`loginAs(page, 'OMBOR')` before that block.
2. **`full-chain.spec.ts` assumed the wrong CHIQIM lab flow for a sulfured line.** `ChiqimTahlilForm`'s `requireVerdict` prop is `cycle.target_so2_mg_kg === null` — false for Subxon, which the test itself set up as sulfured. The test wrote the non-sulfured shortcut (Tahlil -> direct "O'tdi" click) instead of the real two-step sulfured flow (Tahlil -> "Saqlash" -> Sera kutilmoqda -> SO2 entry -> "O'tdi"), so it hung waiting for a verdict button that `ChiqimTahlilForm` never renders for a sulfured line. Fixed by mirroring the already-correct two-step Sera pattern used earlier in the same test for the KIRIM-side lab check.
3. **The teardown helper's own dependency order was wrong, and no delete call checked its error — together these let the bug run silently across three full green suite runs before being caught.** Queried pg's actual FK graph directly (`information_schema`, not assumption) and found `lab_results.wash_cycle_id` references `wash_cycles.id` — meaning `lab_results` must be deleted BEFORE `wash_cycles`, the opposite of the order this task's own prose description specified and `teardown.ts` originally implemented. Every `.delete()` call also omitted its `error` check, so the FK violation this caused was swallowed silently (Supabase returns `{ error }` on a blocked delete, it doesn't throw) — three consecutive full suite runs reported 4/4 green while quietly leaving `kirim_lines`/`kirim_orders` (and everything downstream of the failed `wash_cycles` delete) undeleted every time. Caught only by directly querying the live DB afterward and finding 7 orphaned `TEST-` `kirim_orders` rows the suite itself claimed to have cleaned up. Fixed both: corrected the delete order (`lab_results` now precedes `finished_pallets`/`wash_cycles`), and added a shared `del()` helper that throws with table+scope context on any error, so a future FK-order mistake fails the test loudly in its own `afterEach` instead of leaving debris to be found later. The 7 orphans from the broken runs were cleaned up manually (via the fixed `teardownFixtures()` itself, run once from a throwaway script, confirmed against the live DB) before the real verification below.

**Verification, run for real:** `tsc` sanity-check clean (throwaway `tsconfig.e2e-check.json`), 79 unit tests unchanged. `npx playwright test` run twice back-to-back with NO manual cleanup between runs, per the task's own requirement — run 1: 4/4 passed in 3.1 min; run 2: 4/4 passed in 3.1 min. Confirmed directly against the live DB after both runs: zero `TEST-`-prefixed or `driver='TEST Driver'` rows remain in any of the 11 teardown-chain tables or `owners`, and every operational table's row count matches the pre-session baseline exactly (`kirim_orders=14, kirim_lines=16, storage_intake=16, moyka_sends=16, wash_cycles=16, finished_pallets=34, lab_results=30, chiqim_requests=7, chiqim_lines=0, gate_weighings=21, dispatch_manifest=14, owners=6, calibres=4, product_types=5, product_categories=1, settings_limits=9, notes=0`). `audit_log` grew (35 -> 87) as expected — it's append-only, outside the teardown chain by design, and accumulates one row per state-changing action across every run this session performed, not fixture drift.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** app code, the `-2,200kg` race, UX work.

## 2026-07-22 — UX pass, prompt 1/2: design system + Ombor scan-load, camera scanning

**Context:** First of a two-part UX pass — establish a shared, reusable design system once, then apply it to one screen (Ombor's CHIQIM scan-load, `OmborChiqimTab.tsx`) as the reference implementation, plus wire in camera-based barcode scanning as the pass's one new feature. Every other screen stays untouched until prompt 2. Presentation and one new input path only — no schema, RLS, or `chiqimScan.ts`/data-flow change.

**Inspected the existing visual language across 6 screens before designing anything, rather than inventing a palette.** `OmborChiqimTab`, `OmborIntakeTab`, `QorovulKirimTab`/`QorovulChiqimTab`, `LaboratorKirimTab`/`LaboratorChiqimTab` all already share one unlabeled system: slate borders/text as the neutral base, amber for a pending/informational state (Sera kutilmoqda, gate-variance notes), red for a problem/urgent state (active-row highlight, error text), emerald for a passed/exact state, all via Tailwind's stock palette (confirmed as the app's own identity color too — the PWA manifest's `theme_color` is `#0f172a`, i.e. slate-900). Two inconsistencies found in passing (red-200 vs red-300 borders across two screens; amber-600 vs amber-700 text) — resolved by picking ONE canonical shade per case rather than propagating both, documented inline in `tokens.ts`.

**Design system built as a small `src/components/ui/` library plus one plain-TS token file, not a Tailwind `@theme` rewrite.** Considered formalizing status colors as new Tailwind v4 theme tokens (`@theme` in `index.css`, CSS-first config, no `tailwind.config.js` in this project) but rejected it: the existing usages need multiple shades per status (border/bg/text, light/dark) and a flat custom-color token can't cover that without a verbose per-shade theme block, which is more surface area and risk than a reference-implementation prompt calls for. Instead, `components/ui/tokens.ts` is the single source of truth (`Tone` type, `touch`/`typeScale`/`toneStyles` constants), and 7 small components (`Button`, `IconButton`, `Card`, `StatusNote`, `SectionHeading`, `Stat`, `FormField`/`TextInput`) read from it — every one of the 7 has at least 2-3 already-observed usages across the 6 screens read above, so nothing here is speculative for prompt 2's sake.

**Touch targets bumped from the existing app's ad hoc sizing, named once.** Existing buttons were `px-3 py-1.5` (~32px tall) and icon-only ✕/⋯ controls had no explicit hit area at all beyond their glyph — real friction for a phone used one-handed on a factory floor. `tokens.ts` names three tiers: `touch.primary` (56px, the one primary/confirm action in view), `touch.secondary` (48px, secondary controls and form inputs), `touch.icon` (44px, icon-only). `IconButton` is new specifically to guarantee the 44px floor under the existing ✕ controls without changing their `aria-label` text.

**Button hierarchy formalized as 5 variants, matching the app's own existing convention rather than inventing a new one.** `primary` = the existing dark-filled commit-button style (Ha, yakunlash / Sera kiritish); `secondary` = the existing outlined style; `ghost` = the existing text-only dismiss style (Bekor qilish); `danger`/`success` = the existing red-600/emerald-600 verdict-button colors (Qayta yuvish / O'tdi in the Laborator tabs) — included in `Button` even though scan-load itself doesn't use them, since they're real, already-observed patterns prompt 2 will need, not speculative additions.

**🔒 Every existing button/heading/placeholder string and every ARIA role in `OmborChiqimTab.tsx` is byte-for-byte unchanged — verified against the e2e suite's own contract before touching any JSX, not assumed safe.** `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts`, `full-chain.spec.ts`, and `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts` (this session's own just-verified e2e survivors, see "e2e suite consolidation" above) all drive this exact screen via `getByRole`/`getByPlaceholder`/`getByText` lookups on: the "Yuklash uchun so'rovlar"/"Yuklandi" headings, the collapsed row rendered as a `<button>` containing the plate text, the `"Barcode #2 ni kiriting yoki skanerlang"` placeholder, the `"Skanerlash"`/`"Yuklashni yakunlash"`/`"Ha, yakunlash"` button text, the `"✓ Aniq mos keldi"` per-line text, manifest rows as `<li>` elements, and the `"Skanerlashni bekor qilish"` aria-label on both the pre-finish and post-finish undo controls. All of these are reproduced exactly; only their layout, styling, and (for the scan input) the addition of a camera source changed. Re-ran the full e2e suite after the rework to confirm — see Verification below.

**Ergonomics-first reorder of the expanded scan-load card, the pass's own explicit requirement ("ergonomics lead, visual follows").** Original order was: per-line target list (with progress bars) → scan input → confirm/finish, buried at the bottom past a list that grows with every scan. Reordered to: **(1)** a new big glanceable running-total banner ("Stat") — read at a glance, no scrolling, aggregated from the SAME per-line `lineStatus()` every line card already used (neutral while any line is short, amber if any line is over, emerald only once every line is exact — composed in the component, not a new decision in `chiqimScan.ts`); **(2)** the scan zone (camera button, then manual input as fallback) — the repeated action, 10-20x per truck; **(3)** the Finish button — the one-time action, kept immediately below the scan zone so it's thumb-reachable without scrolling past a growing scanned-pallet list; **(4)** the per-line breakdown — verification detail, checked occasionally rather than every scan, now appropriately last.

**Camera scanning (`BarcodeCameraScanner.tsx`, new): `html5-qrcode`'s `Html5Qrcode` class, restricted to CODE_128 (the one format `barcodeLabel.ts`/`Barcode2Display.tsx` ever generates), calling the exact same scan-resolution path as manual entry.** `handleScan`'s original body was split into `processBarcode(request, barcode2): Promise<boolean>` (all the Supabase lookups + `resolveScan` call + state update, unchanged) and a thin wrapper that only the manual `<form>` needs (trims input, clears it on success only — same as before). The camera's `onDecode` calls `processBarcode` directly — a camera read is byte-for-byte the same code path as typing the same string, including a voided pallet (`status !== 'in_stock'`) failing with the exact same existing message ("Bu pallet omborda emas...") with no new logic. Continuous-scan mode (`Html5Qrcode.start()` keeps firing on every frame with a code in view) is debounced in the component only (same code within 1.5s ignored) to avoid hammering Supabase with repeat lookups of a barcode still in frame — `resolveScan`'s own `duplicate` check is the real guard once a scan actually lands.

**Camera lifecycle hardened for React 19 StrictMode's mount→cleanup→mount dev cycle**, using `Html5Qrcode`'s own public `isScanning` flag rather than a separate tracked ref: a `cancelled` flag set in the effect cleanup, checked both before starting playback and inside `start()`'s resolution, so a StrictMode double-invoke either stops a camera that only just started or never starts a second one. Camera permission/hardware failures (`start()`'s rejection) are caught and shown as a plain-language Uzbek message directing the operator to manual entry or a hardware scanner — never a blocking error, matching every other error-handling convention already in this app.

**API verified directly against the installed package's own `.d.ts` files before writing any code**, not assumed from memory of the library: confirmed `Html5Qrcode`'s constructor/`start`/`stop`/`clear`/`isScanning` shape and that `CODE_128` is a valid `Html5QrcodeSupportedFormats` value via `node_modules/html5-qrcode/esm/*.d.ts` directly.

**New dependency:** `html5-qrcode@2.3.8` (browser `getUserMedia`, no Capacitor — confirmed no native wrapper exists in this project's dependencies). `npm audit` after install shows 3 vulnerabilities, all pre-existing transitive deps (`exceljs`/`fast-uri`/`uuid`), none introduced by this addition.

**🚩 One real bug found and fixed by actually re-running the e2e suite, not by assuming the "unchanged strings" claim above was sufficient.** The first version of the camera toggle button read "📷 Kamera bilan skanerlash" — a label chosen for clarity, not realizing it made `Skanerlash` (the manual submit button's own exact accessible name) a literal substring of the camera button's name too. Playwright's `getByRole('button', { name: 'Skanerlash' })` matches by substring by default, so all three chain specs (`chiqim-undo-scan`, `full-chain`, `rewash-hard-gate` — every survivor that actually scans a barcode) failed identically with a strict-mode "resolved to 2 elements" error the moment they tried to click Skanerlash. Caught only because the full suite was re-run after the rework instead of trusting the "every existing string is unchanged" claim to also cover strings that were NEW; the new string is what broke an old one. Fixed by renaming the camera button to "📷 Kamerani yoqish" ("turn the camera on," paired with the existing "Kamerani yopish" close button) — no collision with any other accessible name on the screen. Re-ran the full suite again afterward: 4/4 pass.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` both clean on the new/changed files. Seeded a small isolated fixture (`TEST-SCANUX-*` plates, an existing real owner, 2 in-stock lab-passed pallets + 1 deliberately voided pallet, one CHIQIM request) via a throwaway service-role script (same pattern as the e2e teardown helper), then drove the live dev server at mobile viewport (375×812) as the Ombor test login: expanded the request and confirmed the new layout order renders exactly as designed (Stat banner → camera button → manual input → Finish → per-line detail); a manual scan of a real barcode updated the running total and per-line detail correctly (0/4,000 → 2,000/4,000 kg); a scan of the voided barcode was rejected with the existing, unchanged message, running total unaffected; opening the camera panel triggered a real `getUserMedia` request (confirmed by the browser tooling itself) which — blocked in this sandboxed session, as expected with no camera hardware available — exercised the failure path exactly as designed, showing the Uzbek fallback message with manual entry still fully usable alongside it; the Finish flow completed the request end to end (moved from "Yuklash uchun so'rovlar" to "Yuklandi" with a real timestamp), and the W2 undo-scan list rendered correctly. **Not verified: an actual successful camera decode**, since no real camera is reachable from this sandboxed browser session — the decode path itself (`onDecode` → `processBarcode`) is exactly the manually-verified path, and the camera wiring around it (start/stop/debounce/error-handling) was exercised via the failure path above; this should be spot-checked once on a real phone before wider rollout. Ran the full Playwright e2e suite twice after the rework (once surfacing the button-label bug above, once clean after the fix) — not the full twice-back-to-back-with-no-cleanup protocol from the prior task, since no fixture/teardown logic changed here, just confirming the UI contract held: all 4 survivors pass. `npm test` 79/79 unchanged (no logic file touched). Fixture teardown confirmed: zero `TEST-SCANUX` rows remain in any table afterward.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** every other screen (prompt 2), the print button (Capacitor phase), Russian on staff screens, any logic/trigger/schema change, the reporting screens.

## 2026-07-22 — Qorovul photo upload silent failure: diagnosis, real error, real fix

**Symptom:** on the deployed Netlify HTTPS URL, on a phone, tapping any gate photo upload (plate/scale/document) opened the picker fine, but after selecting and confirming an image, the form reset with nothing attached — no error, no upload. Reported for Qorovul's gate screen specifically; all three photo fields there failed identically.

**Diagnosis (inspection only, no fix yet):** read the `photos` storage buckets, RLS, and every photo-upload code path. Findings, in order:
1. **Not RLS.** `gate_photos_insert`'s policy (`bucket_id = 'gate-photos' AND my_role() = 'qorovul'`) is correct and demonstrably working — this session's own e2e runs (real qorovul-role uploads) had landed objects in that bucket the same day.
2. **The real bug: `PhotoField.tsx`'s `handleFile` wrapped `compressImage()` in `try { } finally { }` with no `catch`.** Any exception during client-side compression vanished silently — `onChange` never fired, the field looked idle again, nothing was ever attached, no error shown. This happens at file-*selection* time, before any network request to Supabase Storage is even made — confirming the failure is client-side compression, not Storage/RLS/HTTPS.
3. **Not app-wide "never worked," but a real gap in what was ever verified.** `gate-photos` (952 objects), `intake-photos` (357), `lab-photos` (24) all had successful uploads — but the median/mode object size in all three was exactly 759 bytes, the compressed size of the e2e suite's own tiny fixed `test-photo.png` fixture. Every prior verification of these forms (this session's e2e suite included) used that same tiny fixture, never a real phone photo — the shared `PhotoField` bug (also used by Ombor's intake photo and both Laborator sample-photo forms) was exposed everywhere, just never tripped by anything a test or a desk-based check would generate.
4. **A structurally different but related bug in `KirimForm.tsx` (Menejer), found while checking "is this Qorovul-only."** It doesn't use the `PhotoField` component, but has its own independent copy of the same missing-catch call. Its consequence is different: `setPhotoFile(file)` sets the RAW file *before* compression is attempted, so a compression failure there silently uploads the uncompressed original instead of losing the photo — consistent with `kirim-photos`' one and only object being an uncompressed 1.7MB file. Confirmed via `git log --follow` that none of this (`PhotoField.tsx`, `GateStageForm.tsx`, `imageCompress.ts`, `QorovulKirimTab.tsx`/`QorovulChiqimTab.tsx`) was touched by the recent UX pass — pre-existing, original code from Phase 1.

**Interim step: a temporary diagnostic build, explicitly marked and later reverted.** Remote USB debugging (Safari Web Inspector / chrome://inspect) couldn't connect to the affected device, so as a throwaway measure the friendly error was swapped for the raw `err.name + ': ' + err.message` on-screen in both `PhotoField.tsx` and `KirimForm.tsx`, deployed via its own PR (`temp-fix/photo-upload-diagnostic`, merged as #39), read on-device, then reverted in this same task. Direct pushes to `main` are blocked by a repo rule requiring a PR in both directions of this arc — every commit here went through a branch + PR, never a direct push.

**🔒 The real error, read directly off the device: `InvalidStateError: the source image could not be decoded`** — `createImageBitmap` rejecting a real-phone photo outright, confirming the hypothesis (some real-device photo formats/encodings the bitmap decoder rejects) rather than guessing at a fix from the wrong cause.

**The real fix, `imageCompress.ts`:** `createImageBitmap` and an `<img>` element both implement `CanvasImageSource` and can both feed `ctx.drawImage()` identically — so the fix tries `createImageBitmap` first (unchanged for the common case) and falls back to decoding via a fresh `<img>` + `URL.createObjectURL` + `img.decode()` only if that throws. `img.decode()` goes through the browser's ordinary image pipeline rather than `createImageBitmap`'s own decoder, and resolves only once the image is genuinely decoded and safe to draw (not just fetched) — the same guarantee `onload` gives, but as a promise. Whichever path succeeds hands the same `{width, height, source}` shape to the unchanged canvas/resize/JPEG-encode logic, so the compression target (~300KB, 1600px longest edge, JPEG q=0.7) is untouched. If both paths fail, the exception still propagates to `PhotoField`/`KirimForm`'s catch, which still shows the friendly message — this fix reduces how often that catch fires, it doesn't remove the need for it.

**Verified the fallback path actually produces a usable canvas before considering it done — not assumed.** Live in the browser: (1) normal path unchanged — a synthetic 2000×1500 test image compressed identically whether or not the fallback was involved; (2) forced `window.createImageBitmap` to reject with the exact real-device error, confirmed the `<img>`-path fallback still produced a valid compressed JPEG (1600×1200, correctly scaled), and round-tripped that output blob back through the real `createImageBitmap` to confirm it's a genuinely well-formed image, not just a non-empty blob; (3) a truly corrupt file (fails both paths) still rejected cleanly with a real error rather than hanging, confirming the double-failure case still reaches the existing catch.

**Also, camera-first capture:** added `capture="environment"` to `PhotoField.tsx`'s input (covers all 4 consumers: Qorovul's `GateStageForm`, Ombor's `IntakeAcceptForm`, both Laborator Tahlil forms) and to `KirimForm.tsx`'s own input — opens the rear camera directly on a phone instead of the gallery picker, `accept="image/*"` kept so gallery stays available wherever the OS still offers it alongside capture.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean. Full e2e suite run twice (one run invalidated by an unrelated tool mistake — the dev server was stopped mid-run — the clean re-run passed 4/4), confirming the ordinary (non-fallback) compression path used by Qorovul's gate photos and Ombor's intake photo is unaffected. `npm test` 79/79 unchanged. **What's not verified, and can't be from here: the fallback path against the actual real-device photo that triggered this.** The fallback's mechanics are confirmed sound (above), and the exact error that was failing is now the one path this fix specifically targets, but final proof is a real-phone retest after this deploys.

**🔒 Camera-first capture reversed the same day — made real-world selection worse, not better.** `capture="environment"` forced the rear camera open directly instead of letting the OS offer its normal picker; on the real device this added friction and reportedly returned to the screen with nothing selected, the opposite of the intended fix. Removed from both inputs, `accept="image/*"` kept so the OS's normal gallery/camera choice is what opens — restoring the exact picker behavior that was already uploading successfully before any of this arc's changes. The decode fallback and the friendly-message catch (both above) are unaffected and stay; only the forced-camera attribute was wrong.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** the storage layer (RLS already confirmed correct), the barcode scanner, Capacitor, any other screen's logic.

## 2026-07-22 — UX pass, prompt 2/2: design system rollout across all remaining screens

**Context:** Second of the two-part UX pass — apply the fixed `components/ui/` system (built in prompt 1, reference implementation `OmborChiqimTab.tsx`) across every remaining screen. Presentation only, no logic/schema/RLS/data-flow change; ergonomics-first for the floor screens, visual-coherence-only for the desktop screens, per the task's own priority order.

**Group 1 — Qorovul gate (`QorovulKirimTab.tsx`, `QorovulChiqimTab.tsx`, `GateStageForm.tsx`).** Three-tile counters -> `Stat` (canonicalizes the red-200→300 shade prompt 1 already resolved). Active/completed rows -> `Card` (tone="problem" for the in-progress row, matching the same canonical red-300). Row-trigger and stage-submit buttons -> `Button` (primary/lg for submit, ghost/md for cancel, secondary/md for the row trigger). Weight input -> `FormField`+`TextInput`. Completed-row net_kg split onto its own bold line, separate from the timestamp, for glanceability. `SectionHeading` for Faol/Yakunlangan.

**Group 2 — Laborator (`LaboratorKirimTab.tsx`, `LaboratorChiqimTab.tsx`, `KirimTahlilForm.tsx`, `ChiqimTahlilForm.tsx`).** Same Card/Button/FormField/StatusNote/SectionHeading treatment. `SectionHeading tone="pending"` for "Sera kutilmoqda" — the exact case that prop was built for. O'tdi/Qayta yuvish verdict buttons -> `Button` variant success/danger (Button.tsx's own canonical example). **One field kept its original hand-built shape on purpose:** `ChiqimTahlilForm`'s "Namligi %" label carries a nested `<span>` client-target suffix ("Namligi % (Talab: X%)"); the e2e suite's `label:text-is("Namligi %")` locator depends on that exact structure, and `FormField`'s `label` prop only accepts a plain string, so this one field kept its raw `<label>`+`<span>` and only swapped the input for `TextInput` — same resolution pattern as prompt 1's own case-by-case verification, not a new one-off invented.

**Group 3 — Ombor intake (`OmborIntakeTab.tsx`, `IntakeAcceptForm.tsx`).** Nested `Card`s (outer per-order group, inner per-line row) — confirmed as an already-established reference pattern (`OmborChiqimTab`'s own request-row/per-line-breakdown nesting), not a new shape. `IconButton` for the "Batafsil" expand control. `IntakeAcceptForm`'s "Aniq (kg)" field kept its raw `<label htmlFor>`/`<input id>` pairing (only swapped to `TextInput`) since `FormField` has no `htmlFor` support and this field's accessibility linkage predates this pass. `IntakeAcceptForm.tsx` showed as modified in git before this task started; confirmed via `git diff` it was a line-ending-only artifact (empty diff against HEAD), not real prior work — safe to build on directly.

**Group 4 — Menejer (`KirimForm.tsx`, `ChiqimForm.tsx`, `KirimOrdersList.tsx`, `FinishedChiqimList.tsx`).** Lighter interaction changes (desktop, order-creation focus), same component set. Feasibility-hint text (`ChiqimForm`) -> `StatusNote tone="pending"`, unchanged hint strings/logic. `FinishedChiqimList`'s Menejer/Ombor/Qorovul actor-detail block, including every `GatePhoto` call and its exact alt-label strings ("Moshina raqami rasmi", "Tarozi rasmi (kirish/chiqish)", "Chiqish hujjati rasmi", "Qorovul — Yuk bilan vazn (chiqish)"), left byte-for-byte unchanged — confirmed these are e2e-asserted via `getByAltText`/`getByText` before touching anything nearby.

**🔒 Two real locator regressions found via e2e, not assumed safe from inspection alone — both fixed.** (1) `KirimForm`/`ChiqimForm`'s "Haydovchi ismi" field: wrapped in `FormField`, whose own `div.mt-1` around `children` put the input one level deeper than the e2e suite's `div:has(> label:text-is("Haydovchi ismi")) > input` (a direct-child combinator) expects — caught only because "Moshina raqami" (the same shape, already known to need this) was fixed first but this sibling field wasn't checked against the same pattern. Fixed the same way: raw `<label>` + `TextInput` as direct siblings, no `FormField` wrapper. (2) `KirimForm`'s repeatable type/qty row: replaced with `Card`, whose own class list doesn't include `space-y-1` — dropped a class the e2e suite's `form div.space-y-1.rounded-md` locator (used to find "row N" in `full-chain.spec.ts`/`rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts`) depends on. Fixed by passing `className="space-y-1"` through to `Card`. After both fixes, ran a full audit of every class-based and `:has()`/`:text-is()` structural locator across all four e2e spec files against every file this pass touched (not just the two that broke) — every remaining one either targets a screen this pass never touched (`OmborTayyorTab.tsx`, `OmborMoykaTab.tsx` — neither in any of the 5 groups) or was individually confirmed to still match.

**Group 5 — Rahbar + reporting, deliberately minimal.** Read all of `RahbarHome.tsx`, `RahbarSettingsTab.tsx`, `RahbarExceptionsTab.tsx`, `HisobotTab.tsx`, `StockOnHandTab.tsx`/`StockOnHandHeader.tsx`/`StockOnHandTable.tsx`, `WipTab.tsx`/`WipTable.tsx`, `YieldTab.tsx`/`YieldTable.tsx`, `ClientReportTab.tsx`, `SerialPassportModal.tsx`, `ReportResultsTable.tsx`/`ReportTableRow.tsx`, `KirimRowDetail.tsx`/`ChiqimRowDetail.tsx` before touching anything. Found this whole family already has its own complete, internally consistent, more-recently-built visual language (`th`/`td`/`label`/`sectionTitle` constants, sticky summary strips, a uniform aria-expanded/▲▼ row-toggle convention, uniform drill-down links) — genuinely matching the task's own framing ("already more recently designed"), not the ad hoc pre-prompt-1 state the floor screens were in. Most of it is `<table>`-based, where `Card`/`Button`'s div-based rendering doesn't apply without breaking table semantics. Made one change: `RahbarExceptionsTab.tsx`'s bare "→" drill-down button (previously no `aria-label`, just the glyph as its own accessible name) -> `IconButton label="Pasportni ochish"` — a real, zero-structural-risk a11y win, confirmed no e2e test targets that button. Left every other Group 5 file unchanged rather than force a div/card system onto working, recently-designed table rows.

**🚩 Flagging instead of guessing: the print-button requirement.** The task's guardrail says to place an unwired print button "on finished-pallet / sticker-relevant screens." Nothing in this pass's actual assigned file list is that screen — `SerialPassportModal.tsx` (the one passport/certificate view in scope) is a dense multi-section audit trail, not a sticker; the real sticker-rendering components (`Barcode1Display.tsx`, `Barcode2Display.tsx`) and the finished-pallet list (`OmborTayyorTab.tsx`) were never in any of the 5 groups' file lists for this prompt. Rather than guess which one was meant and invent a placement, this is left undone and flagged here.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean across every changed file. `npm test` 79/79 unchanged (no logic file touched). Full Playwright e2e suite run three times over the course of this pass: run 1 (after Groups 1-3) passed 4/4 clean; run 2 (after Groups 4-5) surfaced the two locator regressions above and one unrelated transient flake (`report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts` failed on a raw FK-violation inside its own `page.evaluate` seeding helper, nothing to do with any UI change — confirmed no orphaned rows were left behind, and it passed clean on the very next run); run 3, after both fixes, passed 4/4 clean including `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts` (its previously-flagged fragile 0kg assertion happened not to trigger this run — not something this task fixed, still the same pre-existing, separately-flagged issue). Live-browser spot-check (mobile viewport, real logged-in Qorovul/Laborator/Ombor test accounts) confirmed: `Stat`/`Card`/`Button`/`FormField`/`StatusNote` all render with real computed styles (confirmed 56px/48px touch heights via `getComputedStyle`, not just class-name presence), `ChiqimTahlilForm`'s composite "Namligi %" label renders with the nested span intact, and GateStageForm's stage-2 flow opens/renders correctly end to end.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** camera scanning beyond scan-load (done in prompt 1), the print button wiring (Capacitor phase — and see the flag above on placement itself), Russian on staff screens, the stale `rewash-hard-gate` 0kg assertion (still separately flagged), any logic/schema/RLS change anywhere.

## 2026-07-22 — Menejer visual redesign + nav restructure (mockup "BATU-Manager-Screens-MASTER.pdf")

**Context:** Match Menejer's screens to a supplied 8-page mockup — new responsive nav shell (mobile drawer / desktop sidebar, replacing the shared top-tab bar) plus card/pill visual language on KIRIM, CHIQIM, and Hisobot. Presentation and navigation only; confirmed decision going in was to keep every current logic/query/data-flow path exactly as built.

**🔒 The mockup's "Kuzatuv" (pages 6-8, 3-lens desktop traceability screen) is the pre-consolidation design — already superseded in this app's own spec, not something to build.** `docs/SPEC-reporting-v1.10-revision.md`'s own heading: *"Supersedes §3.2 (Tarix), §3.4 (Kuzatuv), §3.5 (Mijoz hisoboti) — replaced by a single §3.2... A lookup is a filter, not a screen."* Confirmed this isn't just a naming difference: the mockup's "Seriya bo'yicha"/"Mashina bo'yicha" lenses need data no current hook produces (`yield_rows` is completion-date-scoped with no CHIQGAN/OMBORDA columns; no per-truck-trip hook exists at all) — building it as drawn would mean new aggregation logic, directly against this task's own confirmed decision. Treated pages 6-8 as visual-language reference only (dense table, mono serial chips, colored status pills, bordered totals box, "→" drill-down) and applied that language to the screens that actually exist: Hisobot, Ombor qoldig'i, Kutilayotgan ishlar, Hosildorlik, Mijoz hisoboti, the passport modal.

**Nav shell: `AppNavShell.tsx` (new, `src/components/`), Menejer-only this prompt.** One responsive component, not a mobile/desktop pair — a persistent `<aside>` sidebar (`hidden lg:flex`) and a drawer whose contents are conditionally rendered on `open` (not just CSS-hidden), so at any given viewport only one copy of the nav links is ever actually in the DOM — confirmed live via `getComputedStyle`/`offsetParent` at 375px (sidebar: `display:none`, truly absent) and via a real interactive-mode accessibility read at 1280px (only one "KIRIM"/"CHIQIM" link each, no duplicates for `getByRole('link', ...)` to trip on — Playwright's own default viewport is 1280×720, confirmed no e2e spec ever calls `setViewportSize`, so this is the nav path e2e always exercises). Built from existing primitives (`IconButton` for the hamburger/close, `touch.secondary` for nav-item sizing, `Button` for the logout) rather than hand-rolled parallel classes. `RoleShell`/`RoleTabs` (every other role) untouched.

**New token: `Tone` gains `info` (blue).** The mockup threads one consistent highlight color through form section titles, the auto-summed totals box, the auto-generated-serial note, and drill-down links — none of the 4 existing tones (all status states) cover "informational highlight." Added as a proper `toneStyles.info` entry (text/border/bg triplet, same shape as the rest) rather than ad hoc blue classes per usage; `SectionHeading` widened from `'neutral'|'pending'` to the full `Tone` type to accept it (its neutral-tone output is byte-identical to the old hardcoded default, so every prompt-1/2 usage renders unchanged). Two new shared components: `StatusPill` (filled rounded badge — Kutilmoqda/Qabul qilindi/Olib ketildi) and `SerialChip` (mono chip for a serial or the literal "So'rov" placeholder) — both card-list furniture the mockup repeats on every list screen, neither existed in the prompt-1 system.

**🔒 Real bug caught by `getComputedStyle`, not just visual inspection: a `className` override that silently lost the CSS cascade.** The dashed-border "+ Tur qo'shish"/"+ Tur/kalibr qo'shish" buttons pass `text-blue-700` via `Button`'s `className` prop to override its `ghost` variant's baked-in `text-slate-500` — but Tailwind's generated stylesheet order decides which utility wins on a tie, not the order classes appear in the `class=""` attribute, so the override was silently losing every time (confirmed: computed color came back slate, not blue). Fixed with the `!` important-modifier (`!text-blue-700` etc.) on just the overridden utilities. Worth remembering for any future `className`-override of a `Button`/`Card` variant's own color classes — attribute order does not imply cascade order.

**KIRIM/CHIQIM tabs (`KirimOrdersList.tsx`, `FinishedChiqimList.tsx`) — card list with `SerialChip` + headline/meta + `StatusPill`.** `kirim_orders.status` confirmed against the live DB as exactly two values (`kutilmoqda`/`qabul_qilindi`) — a plain label+tone map, no new status. Collapsed-card headline kept to `{plate} · {driver}` (already-fetched fields) rather than the mockup's `{owner} · {type}` — adding owner/type would mean adding `owner_id` to `KirimOrdersList`'s `.select()`, a query change the hard guardrail rules out, so this is a deliberate, flagged divergence from the mockup's exact headline content, not an oversight.

**🔒 Second flagged divergence: Menejer's CHIQIM tab still shows only finished requests, not the mockup's combined Kutilmoqda+Olib-ketildi list.** The existing code comment is explicit and predates this task: *"'Requests ready to load' (an open-requests window) belongs to Ombor's §5.4 screen, not this one."* Building a live "my still-open CHIQIM requests" list for Menejer would mean a new query path that doesn't exist today — same category of change as the Kuzatuv finding, so left alone and flagged rather than quietly added.

**KirimForm/ChiqimForm.** Section title tone → `info` (text unchanged: `getByRole('heading', {name:'Yangi KIRIM'/'Yangi CHIQIM'})` is e2e-load-bearing in three specs, confirmed before touching it — only the color changed). Add-row button moved below the rows, dashed-border `info`-toned per the mockup (confirmed via a full-suite grep that neither button's text is e2e-clicked before renaming CHIQIM's to "+ Tur/kalibr qo'shish" for clarity — KIRIM's own "+ Tur qo'shish" stays, it's the one full-chain.spec.ts clicks). "Jami avto" → `Card tone="info"` with a row count added (pure client-side `rows.filter(...).length`, no new query). Added a "Seriya raqami" info box matching the mockup's intent (serial is automatic) without fabricating the mockup's literal example number — the real serial only exists once `next_serial()` runs server-side on insert, so this shows "Saqlagandan keyin avtomatik beriladi" instead, with the real value still surfacing in the existing post-submit panel. Photo section restyled to a dashed drop-zone box; the underlying `<input type=file>`, `accept`, and `handlePhotoChange` are byte-for-byte untouched. Submit button text stays "Saqlash" (not the mockup's "Saqlash va yuborish") — e2e clicks it by that exact name in both forms.

**Hisobot restyled to the mockup's card list, with a real responsive rendering — not a mobile-only rewrite.** `TotalsStrip` and `StockOnHandHeader`'s sticky strips restyled to the bordered "Filtrlangan jami" `info` box (same numbers, same props). `ReportFilterBar` restyled to the mockup's segmented Hammasi/Kirim/Chiqim toggle + pill selects + date-preset shortcuts (Bugun/7 kun/Bu oy, pure client-side date math calling the exact same `onChange('from'/'to', ...)` the date inputs already did) with the less-common fields (kalibr, barcode2, plate, driver, wash cycle, lab verdict) still fully present behind a "Ko'proq filtrlar" toggle — every field from the original `ReportFilters` contract still reachable, none removed. `ReportResultsTable` now renders two ways from the same `rows`/callbacks — the existing desktop `<table>` (`hidden lg:block`) and a new `ReportRowCard` list (`lg:hidden`, matching the mockup's mobile cards) reusing the exact same `KirimRowDetail`/`ChiqimRowDetail` expand content — confirmed live that only one rendering is ever actually visible/in-DOM per viewport (table: `display:none` at 375px; card list: 10 cards rendered, expand-to-detail verified working end to end). This reverses none of the earlier documented "desktop rework" decision — the table stays the primary desktop rendering, phone-width now gets an actual answer instead of a horizontal scroll of the same dense table.

**Consistency pass on the screens not shown in the mockup (StockOnHandTab, YieldTab, ClientReportTab) — light touch, per the task's own trailing instruction.** Sticky summary strips → the same bordered `info` box as TotalsStrip. Filter rows (owner/type/date) → the same pill styling as Hisobot's. Export buttons → `Button variant="success"` (matches the mockup's solid-green "⬇ Excel" button exactly, an existing variant, no new one needed). `WipTab` has no filter bar of its own to restyle (by original design — thresholds are configured in Administration). Did not build full responsive card views for `StockOnHandTable`/`WipTable`/`YieldTable` — that was a large, mockup-unshown addition beyond this pass's core mandate; flagged here as a reasonable scope boundary rather than done silently.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean across every changed/new file. `npm test` 79/79 unchanged. Full Playwright e2e suite run once (per the task's reduced-testing plan): 4/4 clean on the first run — every locator risk (the two `space-y-1`/direct-child lessons from the prior UX pass, plus every new nav/card structure this pass introduces) was checked against a full grep of every class-based, `:has()`, and `:text-is()` selector across all four spec files before finalizing, not discovered by re-running. Live-browser spot-check at both viewport sizes (desktop sidebar, mobile drawer + card views) confirmed real computed styles (`display:none` sidebar at mobile, 48px nav-item/button heights, blue `info`-tone colors after the important-modifier fix) and working interaction (drawer open/close, card expand-to-detail, filter pills).

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** all other roles' nav (later prompts), printer wiring, Russian on staff screens, any logic/RLS/schema/query change, restructuring the reporting engine, the Kuzatuv 3-lens screen (see flag above), Menejer's own pending-CHIQIM list (see flag above).

## 2026-07-23 — Rahbar visual redesign + nav migration (inherits the Menejer pass)

**Context:** Migrate Rahbar to the shared `AppNavShell` and visual language the Menejer prompt built, then give the dashboard/exceptions/settings screens real care rather than a mechanical restyle. Presentation and navigation only, same confirmed-architecture-stays constraint as the Menejer prompt.

**Nav shell reused as-is, not forked.** `RahbarLayout.tsx` dropped `RoleShell` + its inline horizontal `<nav>` for `AppNavShell`, same 9 destinations (`to`/`label`/`end` unchanged) as one `NavItem[]`. Confirmed before touching anything that no e2e spec navigates to any `/rahbar` route or exercises the dashboard/exceptions/settings screens directly (grepped all 4 specs) — the only Rahbar-adjacent coverage is the reporting views Menejer and Rahbar share, already e2e-verified in the Menejer pass.

**Found a second mockup not named in the task text: `BATU-Rahbar-Screens-v1_1.pdf`, sitting alongside the Manager one.** Read it since it's obviously on-topic for the dashboard/exceptions/settings screens. It disagrees with the live app in three places — each resolved by reading this codebase's own spec/decisions rather than guessed:
1. **Its dashboard shows a live "HOZIR FABRIKADA" now-inventory strip (Xom skladda/Moykada/Tayyor by client).** `SPEC.md` §6.1 still lists this, but this repo's own 2026-07-21 dashboard-build entry explicitly scoped `RahbarHome.tsx` to "monthly trends + period-scoped client ranking + product mix" only, and this task's own dashboard bullet list (trends/ranking/mix/lab-turnaround/capacity) matches that exact built scope, omitting live inventory too. Never built for this screen; not added now — it would mean a brand-new query into a screen that has none today.
2. **Its exceptions list shows 6-7 problem kinds** (adding "Kam chiqdi" shortfall detection and "Nishonga to'g'ri kelmadi" manifest-mismatch detection to the four that exist). `SPEC.md` §6.2 still lists all 6, but `rahbarDashboard.ts`'s `ExceptionKind` union has exactly 4, and this task's own text says "four kinds in one list" — matching the code, not the mockup or the older spec text. Restyled the 4 that exist; did not add shortfall/manifest-mismatch detection.
3. **Its "Boshqaruv" page merges Foydalanuvchilar + Mijozlar + Ostonalar + Mahsulot into one page.** `SPEC.md` §6.4 explicitly says Sozlamalar is "mounted **alongside** the existing Foydalanuvchilar screen... no new layout" — two screens by design. Kept `/rahbar/sozlamalar` and `/rahbar/foydalanuvchilar` as two separate nav items/routes, restyled in place, no merge.

All three read the same way the Menejer pass's Kuzatuv finding did: a mockup drawn against an earlier design intent, superseded or narrowed by the time the screen was actually built — visual-language reference only, not a spec to implement now.

**Dashboard (`RahbarHome.tsx`).** Inline stat strip → `Stat` tiles: lab-turnaround (unchanged data), capacity (unchanged "hides entirely when unset" logic, now a tile instead of a hidden inline span), and one new derived tile — current month's loss % against the prior month, with a `▲`/`▼` sublabel — computed entirely from `trends`, already fetched, no new query. `Stat` gained an optional `sublabel` prop for this (defaults to nothing, so `QorovulKirimTab`/`QorovulChiqimTab`'s existing usages render unchanged). Trends table's loss%/rewash% cells changed from plain numbers to `StatusPill`, toned by comparing each row's own value against the existing `abnormal_loss_pct`/`high_rewash_rate_pct` thresholds (already fetched via `useSettingsLimits` for §6.2) — a presentational reuse of numbers already on the page, not a new rule. Verified live against real seeded data: 2026-07's 26.9% loss (above the 22% threshold) renders red, 2026-09's 50% rewash rate (above 20%) renders red, everything else renders green, the no-activity month renders a plain dash with no pill. Section headings swapped to the shared `SectionHeading` component (neutral tone, matching the "list/browse" convention `KirimOrdersList`/`FinishedChiqimList` already established — `info` tone stays reserved for form/action headings per the Menejer pass, not applied here). Desktop-first per the task's own instruction — no responsive card rework for this table.

**Exceptions (`RahbarExceptionsTab.tsx`) — the real problem here was that all 4 kinds got the identical hardcoded red pill, so nothing actually read as triage.** Added: kind-filter pills ("Hammasi (N)" + one per kind actually present, with live counts) and a serial/owner search box, both pure client-side filters over the `rows` this screen already fetches in full — no new query. Replaced the one hardcoded red pill with a per-kind `StatusPill` tone (`high_loss`→problem, `lab_overdue`/`ageing_stock`→pending, `high_rewash`→info, reasoned by how acute/time-sensitive each kind is). Passport drill-down changed from a bare `IconButton` arrow to a visible "Pasport →" text link, matching the exact link style (`text-slate-700 underline hover:text-slate-900...`) already established across `KirimRowDetail`/`ChiqimRowDetail`/`YieldTable`/`WipTable`/`StockOnHandTable` — not the mockup's blue, since the in-app convention for this exact link is more authoritative than a mockup's generic clickable-blue rendering. Verified live: filter pills narrow the table and compose correctly with the search box, per-kind tones render as designed (amber/red/blue).

**Settings (`RahbarSettingsTab.tsx`'s five sections + `UsersAdminPage.tsx`) — plain forms, deactivate made obvious rather than blended with "edit."** Every section's hand-rolled Faol/Nofaol span → `StatusPill`; every plain underlined text-link action (Tahrirlash/Saqlash/Bekor qilish/Faolsizlantirish/Faollashtirish/Qo'shish) → a real `Button` (`secondary` for edit/deactivate, `ghost` for cancel per `Button.tsx`'s own documented convention, `primary` for the add-form's submit) — a real button, not a link indistinguishable from "edit," is what makes "deactivate, not delete" actually read as its own action. Add-forms → `FormField`/`TextInput`. `ThresholdsSection`'s per-row wrapper (already `rounded-md border p-3`) swapped for the `Card` component outright — identical output, one less bespoke class string. `ClientsSection` is shared with Menejer's own Mijozlar screen (`allowDeactivate` prop), so this restyle reaches both; confirmed via grep neither screen has e2e coverage. `UsersAdminPage`'s bespoke `Field` helper removed (no longer referenced) after both its forms moved to `FormField`/`TextInput`/`Button`/`StatusNote` — the latter's `ok` tone (emerald) also quietly fixes a pre-existing inconsistency where this one page used plain Tailwind `green` instead of the rest of the app's `emerald`. Verified live: edit → Saqlash/Bekor qilish round-trip opens and cancels correctly; a pre-existing deactivated test client ("Sinov Mijozi QA," left over from the original §3.3 build's own verification) still renders `Nofaol` correctly, confirming no regression.

**Shared reporting screens (`HisobotTab`, `StockOnHandTab`, `WipTab`, `ClientReportTab`, `YieldTab`) — confirmed, not rebuilt, per the task's own instruction.** All already restyled by the Menejer pass; live-verified each renders correctly inside Rahbar's new `AppNavShell` with real data (filter bar, totals strip, desktop table all populated) and no write affordances, matching the read-only-for-Rahbar shape. No changes made.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean. `npm test` 79/79 unchanged (no logic file touched). Full Playwright suite run once (per the task's reduced-testing plan): 4/4 passed clean (`chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` 42.3s, `full-chain.spec.ts` 1.1m, `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts` 42.0s, `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts` 58.1s, total 3.5m) — no regressions, consistent with the pre-verified fact that none of the 4 specs touch any `/rahbar` route. Live-browser-verified end to end as the real Rahbar test login (`.env.test`, phone-based): nav shell at both viewports (desktop sidebar exactly 9 links, mobile drawer opens with the same 9 + Chiqish, confirmed via accessibility-tree reads, not just CSS), dashboard stat tiles and severity-colored table cells against real seeded data, exceptions kind-filter/search interaction, settings edit/cancel/deactivate flow, and all 5 shared reporting screens.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** Ombor/Qorovul/Laborator nav (later prompts), printer wiring, Russian on staff screens, any logic/RLS/schema/query change, the reporting query engine itself, the live-inventory dashboard strip and the 2 unbuilt exception kinds and the Boshqaruv page merge (all three flagged above), responsive card views for the underlying reporting tables (unchanged from the Menejer pass's own flagged scope boundary).

## 2026-07-23 — Qorovul gate screens: visual redesign (mobile-only, mockup "BATU-Qorovul-Screens-v1_1.pdf")

**Context:** Match Qorovul's KIRIM/CHIQIM gate screens to the supplied mockup. Two deviations instructed up front and not built: no O'z/Ru toggle (staff screens stay Uzbek-only; the toggle's own weight-label gloss, e.g. "Yuk bilan vazn (Гружёный)", was already present in the current code and is NOT toggle-gated — it's a permanent part of the label in the mockup's own O'z-selected pages too, so nothing needed removing there), and no nav migration (`RoleShell`+`RoleTabs` top tabs kept exactly, `QorovulHome.tsx` untouched — two sections used constantly, tabs are correct here per the task).

**One real data gap, found by reading `useKirimTrips.ts`/`useChiqimTrips.ts` directly, not assumed.** Neither hook's query selects an owner reference at all (`KirimOrderRow`/`ChiqimRequestRow` have no `owner_id`) — so the mockup's "Buyurtmachi GLOBAL EXPORT" line in the stage-form's read-only block cannot be built without widening an existing `.select()`, which the hard guardrail rules out. Built every other read-only field (Seriya, Tur, So'ralgan, Moshina·haydovchi, all already fetched) and omitted Buyurtmachi — flagged here rather than built.

**A second, smaller data mismatch, also found by reading the hooks: `order_id`/`request.id` are raw uuids, not the "120826-001"-style human-readable serial the mockup shows.** Caught live in the browser, not by inspection alone — the first render showed full uuids in the `SerialChip`. The real per-line serial lives on `KirimLine.serial` (`ChiqimLine` has no serial field at all, by design — a chiqim request isn't tied to one product serial). Fixed by reusing precedent already built elsewhere in this app rather than inventing a new resolution: Menejer's own `KirimOrdersList.tsx` already uses "first line's serial represents the trip" for exactly this multi-line-order case, and `FinishedChiqimList.tsx` already uses the literal chip text `"So'rov"` for chiqim requests (which have no per-line serial to show at all). Both precedents applied here unchanged — `primarySerial(trip)` = `trip.lines[0]?.serial ?? trip.order.order_id`, CHIQIM's chip/tripInfo dropped to the literal `"So'rov"` text with the "Seriya (so'rov)" tripInfo row removed rather than showing a raw uuid.

**Two e2e-critical constraints found by grepping the specs before touching anything, not guessed:**
1. `getByRole('heading', {name: 'Faol'})`/`{name: 'Yakunlangan'}`, each followed by `.locator('xpath=following-sibling::div[1]')`, scope into these sections across all three specs touching Qorovul. Kept both heading strings byte-for-byte unchanged — no "1 · Faol yuklar" numbering prefix, no rewording, and nothing inserted between the heading and its immediate sibling div. The 3-counter Stat labels have no such coverage, confirmed by the same grep, so "Kirdi·bo'shatilmoqda" was freely renamed to "Bo'shatilmoqda" (KIRIM) / "Yuklanmoqda" (CHIQIM) per the mockup, and "Yakunlandi" got `tone="ok"` (always green, matching the mockup, since nothing depends on its current styling).
2. `PhotoField`'s labels — "Moshina raqami rasmi", "Tarozi rasmi", "Chiqish hujjati rasmi" — are matched via `div:has(> label:text-is(...))` in every gate-touching test, and "Tarozi rasmi" specifically is reused identically across all four stage/direction combinations even though the mockup wants more specific per-context wording ("Yuk bilan vazn rasmi (tarozi)", "Bo'sh vazn rasmi", etc.). Kept the existing generic labels exactly as-is — renaming would have broken every gate test in the suite. Also confirmed the form's own submit button text ("Qabul qilish"/"Yakunlash", not the mockup's "Saqlash") is a deliberate existing pattern, not an oversight: the row-level trigger button disappears once the form opens, and e2e clicks the identically-named button a second time to submit — reusing the same accessible name is what lets one locator find "the currently-visible primary action" whether the form is open or closed. Kept unchanged.

**`GateStageForm.tsx` gained real structure** (previously it had none of this): a stage/direction badge (`KIRIM/CHIQIM · BOSQICH N`, ok-toned at stage 1, problem-toned at stage 2), a plain-language title+subtitle pair, a read-only `tripInfo` block (stage 1 only — the mockup's own stage-2 screens drop the full manager-values block, showing just the saved weight instead), a saved-weight-with-photo-confirmation line at stage 2 (`{label} (saqlangan)` + "rasm bor"), a live-computed net-weight preview box at stage 2 ("Yuk og'irligi (avto): N kg", verified live against real data: saved 2,900 kg − typed 480 kg = 2,420 kg, computed purely from values already in the browser — `net_kg` itself stays the same generated column it always was), a large bold weight input with a floating "kg" suffix, and a confirm button that's proactively `disabled` until every required field is present (verified live: stayed disabled with a valid weight typed and no photos attached) — on top of, not instead of, the existing on-submit validation. `tripInfo`/`savedWeightKg` are new but fully optional props, built from data the parent tabs already fetch in full; no new query anywhere in this component.

**`PhotoField.tsx` — restyled around the upload path, not through it.** Added a bordered box that tones green once a file is attached, a filename display (new local state, mirrors how `sizes` was already tracked), and a "majburiy" badge. The badge is a `<span>` *sibling* of the `<label>`, not nested inside it — `<label>` renders only the raw label text, confirmed live via `label.textContent === 'Tarozi rasmi'` (exact match holds) with a real 8px visual gap to the badge (confirmed via `getBoundingClientRect`, since the two elements read as directly adjacent in a plain-text extraction despite the CSS margin between them). `accept="image/*"`, `compressImage`, `required`, and the decode-fallback error handling are all byte-for-byte unchanged.

**Row cards (`QorovulKirimTab.tsx`/`QorovulChiqimTab.tsx`) — `SerialChip` + type-summary headline + status-dependent meta line + checkmark, `DD.MM · HH:MM` time format instead of the browser locale default.** The active-row meta line differs by state, matching the mockup: not-started shows `So'ralgan {total} kg · {driver} · {plate}`; once stage 1 is saved (red) it shows the already-recorded weight and what's still pending (`Yuk bilan {kg} kg · bo'sh vazn kutilmoqda` for KIRIM, `Bo'sh {kg} kg · yuklandi · yuk bilan vazn kutilmoqda` for CHIQIM) — with `{driver} · {plate}` always appended regardless of state (see the locator regression below; this isn't just the mockup's own "who is this truck" cue). Row-trigger buttons changed from outlined `secondary` to solid `primary`/`danger` (matching the mockup's black "Qabul qilish" / red "Yakunlash") and bumped to `size="lg"` for a bigger mobile tap target — text unchanged, so this doesn't touch the button-reuse pattern above. CHIQIM has no `declared_total` column on `chiqim_requests`; its "So'ralgan" total and line count are both derived client-side from `chiqim_lines.qty_kg`, already fetched in full — no new query.

**🚩 A real locator regression, found by the required end-of-task e2e run, not by inspection.** The first run failed 3 of 4 specs, all at the identical point: `faol.locator('.rounded-md.border-red-300', {hasText: <plate>}).toBeVisible()` timing out right after stage 1's submit. Root cause: the plate/driver text — which `PLATE`/`PLATE_IN`/`PLATE_OUT` in these specs are e2e's own synthetic values used specifically to find a row again by ID — had been dropped from the row entirely once a row turned red (and, separately, from the completed row too, breaking `yakunlangan.locator('.rounded-md', {hasText: <plate>})` in the same two specs) in favour of the mockup's own "already-recorded weight" phrasing. This was a real behavior gap this pass introduced, not a stale locator to update: the plate/driver line is genuinely useful information on a completed or in-progress row, not just an e2e hook. Fixed by keeping `{driver} · {plate}` present in the meta line for every state (active-not-started, active-red, completed) rather than replacing it — the completed row gained its own dedicated `{driver} · {plate}` line under the serial/type headline for the same reason. Confirmed via `git diff` against the pre-task file that this was the only place text got dropped rather than added-to.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean throughout. `npm test` 79/79 unchanged (no logic file touched — only `.tsx` components and `PhotoField.tsx`'s presentational state). Full Playwright suite run repeatedly per the task's own reduced-testing plan, not just once, because the first run surfaced a real bug: run 1 was 1/4 passed, 3/4 failed on the locator regression above (every spec that exercises the Qorovul gate flow — `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts`, `full-chain.spec.ts`, `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts`); fixed, then run 2 was 3/4 passed, with `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` failing on an unrelated `page.waitForURL` timeout inside its own mid-test Ombor-role login, nowhere near anything this task touched. Re-ran that one spec alone and it passed clean (38.5s) — confirmed a one-off flake, not a regression, same as this repo's own prior-documented precedent for isolating flakiness from real breaks. Ran the full suite once more for a single clean combined result and hit a second, different flake: `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts` (also untouched by this task) failed twice in a row on its own early login step during test seeding, then passed clean (43.6s) on a third attempt, with zero running `node` processes found in between to explain it as leftover contention. Net result across every run: every spec that actually exercises code this task touched passed consistently once the real regression was fixed; the only remaining flakiness was two isolated login-step timeouts on two different, otherwise-passing, unrelated specs — reported here rather than quietly re-run away. Live-browser-verified as the real Qorovul test login (`.env.test`, phone-based) at mobile width (the primary target) and confirmed no horizontal overflow / no console errors at desktop width (must-not-break, not optimized-for): both KIRIM stage 1 and stage 2 forms opened and rendered correctly with real trip data, the button-lock and live net-weight math were both confirmed against real numbers, and the raw-uuid serial-display bug was caught and corrected during this same live pass, before the e2e run surfaced the plate/driver regression above.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** Ombor/Laborator screens, printer wiring, any language toggle, any logic/RLS/schema/query change, the "Buyurtmachi" omission (flagged above).

## 2026-07-23 — Qorovul gate screens: proper visual redesign (supersedes the prior pass)

**Context:** the prior entry's own pass was judged over-constrained — real visual change (owner names, exact mockup wording) got dropped to preserve every existing string, producing "almost no visual change." This task explicitly reopened two of that pass's own guardrails and gave a third, unrelated fix:

1. **String changes are now allowed to break e2e locators, on the condition that the spec gets updated to match** — "the design wins, the test follows." Not a general license: applied narrowly, only to the specific strings the mockup names (section headings, photo labels), not invented beyond that.
2. **`owner_id` may be added to both gate queries** — explicitly scoped as "a `.select()` addition and a name lookup, nothing more." Confirmed via direct SQL first, not assumed: `owner_id uuid` already exists on both `kirim_orders` and `chiqim_requests` (so this is genuinely query-only, no migration), and `owners` has a blanket `auth.uid() IS NOT NULL` SELECT policy, so Qorovul's role can already read it.
3. **Mobile header fix**, unrelated to the mockup itself — `RoleShell.tsx`'s header had no responsive behavior at all (one non-wrapping flex row), so title/tabs/username/Chiqish collided and wrapped across three lines at phone width.

**Locator-safety audit before touching anything, since "Yakunlangan" is not Qorovul-exclusive.** Grepped `src/` first: `LaboratorKirimTab.tsx`/`LaboratorChiqimTab.tsx` render the identical heading text "Yakunlangan". Renaming Qorovul's own heading to "2 · Yakunlangan" is safe, but every e2e occurrence of that locator had to be individually traced back to its nearest preceding `loginAs()` call to tell which role's screen it actually targets before deciding whether to touch it. Result: `full-chain.spec.ts` lines 132/398 and `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` line 152 are Qorovul-context (updated); `full-chain.spec.ts` lines 179/290 and `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts` lines 161/274 are Laborator-context (left untouched). "Faol" has no such ambiguity — Qorovul-exclusive, every occurrence updated. Also confirmed `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts` and everything in `tests/e2e/helpers/` seed `gate_weighings` directly via `page.evaluate` + raw Supabase calls, never touching Qorovul's rendered UI at all — neither needed any change.

**`RoleShell.tsx` (shared by Qorovul, Ombor, Laborator) — rebuilt as two rows instead of one.** Row 1: title (drops the "BATU EXPORT — " prefix below `sm`, confirmed via computed `display:none` + `offsetParent === null` at 375px, not just visual inspection) and a compact Chiqish; username hidden below `sm` the same way. Row 2: nav, given its own horizontally-scrollable row rather than fighting row 1 for space. `RoleTabs.tsx` (also shared with Ombor) gained real `touch.secondary` (48px) tap targets on each link — previously plain text with no hit-area padding at all. Both fixes reach Ombor's and Laborator's own screens as a beneficial side effect; neither role's own content was touched. Verified live: at 375px, nav's `scrollWidth === clientWidth` (no scroll needed, all three tabs fit), Chiqish's right edge sits at 363px (12px clear of the 375px viewport), and `document.body.scrollWidth <= window.innerWidth` (no page-level horizontal overflow) — confirmed again unbroken at ~800px.

**`owner_id` wired through:** `KirimOrderRow`/`ChiqimRequestRow` gained the field, both `.select()` calls gained the column, both `QorovulKirimTab.tsx`/`QorovulChiqimTab.tsx` gained `useOwners(true)` + an `ownerName()` resolver (§3.3 pattern: `includeInactive` so a deactivated client's historical trips still resolve to a real name). Card headlines are now `{owner} · {type}` (verified live against real seeded data: "Boysun Quritilgan Mevalar · Subxon", "Toshkent Agro Savdo · Isfara", etc.), and the stage-1 read-only block gained its own "Buyurtmachi" row between Seriya and Tur (KIRIM) / as the first row (CHIQIM, which has no Seriya row to follow — see below). This directly reverses the prior entry's own flagged omission.

**Still not shown, and still a genuinely separate gap from the one above:** CHIQIM's request id remains a raw uuid with no human-readable equivalent anywhere in the schema (`chiqim_lines` has no `serial` column) — this was never about `owner_id` and the new permission doesn't cover it. `SerialChip` keeps the literal `"So'rov"` placeholder (Menejer's own `FinishedChiqimList.tsx` precedent), and the stage-1 tripInfo block still has no "Seriya (so'rov)" row.

**String changes, matched exactly to the mockup, each with its e2e updates:**
- Section headings: "Faol" → "1 · Faol yuklar", "Yakunlangan" → "2 · Yakunlangan" (both tabs). 7 heading-locator updates across the 3 affected specs (traced above).
- `PhotoField` labels: "Moshina raqami rasmi" → "Moshina rasmi" (4 spec updates). The scale-photo label is no longer one generic "Tarozi rasmi" reused across all four stage/direction combinations — it's now derived as `` `${stageTitle} rasmi${stage === 1 ? ' (tarozi)' : ''}` ``, reusing the `stageTitle` constant `GateStageForm.tsx` already computed for the big heading, so it comes out to "Yuk bilan vazn rasmi (tarozi)" / "Bo'sh vazn rasmi" / "Bo'sh vazn rasmi (tarozi)" / "Yuk bilan vazn rasmi" for KIRIM-1/KIRIM-2/CHIQIM-1/CHIQIM-2 respectively, matching the mockup's own per-page wording exactly. 7 spec updates (one per occurrence, each mapped to its specific stage/direction by reading the surrounding test code, not pattern-matched blindly).
- Stage-1's own confirm button: "Qabul qilish" → "Saqlash" — the mockup uses two different verbs for two different actions (the row-trigger accepts the truck onto the gate; the form's own button saves the weighing), where the prior pass had deliberately collapsed both into one reused string so a single locator could find "whichever button is currently showing." Splitting them apart meant the 4 e2e blocks that used to click the same name twice in a row now click "Qabul qilish" once (open) then "Saqlash" once (submit) — updated in all 4 (`full-chain.spec.ts` ×2, `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts` ×1, `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` ×1). Stage 2 keeps "Yakunlash" in both places, matching the mockup, so that pattern is untouched. The submitting-state text also now differentiates ("Saqlanmoqda…"/"Yakunlanmoqda…") — free, since no locator reads it.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean throughout. `npm test` 79/79 unchanged. Live-browser-verified end to end as the real Qorovul test login at mobile width: both stage-1 (badge/title/subtitle/tripInfo-with-Buyurtmachi/"Moshina rasmi"/"Saqlash"(disabled-until-valid)) and stage-2 (saved-weight-with-photo-confirm/"Bo'sh vazn rasmi"/unchanged "Yakunlash") rendered exactly as designed against real data, and every card headline resolved a real owner name. Full Playwright suite run once, per this task's own testing plan (no mid-work runs) — **4/4 passed clean on the first attempt**, no iteration needed: every one of the 21 individually-traced locator updates across the three affected specs was correct on the first try.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** Ombor's/Laborator's own screen content (only their shared `RoleShell`/`RoleTabs` chrome improved), printer wiring, any language toggle, any RLS/trigger/business-logic change, the CHIQIM request reference-number gap (flagged above, distinct from the now-resolved Buyurtmachi gap).

## 2026-07-23 — Qorovul redesign: real-phone-width audit, one real bug found and fixed

**Context:** the merged redesign had never been checked at an actual 375px viewport — every prior verification pass (this one included, before today) resized the browser but never actually looked hard at wrapping/overlap at that exact width.
