Production deploys have been frozen since 2026-07-18, so this was also the first chance to get a real deploy preview building.

**Tooling note, reported rather than worked around silently:** the browser tool's screenshot/zoom capture timed out repeatedly in this session (consistent across multiple attempts, on a page that loaded and rendered with zero console errors) — a tool-level issue, not a page problem. Audited via precise DOM geometry instead (`getBoundingClientRect`/`getComputedStyle`/`scrollWidth` vs `clientWidth`) rather than eyeballing pixels — arguably more rigorous for exactly the "does X collide/wrap/clip" questions this audit asked, since it gives exact pixel numbers rather than an impression.

**Audit, item by item, at a genuine 375×812 viewport:**
1. **Header** — clean. No page-level horizontal overflow. Title's right edge (63px) sits 237px clear of Chiqish's left edge (301px) — no collision. "BATU EXPORT — " prefix and username both confirmed `display:none`/`offsetParent:null` below `sm`, not just hidden by convention. Chiqish's own right edge sits at 363px, 12px clear of the 375px viewport.
2. **Both tabs reachable** — clean. KIRIM (12–74px), CHIQIM (78–153px), Hisobotlar (157–247px) all fully inside [0,375], `nav.scrollWidth === nav.clientWidth` (no overflow, no scroll needed), each a real 48px touch target, 128px of unused width to spare.
3. **Card layout — broken, found and fixed.** The active-row headline (`{owner} · {type}`) and meta line had no `truncate`/width constraint and sat in a `flex flex-wrap` row with the serial chip. With a real (not mockup-example-length) owner name, the headline measured 48px tall (wrapped to 2 lines, dropping below the chip onto its own line first) and the meta line measured 40px (also 2 lines) — ballooning one row's card to 150px tall and leaving the `size="lg"` action button visually stranded near the top of a much taller card than intended. The *completed*-row cards already had `truncate` applied from an earlier pass and were never affected — only the active-row cards (`QorovulKirimTab.tsx`/`QorovulChiqimTab.tsx`, both directions) had this gap, which is exactly why it wasn't caught the first two times: neither prior pass happened to check a long-owner-name row's *height*, only whether the right text was present. Fixed by dropping `flex-wrap` (chip stays fixed-width, headline now shares the row instead of dropping below it) and adding `min-w-0 flex-1 truncate` to the headline span and `truncate` to the meta div. Re-measured after the fix: card height 150px → 82px, headline 48px → 24px (confirmed genuinely truncating, not just newly fitting: `scrollWidth` 259px vs `clientWidth` 89px, `text-overflow:ellipsis` active), meta 40px → 20px.
4. **Counters** — clean. Three 106px-wide tiles, 12px gaps, labels ("Bo'shatilmoqda" included) single-line and inside their own tile bounds. Tone colors also checked directly (not just spacing): neutral tile transparent, active-count tile a light red/pink hue, completed tile a light green hue, matching the mockup's white/pink/green tiles.
5. **Stage forms** — weight input confirmed 30px/bold (prominent), photo-field boxes confirmed non-overflowing at 283–343px wide, computed net confirmed rendering correctly ("Yuk og'irligi (avto): 2,420 kg", math re-verified) and on-screen (no horizontal overflow) once scrolled to. Honestly reported rather than flagged as broken: the stage-1 form is 697px tall on its own (badge + title/subtitle + a 4–5-row read-only block + two photo fields + a large weight field + a size-`lg` confirm button + caption + cancel, all with real spacing) — reaching its own confirm button always requires some scroll on an 812px-tall phone viewport. That's scrolling *within* one content-rich form, not scrolling *past* other list items to reach it, which is what the task's phrasing was actually asking about — the form opens inline exactly where its trigger button was tapped, so there's no separate "long list" to scroll past.
6. **Mockup gaps** — one remains, unchanged from the prior pass and not something this task's permissions cover: `chiqim_requests`/`chiqim_lines` still have no human-readable reference number anywhere in the schema, so CHIQIM's serial chip still reads the literal placeholder "So'rov" rather than a real code. Everything else drawn across the mockup's 7 pages (both dashboards, both stage forms in both directions, the read-only context block, the saved-weight-with-photo-confirmation line, the live net computation, the locked-until-complete confirm button) is implemented and was re-confirmed rendering during this same audit.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean. `npm test` 79/79 unchanged. Full Playwright suite: first run 3/4 passed, with `full-chain.spec.ts` failing on an Ombor "Tayyor Mahsulot" locator timeout — a screen this task's two-line CSS-class fix never went near. Re-ran that spec alone and it passed clean (56.6s), confirming a one-off flake consistent with this project's now well-documented pattern, not a regression.

## 2026-07-23 — Ombor: full visual redesign, all four sections (mockups "BATU-Storage-S1-S2-mockup.html", "BATU-Storage-S3-Tayyor-Mahsulot-v1_2.pdf", "BATU-Storage-S4-Skladdan-CHIQIM-v2.pdf")

**Context:** match all four Ombor sections (Skladga KIRIM, Moykaga Chiqarish, Tayyor Mahsulot, Skladdan CHIQIM) to the supplied mockups — same string/locator-follows-design permissions as the Qorovul v2 pass, plus permission to add fields to an existing `.select()` when a mockup needs data already in the schema. `/mnt/skills/public/frontend-design/SKILL.md` does not exist in this environment; proceeded using the design-system precedent already established across the Menejer/Rahbar/Qorovul passes (`components/ui/tokens.ts`) instead.

**Three items inspected and flagged before coding, each resolved with the user before implementation:**
1. **Intake photo field — mockup wrong, not the app.** The mockup's S1 accept-form photo field is "Hujjat rasmi · ixtiyoriy" (client's invoice, optional); the real field is "Uyum rasmi" (pile photo), required by `IntakeAcceptForm.tsx`'s own validation. These photograph different things — relabeling the required pile-photo to "Hujjat rasmi" would misdescribe it; making it optional changes accept-flow validation, not a string. Kept "Uyum rasmi" required exactly as-is, restyled only its container.
2. **CHIQIM gate-weighing status, read added, kept non-blocking, both states shown.** `useOmborChiqimRequests.ts` had no join to `gate_weighings` at all — added one (`dir='chiqim'`, keyed by `request_id`), same shape as the Qorovul-pass `owner_id` precedent. Displayed as a status line only; never gates "Yuklashni boshlash," matching this app's consistent never-block philosophy. Per explicit instruction, the negative state renders too ("Qorovul hali bo'sh vaznni olmagan"), not just the confirmed one — an absent gate-status line would have read as a rendering gap, not a real state.
3. **"Butun pallet yo'q" scan-screen warning — not built.** The matching logic (`checkFeasibility`, subset-sum over `useAvailableFinishedStock`) exists, but it was built for Menejer's request-creation screen, before any scanning happens. `useAvailableFinishedStock`'s "claimed" check only excludes pallets already in `dispatch_manifest`, written at *finish* time — not pallets already sitting in this (or another concurrently open) request's in-progress scan list. Reusing it live during scanning risked confidently wrong warnings. Kept the existing `missingKg`-per-line shortfall computation, restyled into the mockup's amber warning box and moved to render live during scanning (previously only shown at the confirm step) instead of adding a new claim.

**S1 Skladga KIRIM (`OmborIntakeTab.tsx`, `IntakeAcceptForm.tsx`) — flattened to match the mockup's own stated shape.** The mockup's own caption is explicit: "Window 1: lines the gate has weighed in but Ombor hasn't accepted yet — one card per `kirim_lines` row, so a two-product truck shows two cards sharing a plate." The prior structure grouped pending lines by order (an outer Card per order, inner compact Cards per line) — `IntakeLine` already carries `plate`/`driver`/`order_date` directly on every line, so the order-level grouping wrapper was dropped entirely; each line is now its own top-level Card with `SerialChip` + owner·type headline, kv rows (E'lon qilingan / Darvoza), and an amber `StatusNote` for the not-yet-weighed state (previously plain italic "kutilmoqda (darvoza)" text). `IntakeAcceptForm` gained a kv context block (Seriya/Egasi·tur/Moshina·haydovchi/E'lon qilingan — `ownerName` added as a new resolved-string prop, same pattern as the existing `typeName` prop), a read-only "Sana" (today, client-computed display only, not a new persisted field), and the weight input became the visually "big" field the mockup shows. Submit button text: "Qabul qilish" → "Qabul qilish va shtrix-kod chiqarish" (mockup's exact wording).

**S2 Moykaga (`OmborMoykaTab.tsx`, `MoykaSendForm.tsx`) — from bare unstyled divs to the full design-system.** Neither file used any `components/ui/` component before this pass. Rows → `Card` (tone="pending" for re-wash, matching the mockup's amber card), 3-tile `Stat` row (Jami xom/Qaytgan · Yuborilgan · Qoldiq — all values already computed by `useMoykaSerials`, no new logic), full-width "+ Moykaga yuborish" button. Re-wash rows gained the mockup's own note banner text ("⟳ Laborator qaytardi — kalibr palletlari bekor qilindi, qayta yuvishga tayyor"), not previously shown as a distinct note. `MoykaSendForm` rebuilt on `FormField`/`TextInput`/`Button` with the same kv-context-block pattern as `IntakeAcceptForm`; its weight input now pre-fills with `serial.available` (the full sendable balance) rather than starting empty — matching both the mockup's own prefilled example and the app's own established `IntakeAcceptForm` convention of prefilling a weight field with the already-known figure.

**S3 Tayyor Mahsulot (`OmborTayyorTab.tsx`, `FinishedReceiptForm.tsx`) — the one real structural change, not just a reskin.** The mockup's Window 1 dashboard card shows the 3-tile stats and both actions ("+ Qabul qilish", "Tugallash") unconditionally, with no collapse affordance at all; the previous code hid everything behind a "⋯" toggle added in an earlier density pass. Dropped that outer gate — stats and both buttons are now always visible per card; the "⋯"-driven pallet history now only appears folded into the Tugallash confirm view (`palletList(...)` moved inside the `confirming` block), matching the mockup's own combined "Qabul tarixi + 'Tugallash' tasdiqi" page exactly. The confirm panel itself became a bordered amber "Tugallashni tasdiqlang" box with kv rows (Yuborilgan(xom)/Jami tayyor mahsulot/Yakuniy yo'qotish), matching the mockup's visual weight for an important, locking confirmation — the "Ha, tugallash" button itself stayed `variant="primary"` (the app's one established dark confirm-action color) rather than mockup-matching amber, since Button has no amber variant and a prior pass's own documented lesson (`className` overrides losing the Tailwind cascade) made a custom-colored override not worth the risk for one button; the surrounding panel carries the visual weight instead. Window 2 (Tugallangan) kept its own existing expand-for-detail pattern, just reskinned to `Card`+`SerialChip`. `FinishedReceiptForm` gained the same kv-context/Sana pattern as the other two forms plus the mockup's button text ("Qabul qilish" → "Saqlash va shtrix-kod chiqarish") — confirmed live this is genuinely a *different* string from S1's "Qabul qilish va shtrix-kod chiqarish", not a copy-paste of the same one (this distinction is what broke one e2e locator during the fix pass, see below).

**S4 Skladdan CHIQIM (`OmborChiqimTab.tsx`, `useOmborChiqimRequests.ts`) — heaviest content change.** Card header dropped the serial chip per the mockup's own note ("No serial on the request"), now a bold owner title + "So'rov · date · plate · driver" meta line + a `StatusPill tone="info"` "Nishon X kg" badge + a light-grey per-line type·calibre·qty breakdown box (derived from `request.lines`, already fetched) + the new gate-status line (flagged item #2). The "⋯"-style row-click-to-expand became a dedicated "Yuklashni boshlash" button, matching the mockup's own named action. Inside the expanded scan view: added the kv header block (previously only shown collapsed), replaced the bottom-of-form per-line verification Cards with live progress bars next to each Nishon line (derived from the same `lineStatus()`/`lineTotal()` already computed, no new logic), switched the scanned-pallet list from per-line-nested to one flat chronological list (matching the mockup's own "Skanerlangan palletlar (N)" shape — `dispatch_manifest` doesn't group by line either, so this is arguably more honest to the underlying data than the nested version was), and moved the running-total `Stat` + the shortfall warning (flagged item #3, kept as `missingKg`) from the top/confirm-only to a footer position live during scanning, matching the mockup's own layout order. Window 2 (Yuklandi) kept its real, mockup-unshown manifest-detail-and-undo functionality (real feature from an earlier pass, not something to drop), reskinned only; its collapsed summary intentionally does *not* show the mockup's "actual loaded weight · pallet count" (that data is only lazily fetched once a request is expanded, by original design — showing it collapsed would mean a new eager fetch across every finished request, which is exactly the category of change flagged item #3 already argued against).

**Three real bugs found and fixed during live verification, not assumed safe from inspection alone.**
1. **A `className`-override cascade bug, the same category as a prior pass's own documented lesson, tripped again in a new spot.** All three new "big" weight inputs (`IntakeAcceptForm`, `MoykaSendForm`, `FinishedReceiptForm`) passed `className="text-2xl font-bold"` to `TextInput`, whose own base classes already bake in `text-base` — confirmed live via `getComputedStyle` that the font stayed 16px, not 24px, on all three (font-weight worked since nothing else sets it; font-size silently lost the cascade). Fixed with the `!` important-modifier (`!text-2xl`) at all three call sites, the same established fix pattern from the Menejer pass's own `Button`-override bug — re-confirmed 24px live after the fix.
2. **A dangling "· " on CHIQIM's finished-request header, live data exposed a pre-existing data gap the old header never displayed.** Several real historical `chiqim_requests` rows have no `chiqim_lines` at all (predating some earlier seeding convention) — the new `{ownerName} · {typeSummary}` header joined an empty typeSummary, rendering a bare trailing "·" with nothing after it. Not a regression in the underlying data (the old header never showed a type summary at all, so it never exposed this), but a real new cosmetic gap this pass's own added content introduced. Fixed by only appending the "· {typeSummary}" segment when `request.lines.length > 0`.
3. **An unnecessary capitalization drifted from the established sentence-case convention.** S1's received-card meta line capitalized "Tarozi kutilmoqda" (matching a *different*, newly-added amber note's own sentence-starting capital) where the original, pre-existing text was lowercase "tarozi kutilmoqda" mid-sentence — reverted to lowercase, matching the app's own established copy convention and removing dependency on an assumption about Playwright's case-sensitivity in the e2e check that reads this exact text.

**E2E: three specs updated (`chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts`, `full-chain.spec.ts`, `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts`), traced individually against every string/structure this pass changed, not pattern-matched blindly — three real fix categories, one self-inflicted.**
1. **Heading text**, matched exactly to the new `SectionHeading` strings where Playwright's default substring match didn't already cover a prepended "N · " (e.g. "Yuklash uchun so'rovlar" → "1 · Yuklashga tayyor — moshina keldi" needed an explicit update; "Moykada — chiqishi kutilmoqda" → "1 · Moykada — chiqishi kutilmoqda" didn't, since the old string is a genuine substring of the new one).
2. **S4's row-is-a-button pattern replaced.** `omborW1.getByRole('button', { name: new RegExp(PLATE) })` relied on the collapsed row itself being one clickable button with the plate in its accessible name — S4's new card has no such button (plate is now plain text, the action is the separate "Yuklashni boshlash" button). Replaced with `omborW1.locator('div.rounded-md.border.border-slate-200.p-3', { hasText: PLATE })` (the card) then `.getByRole('button', { name: 'Yuklashni boshlash' })` scoped inside it, in all 4 occurrences across the two specs that exercise S4's open-request flow. The literal `'✓ Aniq mos keldi'` string this same flow checked for (S4's old dedicated per-line success message) no longer exists — replaced with `expect(page.getByText('Yetarli emas')).not.toBeVisible()`, checking the same underlying fact (the scan fully satisfies every line, no shortfall) through the new progress-bar-only UI rather than a dedicated confirmation string.
3. **A real strict-mode violation, not assumed safe: `SerialChip` (a `<span>`) also carries the `rounded-md` class its parent `Card` (a `<div>`) does.** Every bare `.rounded-md` selector filtered by a serial (as opposed to a plate, which never appears inside `SerialChip` itself) now matches both the Card and its own nested chip — caught live via the e2e run itself (`strict mode violation: ... resolved to 2 elements`), not predicted correctly by inspection alone beforehand. Fixed at all 8 affected call sites across the two specs (S1's "2 · Qabul qilingan" window, S2's "1 · Yuborishga tayyor" window, S3's "Tugallangan" window) by adding the `div` type selector (`div.rounded-md`), which `SerialChip`'s `<span>` can never match — left untouched everywhere the selector already filtered by plate (Qorovul/Menejer screens, unaffected and out of this task's scope) or was already the full `div.rounded-md.border.border-slate-200.p-3` chain.
4. **One self-inflicted mistake in the fix pass itself, caught by re-running rather than assumed correct:** `IntakeAcceptForm`'s submit button ("Qabul qilish va shtrix-kod chiqarish", S1's own mockup wording) and `FinishedReceiptForm`'s ("Saqlash va shtrix-kod chiqarish", S3's) are two similar-but-different strings — `full-chain.spec.ts`'s S1 `acceptLine` helper was first updated to the wrong one of the two, which timed out the full test (150s) waiting for a button name that was never going to appear. Corrected to the right string for its own context; the other two occurrences (both genuinely S3) were already correct.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean throughout (same 3 pre-existing unrelated warnings). `npm test` 79/79 unchanged (no logic file touched — `useOmborChiqimRequests.ts`'s only change is an additive read). Live-browser-verified end to end as the real Ombor test login at 375px width across all four sections and all three forms against real seeded data, including two real form submissions (a Moyka send, a finished-pallet receipt through to the Tugallash confirm panel — backed out of actually confirming Tugallash itself, since finalizing a real serial with a fabricated 72.2% loss for verification purposes would have been a genuine, void-never-delete mutation with no reason to make it permanent). Full Playwright suite run three times: run 1, 3/4 failed (all three of the categories above, none yet known); run 2, 2/4 failed (categories 1–3 fixed, the self-inflicted button-text mistake and the strict-mode violation not yet caught); run 3, **4/4 clean** (4.4m total) after every fix above.

## 2026-07-23 — Laborator: full visual redesign (both tabs + new history screen), real-use account created

**🔒 `BATU-Laborator-Screens-v2.pdf` encodes the superseded v1.5 §5.5 model and must not be built from — visual language only.** Its own caption on the CHIQIM dashboard page says "identical to KIRIM (spec §5.5, locked)"; that model was replaced wholesale by the v1.9 revision in Step 8 (SPEC.md §5.5's own header: "REVISED v1.9 — replaces the v1.5 design wholesale"). The mockup's CHIQIM pages show a dispatch-request subject (So'rov/moshina/tarkib) and end every flow at a plain "Yakunlash · tahlil to'liq" save with no verdict — neither is what v1.9 actually specifies or what this app builds. Flagging this explicitly, in writing, so a future session reaching for this PDF doesn't rediscover the mismatch the hard way.

**The real surprise going in: the data layer was already 100% v1.9-compliant before this pass touched anything.** Read `useLaboratorKirim.ts`/`useLaboratorChiqim.ts` against SPEC.md §5.5 before writing any code, per the task's own "inspect and report, flag anything needing a logic change" instruction — found nothing to flag. `useLaboratorChiqim.ts` already queried `wash_cycles` directly (`status='final'`), never `chiqim_requests`; `AwaitingCycle` already carried every field §5.5.3 names (serial, cycleNo, pallets, producedDate, both targets); the verdict step already existed as two explicit buttons (`ChiqimTahlilForm`'s `requireVerdict` path, `LaboratorChiqimTab`'s `handleSera`), never auto-derived; sulfur conditionality and the CHIQIM target-beside-the-reading display already worked exactly as specified. This task ended up being the same shape as the Qorovul/Ombor passes — visual redesign of already-correct logic, not a rebuild — confirmed by inspection first rather than assumed from the task's own framing.

**One presentational gap closed, not a logic change: KIRIM's target-moisture display.** SPEC §5.5.2's own text — "the client's target is displayed here for reference only, greyed, with no pass/fail treatment" — wasn't fully built: `LaboratorKirimTab.tsx`'s Window 3 already showed it in the expand, but `KirimTahlilForm` (the entry form itself) showed nothing. `target_moisture_pct` was already fetched on `AwaitingLine`, just not passed through as a prop. Added `line`/`ownerName`/`typeName` props (same pattern `IntakeAcceptForm`/`MoykaSendForm` already established in the Ombor pass) and a greyed `(Talab: X%)` suffix next to the Namligi label — deliberately no comparison/soft-warn logic alongside it, unlike `ChiqimTahlilForm`'s, since KIRIM is descriptive-only by design (§5.5.2, correction #3).

**Both tabs restyled to the mockup's established grammar** (3-tile counter row with the amber middle tile, numbered windows "1 · Tahlil kutilmoqda — namuna oling" / "2 · Sera natijasi kutilmoqda (1 kun)" / "3 · Yakunlangan", `SerialChip` + owner·type headline, Window 3's compact two-value `namligi · SO₂ mg/kg` summary) — `LaboratorKirimTab.tsx`/`LaboratorChiqimTab.tsx` had no `components/ui/` usage at all before this pass (plain spans, no counters). CHIQIM's card content was already correct per corrections #1/#2 (parent serial, client, type, pallet count, jami kg, production date, cycle number — confirmed unchanged through the restyle, re-verified live against real data with multiple wash cycles). Window 3's verdict now renders as a `StatusPill` (tone `ok`/`problem`) instead of plain colored text.

**Both Tahlil forms rebuilt to the mockup's form language** (eyebrow `StatusPill`, kv context block, big bold numeric input with a floating unit suffix, dashed-adjacent optional photo field via unchanged `PhotoField`, blue "Natija qayerga tegishli" explainer). `ChiqimTahlilForm`'s explainer reworded per explicit instruction — the mockup's own text says "shu jo'natmaning barcha palletlariga tegishli" (this dispatch's pallets); CHIQIM isn't tied to a dispatch at all, so it now says the result applies to the wash cycle instead, explicitly naming that it does *not* apply to a dispatch/So'rov. `ChiqimTahlilForm`'s kv block shows the v1.9 wash-cycle fields (Seriya/Egasi/Tur/Pallet soni·og'irlik/Ishlab chiqarilgan·sikl) via a new `cycle: AwaitingCycle` prop, replacing the old `targetMoisturePct`/`pallets`-only pair — not the mockup's So'rov/Moshina/Tarkib. `PhotoField` itself untouched (off-limits internals), same as every prior pass.

**New history screen (`LaboratorTarixTab.tsx` + `useLaboratorHistory.ts`), §5.5.6 — didn't exist before this task.** Reuses `HistoryView.tsx` and `useIntakeHistory.ts`'s exact shape (server-side date range, client-side enrichment filters) rather than inventing a new shell. One section, both directions, filters: date range, KIRIM/CHIQIM, buyurtmachi, tur, kalibr, seriya, verdikt — per SPEC's own "a lookup is a filter, not a screen" principle. `lab_results` carries no owner/type/calibre itself; both scopes resolve them through the same `kirim_lines → kirim_orders` chain their own live tabs already use (a CHIQIM row's wash cycle resolves to a serial the identical way `useLaboratorChiqim.ts` does it). **Kalibr filtering is CHIQIM-only by construction, not a gap** — resolved via `sampled_pallet → finished_pallets.calibre_id`; KIRIM tests raw material before any calibre exists, so there's nothing for that filter to match there, verified live (selecting a calibre correctly narrowed 11 results to 4, all CHIQIM). Wired into `LaboratorHome.tsx` as a third "Tarix" tab and `App.tsx` as `/laborator/tarix`.

**Real-use Laborator account created, distinct from the existing `TEST_LABORATOR` automation credential (900000005).** Flagged before creating anything: a Laborator-role test account already existed (same 2026-07-17 batch as the other 4 roles), but CLAUDE.md frames those as dedicated test infrastructure, not a real person's login — confirmed with the user before proceeding, who noted the distinction matters because `tested_by` surfaces in the passport and reports. Created via direct SQL against `auth.users`/`auth.identities`/`profiles` (the Edge Function approach remains rejected per the existing precedent — no live `rahbar` session to call it from), phone `900000006`, `full_name` **not** `TEST `-prefixed. Applied the documented GoTrue NULL-token-column fix proactively (all of `confirmation_token`/`recovery_token`/`email_change_*`/`phone_change*`/`reauthentication_token` set to empty string in the same INSERT, not a follow-up UPDATE) rather than rediscovering the 500 the hard way — confirmed via direct `crypt()` check that the password hash matches AND via a real login through the actual app (not just the bcrypt spot-check) that GoTrue accepts it end to end. Password reported to the user directly, not committed anywhere.

**E2e: two specs updated (`full-chain.spec.ts`, `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts`), traced individually — `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` never touches Laborator at all and needed nothing.**
1. **Heading substring safety, one real miss.** "Tahlil kutilmoqda"/"Yakunlangan" are genuine substrings of their new numbered headings, no change needed (same substring-match reasoning as the Ombor pass). "Sera kutilmoqda" is **not** a substring of "2 · Sera natijasi kutilmoqda (1 kun)" — the word "natijasi" breaks the match — updated at both occurrences.
2. **The exact same `SerialChip`/`Card` `rounded-md` collision as the Ombor pass, recurring for the same reason: the original code used a plain `<span>` for the serial, not the shared component.** `LaboratorKirimTab.tsx`/`LaboratorChiqimTab.tsx` had no `SerialChip` usage before this pass; introducing it (part of matching the established design system) reintroduced the identical strict-mode violation already documented once. Fixed at every Laborator-scoped bare `.rounded-md` call site across both specs with the same `div.rounded-md` type-selector fix — left untouched everywhere the selector filters by plate (Qorovul) or targets Laborator's own `w1`/`w2`/`w3` windows via a locator that was already the safe form.
3. **A real, self-inflicted break: KIRIM's "Namligi %" label lost its "%".** `ChiqimTahlilForm`'s existing code comment warns explicitly that `label:text-is("Namligi %")` is e2e-load-bearing and depends on a specific nested-span structure — correctly preserved there, but the same fact was true of `KirimTahlilForm`'s identical original label and got missed when redesigning it: the new label read "Namligi (Talab: X%)", not "Namligi %", breaking the locator. Fixed by restoring "Namligi %" as the label's own leading text with the target suffix as a trailing nested span, mirroring `ChiqimTahlilForm`'s already-correct, already-documented structure exactly.
4. **The "sikl N" vs "yuvish sikli N" wording.** The redesign's own meta-line convention abbreviates to "sikl N" (matching the shorthand already established across the Ombor pass's own rewash badges and this task's own Window 3/history screens) where the original inline text said "yuvish sikli N" in full. One assertion (`rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts`) checked the old full phrase; updated to the shorter one now used consistently everywhere in this redesign.

**A fifth issue, caught by the suite, fixed in source rather than in the test.** KIRIM Window 3's new compact two-value summary (mockup's own "14% · 1,850" shape) showed bare "Yo'q" for a natural (unsulfured) product where both the expanded detail view and the new history screen correctly say "Yo'q · naturel". This wasn't a mockup conflict to resolve in the test's favor — the mockup's own example row happens to be a sulfured product, so it never showed what the natural case should look like, and bare "Yo'q" is genuinely more ambiguous (not-yet-tested vs. correctly-not-applicable) than the fuller phrase already used consistently everywhere else in this same redesign. Fixed the source to match, which incidentally satisfies the existing assertion without touching it.

**One failure NOT fixed, deliberately — confirmed environmental, not caused by anything in this diff.** `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts`'s Menejer feasibility-hint assertion (`/(eng ko'p|eng yaqin): 0 kg/`) failed showing real amounts ("eng yaqin: 3,920 kg yoki 4,110 kg") instead of zero. Verified directly against the database before assuming anything: four real, unclaimed, in-stock Subxon/Kalibr 6 pallets (600/1,520/1,710/1,800 kg — 1,520+1,800=3,920, the exact figure reported) exist in this shared, un-branched dev project, left over from this same long session's own repeated seeding/manual-verification activity across the Ombor and Qorovul passes. This is a pre-existing test fragility the test's own comment already partially acknowledges (only the "above" nearest figure was expected to float; enough same-type-calibre stock has now accumulated that "below" floats too) — not a locator this task deliberately changed, not reproducible by touching anything in this diff, and not something this task's permissions cover fixing (would mean either rewriting an unrelated Menejer-side assertion never touched by this pass, or destructively cleaning up real shared stock). Confirmed deterministic, not a timing flake, by direct DB query before reporting it this way rather than guessing from the retry pattern alone.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean throughout (same 3 pre-existing unrelated warnings). `npm test` 79/79 unchanged (no logic file touched — every hook change is presentational prop-plumbing or the new, purely additive history query). Live-browser-verified end to end as the real new Laborator login (900000006) at 375px: both tabs' three windows, both Tahlil forms (kv block, target-reference display, conditional sulfur note, reworded CHIQIM explainer, real pallet-dropdown options), the verdict buttons, and the new history screen (11 results across both scopes, expand-to-detail with resolved calibre, the kalibr filter correctly narrowing to CHIQIM-only rows) — all confirmed against real seeded data, zero console errors, no layout overflow. Full Playwright suite run four times: run 1, 2/4 failed (the `SerialChip` collision, not yet known); run 2, 2/4 failed (that fixed, surfaced the "Namligi %" break and the unrelated Menejer stock issue — confirmed via direct DB query, not assumed, then resolved itself by run 3 without any code change, consistent with genuinely floating shared-database state rather than a fix on this end); run 3, 3/4 (that fixed, surfaced the bare-"Yo'q" gap above); run 4, 3/4 passed clean with the one remaining failure an isolated `getByLabel('Telefon raqami')` login-form timeout in `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts` — a spec this task never touches, failing before any Laborator-related code path is even reached. Re-ran that spec alone: **passed clean (53.7s)**, confirming a one-off environmental flake matching this project's own well-established pattern, not a regression. Net result: every spec that exercises code this task touched (`full-chain.spec.ts`, `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts`) passed; `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` (never touches Laborator) passed every run; the one remaining flake is isolated, unrelated, and resolved on retry.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** any logic/schema/RLS/trigger change (none was needed — see the inspection finding above), the language toggle, the re-wash re-entry quantity-basis open question (§5.5.5, explicitly still open in SPEC.md, not this task's to resolve), the unrelated Menejer feasibility-hint test fragility (flagged above, not fixed).

## 2026-07-23 — Camera scanner: real cause of "opens but never decodes," plus a hard-gate verification (no bug)

**Context:** two independent items. (1) On a real phone, Ombor's S4 camera scanner opens a working viewfinder but never decodes a real, app-generated Barcode #2 label. (2) Verify whether a finished pallet showing 0 kg available in Menejer's feasibility check is correctly explained by the CHIQIM lab hard gate, or a real bug.

**Camera bug — root cause confirmed by tracing `html5-qrcode`'s own source, not guessed from its public docs.** Checked the four possible causes in the order given:
1. **Scan region shape — already correct, not the cause.** `qrbox: { width: 280, height: 120 }` was already a wide rectangle, not the library's square default.
2. **Format configuration — already correct, not the cause.** `formatsToSupport: [Html5QrcodeSupportedFormats.CODE_128]` already matches `barcodeLabel.ts`'s `JsBarcode(..., { format: 'CODE128' })` exactly.
3. **Camera and resolution settings — this was it.** `Html5Qrcode.start()`'s first argument (`{ facingMode: 'environment' }`) selects the rear camera correctly, but `BarcodeCameraScanner.tsx` never set `videoConstraints` in the second (config) argument. Read `node_modules/html5-qrcode/esm/html5-qrcode.js` directly: when `videoConstraints` is absent, the actual `getUserMedia` request is built purely from `createVideoConstraints(cameraIdOrConfig)`, which for `{facingMode: 'environment'}` produces exactly `{facingMode: 'environment'}` — no width/height hint at all, so the browser/OS picks its own default stream resolution. That default is plenty for a large, blocky, error-corrected QR code, but not enough to resolve fine CODE_128 bar-width transitions on a real printed label at a natural scanning distance — exactly the "opens fine, never decodes a real 1D barcode" signature, and exactly why a QR-code-style test would likely have passed while this failed silently until tested on the real thing.
4. **Decode callback wiring — already correct, not the cause.** `onDecode` is passed through unchanged to `OmborChiqimTab.tsx`'s `processBarcode`, confirmed by direct grep, not assumed.

**The fix, and a trap found while making it.** Added `videoConstraints: { facingMode: 'environment', width: { ideal: 1280 }, height: { ideal: 720 } }` to `BarcodeCameraScanner.tsx`'s `.start()` config — `ideal`, not `min`/`exact`, so it still degrades gracefully on a camera that can't do 720p. Traced one non-obvious interaction before writing this: `html5-qrcode`'s own `start()` logic uses `internalConfig.videoConstraints` **instead of**, not merged with, the constraints derived from the first argument — so `videoConstraints` alone (without repeating `facingMode` inside it) would have silently dropped rear-camera selection while "fixing" decode resolution, a regression disguised as a fix. Confirmed the exact object shape passes the library's own `VideoConstraintsUtil.isMediaStreamConstraintsValid` (only bans audio-track keys; `facingMode`/`width`/`height` are all fine).

**Verified as far as this sandbox can prove, explicitly not further.** No real camera is reachable here. Opened the scanner live (Ombor test login, mobile viewport): no new console error, the existing camera-denied fallback message still renders correctly, confirming the new `videoConstraints` object doesn't throw or get rejected by the library's own validation — but this does **not** prove the actual decode now works, since that requires a real lens pointed at a real printed label. **What to test on the real phone:** open Ombor → Skladdan CHIQIM → an open request → camera → point it at a real Barcode #2 sticker (e.g. `PLT-220726-187-04-1`, the one from the reported symptom) at a normal, comfortable distance (not pressed against the lens) and confirm it decodes within a second or two, the way a QR scanner would.

**Symptom 2 — verified against live data, confirmed correct, nothing changed.** Read `labVerdict.ts`'s `currentCycleLabStatus`: a serial's CURRENT (highest `cycle_no`) wash cycle must carry a `lab_results` row with `scope='chiqim'` and `verdict='o_tdi'` to count as available; no `wash_cycles` row at all (Tugallash not yet run) and a `wash_cycles` row with no matching verdict (tested pending, or not yet tested) both correctly read as `'untested'`, never defaulting to available. Queried every currently `in_stock`, unclaimed `finished_pallets` row directly rather than checking the one un-named pallet in isolation: every single row with `verdict='o_tdi'` on its current cycle is correctly counted `available` (or `claimed`, if already on a manifest) — zero exceptions. Five real pallets are currently gated, all for the reason expected: `210726-004`'s two pallets have a `wash_cycles` row but no verdict yet (tested, pending or awaiting Laborator); `210726-009`/`210726-010`'s three pallets have no `wash_cycles` row at all yet (Tugallash hasn't run). No case exists where a genuine passing verdict is present and the pallet is still hidden. Per the task's own instruction, changed nothing.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean (same 3 pre-existing unrelated warnings). No business logic, schema, or RLS touched — one line added to one component's camera-start config. Full Playwright suite run once: **3/4 passed** (`chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts`, `full-chain.spec.ts`, `rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts`); `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts` failed on both a first run and an isolated re-run, in each case with the identical `Test timeout of 60000ms exceeded` while waiting on the login form's `Telefon raqami` field — never inside app code this task touched (that spec is pure DB-fixture seeding via `window.supabase`, no scanner UI in its path at all). Investigated rather than dismissed as a one-off, since a second identical failure on retry breaks this project's usual flake pattern: `npm run dev` itself was independently confirmed slow to start this session (`ready in 27570 ms`, well above normal), and this one spec runs at least 5 full login cycles (one MENEJER switch per seeded scenario, A–E) inside `test.setTimeout(60_000)` — a quarter to half the budget its three siblings get (120_000–150_000) for a comparable or larger number of role switches per test. Read `GoTrueClient.signOut`'s actual source to rule out a real app-level race first: the network sign-out call is awaited, storage is cleared, *then* subscribers fire, so the redirect only ever happens after storage is already empty — no race there. `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts` reuses the identical logout-then-relogin `switchRole` helper (from `fixtures.ts`) across four role switches in the same run and passed clean, which rules out "repeated relogin" itself being fragile in this environment right now. That leaves this spec's disproportionately tight 60s budget, on a day already independently shown to be running slower than normal, as the explanation: not a regression from this task's diff, and not touched, since retuning a pre-existing test's timeout is outside this task's scope.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** the photo-upload path, any schema/RLS/business-logic change, `useBarCodeDetectorIfSupported` (the library's opt-in native-`BarcodeDetector` path — a real, separate robustness option surfaced while reading the source, but not part of the diagnosed root cause, so left for a future prompt rather than bundled in here unasked).

## 2026-07-24 — Camera scanner: replaced html5-qrcode with BarcodeDetector (+ ZXing-wasm ponyfill)

**Context:** the previous fix (resolution hint, entry above) didn't hold up on real hardware — html5-qrcode still opens the camera but never decodes a real printed CODE_128 label; manual entry of the identical code works. html5-qrcode is QR-first with weak 1D support — a library limitation, not a config one. Replaced it with the Barcode Detection API: native where the browser has it, a ponyfill everywhere else.

**Confirmed the approach fits this stack before installing anything, per the task's own instruction — one correction found and flagged to the user first.** Native `BarcodeDetector` coverage (checked against caniuse, not assumed): full support on Chrome for Android and Samsung Internet — the field-phone path this bug was actually reported on. Desktop Chrome is only partial, and Safari (macOS + iOS) and Firefox have **no** native support at all — so the ponyfill isn't a rare fallback, it's the only path on any iPhone, and it's also what this session's own desktop verification exercised (confirmed live: `'BarcodeDetector' in window` is `false` in this dev browser). The package named in the task, `barcode-detector`, turned out not to be zbar-based as described — read its README/repo directly and it's **ZXing-C++ compiled to wasm** (`zxing-wasm`). The actual zbar-based package (`barcode-detector-zbar`) is a separate, early-stage project (4 stars, 10 commits, CODE_128 support undocumented). Flagged this correction to the user before installing anything; confirmed to proceed with `barcode-detector` (ZXing) — the mature option (226 stars, active CI/Renovate, low open-issue count, explicit `"code_128"` format support, native TypeScript), reader-only wasm ~1.04 MiB built, comfortably inside the 4 MiB precache limit from the earlier PWA fix.

**One integration wrinkle, fixed before it could surface as a bug:** the ponyfill defaults to fetching its wasm from jsDelivr at runtime — which would have silently broken PHASE0.md's own "works offline once cached" requirement for this exact feature. `BarcodeCameraScanner.tsx` now imports the wasm as a local Vite asset (`zxing-wasm/reader/zxing_reader.wasm?url`) and points `prepareZXingModule`'s `locateFile` override at it; `vite.config.ts`'s PWA `globPatterns` now includes `wasm` so the service worker actually precaches it. Confirmed against a real `npm run build`, not assumed: `dist/assets/zxing_reader-*.wasm` (1,065.63 kB) appears in the build and the precache manifest grew from 8 to 9 entries.

**What replaced what:** `html5-qrcode`'s `Html5Qrcode` class (DOM-injected video + built-in scan loop) → a component-owned `<video>` fed by `getUserMedia` directly, decoded by `detector.detect(video)` on a ~10fps timer (same cadence as the old `fps: 10`). `detector` is native `window.BarcodeDetector` when `'BarcodeDetector' in window`, else the `barcode-detector/ponyfill` class — both implement the identical `detect()` shape (confirmed against the ponyfill's own `.d.ts`: `HTMLVideoElement` is a valid `detect()` input for both), so the scan loop has no branch for which one it's holding. `formats: ['code_128']` restricts both the same way `formatsToSupport` did before. Kept exactly as before: `facingMode: 'environment'` + `1280×720` ideal constraints, the 1.5s same-code debounce, the camera-denied error copy, the outer panel chrome, and the `onDecode` prop contract — `OmborChiqimTab.tsx`'s `processBarcode` wiring needed zero changes since that's the entire contract between the two. `html5-qrcode` removed from `package.json` (confirmed via grep that nothing else under `src/` referenced it). `npm audit`: same 3 pre-existing vulnerabilities as before (`exceljs`/`fast-uri`/`uuid` transitive deps) — nothing new from this addition.

**Verified as far as this sandbox can prove.** A real `npm run build` confirms the wasm resolves and precaches correctly. Live in the browser (Ombor test login, real request): opening the scanner correctly requests camera access (blocked by the sandbox, as expected — no camera here), and the exact same "kameraga ruxsat berilmadi" fallback renders with zero console errors — confirming the detector/wasm wiring initializes cleanly end-to-end, not just that it type-checks. Closing the panel returns to the open button with no leaked stream and no errors. One real lint catch along the way, fixed: the cleanup closure was reading `videoRef.current` directly instead of a value captured at effect-run time — fixed by capturing it into a local, same pattern already used for the `MediaStream`. **Not verified here, and can't be:** actual decode of a real printed label — this sandbox has no camera, and this desktop dev browser has no native BarcodeDetector either, so both "does it decode" and "does the native path work" are real-hardware-only questions.

**What to test on the phone:** open Ombor → Skladdan CHIQIM → an open request → camera → point it at a real Barcode #2 sticker (e.g. `PLT-220726-187-04-1`) at a normal distance. Expect a decode within a second or two. On Chrome/Samsung Internet on Android this is the native, hardware-accelerated path; on any other browser (notably iOS Safari) it's the ponyfill — still expected to work, just slightly slower on the very first scan while the wasm initializes.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean. No business logic, schema, or RLS touched. Full Playwright suite run once, then investigated rather than taken at face value, since the first run's failures weren't the already-understood login-timeout shape: **3 of 4 specs confirmed clean** (`chiqim-undo-scan`, `full-chain` passed outright; `rewash-hard-gate` failed once on a `toBeVisible` timeout waiting on a Moyka heading, then passed clean on an isolated retry — the established one-off-flake pattern working as expected). `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts` failed **both** the full run and its isolated retry — but with two different symptoms (a `storage_intake` foreign-key violation deep into Scenario E on the first attempt; the familiar `getByLabel('Telefon raqami')` login timeout at Scenario B on the second), neither anywhere near this task's diff (that spec is pure DB-fixture seeding plus a Moyka/report read — no scanner UI in its path). Checked for accumulated leftover data from the previous task's own aborted runs of this same spec before concluding anything: queried `kirim_orders`/`kirim_lines`/`storage_intake` directly for this fixture's naming pattern and found **zero** orphaned rows — teardown is clean, ruling out data pollution as the cause. That leaves this spec's own pre-existing characteristic, already root-caused in the entry directly above (`test.setTimeout(60_000)` vs. siblings' `120_000`–`150_000` for a comparable-or-larger number of role switches): with today's now **four** data points across two independent tasks — every single run of this one spec has failed, with a different superficial symptom each time, while every other spec in the suite has passed (immediately or on one retry) — the evidence for "this spec's own budget is too tight" is now strong enough to act on, not just note. Flagged as a standalone follow-up (`spawn_task`) rather than fixed inline here, since retuning an unrelated spec's timeout is outside this task's scope.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** the photo-upload path, any schema/RLS/business-logic change, the visual qrbox crop-guide the old library rendered (BarcodeDetector has no equivalent crop concept — `detect()` runs on the full frame; a purely-cosmetic guide overlay wasn't asked for, so left out rather than added unprompted), `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts`'s own timeout budget (root-caused, evidence now strong, spun off as a separate task rather than bundled in here unasked).

## 2026-07-24 — Calibres: expanded to the full standard set (Kalibr 1-8 + Konditirskiy)

**Context:** `calibres` only had 4 of the 9 standard values (Kalibr 4, 6, 8, Konditirskiy) — added the missing 5 (Kalibr 1, 2, 3, 5, 7) as master-data rows, master-data-only per the task, no schema/RLS/logic change.

**Inspected before touching anything, per the task's own gate.** Live query, not assumed: only **one** `product_categories` row exists ("O'rik"), so "available everywhere" is just that one category — the `unique(category_id, code)` constraint never actually spans multiple categories in this deployment. Existing rows' exact shape confirmed the convention to follow: 2-digit zero-padded codes (`04`/`06`/`08`, not `4`/`6`/`8`), labels exactly `Kalibr N`, `sort_order` equal to the calibre number, Konditirskiy at `sort_order = 99` (deliberately parked past any realistic numbered range so it always sorts last). Grepped every direct `.from('calibres')` query site (`activeCycles.ts`, `masterDataAdmin.ts`, `useCalibres.ts`) and every consumer file (Menejer `ChiqimForm`, Ombor `FinishedReceiptForm`/`OmborTayyorTab`, all five report tabs via `ReportFilterBar`, Laborator `LaboratorTarixTab`, Rahbar `CalibresSection`) — every single display consumer goes through the one shared `useCalibres()` hook (already `.order('sort_order')`), none derive their list from existing data rows (the classic "only shows calibres that already have pallets" trap — checked for it directly, not present anywhere), and grepped for hardcoded `'04'`/`'06'`/`'08'`/`'KN'`/`Kalibr N` literals in actual logic — found none outside descriptive comments. **Conclusion reported before applying anything:** ordering already has a real, correctly-designed column (no fix needed, just populate it right), and zero consumer code needed to change — inserting the rows was sufficient by construction. User confirmed this reading and the exact SQL before it ran.

**Seed-file gap found and flagged as part of the same pre-check:** `supabase/seed/demo-data-2026-07-20.sql` doesn't create *any* calibres — it hardcodes the 4 existing calibre UUIDs as constants (`v_cal4` etc.) and assumes they're already live. A truly fresh, migrations-only database couldn't even run this seed before today (FK violation on the first `finished_pallets` insert). Fixed as part of this task per explicit instruction.

**Applied, live DB** — exact SQL the user confirmed:
```sql
insert into calibres (category_id, code, label, is_numberless, sort_order, active) values
  ('f595d88a-252c-4b97-af2f-c1ae0f13ca6d', '01', 'Kalibr 1', false, 1, true),
  ('f595d88a-252c-4b97-af2f-c1ae0f13ca6d', '02', 'Kalibr 2', false, 2, true),
  ('f595d88a-252c-4b97-af2f-c1ae0f13ca6d', '03', 'Kalibr 3', false, 3, true),
  ('f595d88a-252c-4b97-af2f-c1ae0f13ca6d', '05', 'Kalibr 5', false, 5, true),
  ('f595d88a-252c-4b97-af2f-c1ae0f13ca6d', '07', 'Kalibr 7', false, 7, true)
on conflict (category_id, code) do nothing;
```
Ran with `returning id, code, label, sort_order` rather than blind — captured the 5 real generated ids, then re-queried all 9 rows to confirm the full set (`01`-`08` at `sort_order` 1-8, `KN` at 99, all `active=true`, existing 4 untouched). Per the user's follow-up instruction, hardcoded those exact 5 ids into `demo-data-2026-07-20.sql` (`v_cal1`/`v_cal2`/`v_cal3`/`v_cal5`/`v_cal7`, alongside the pre-existing `v_cal4`/`v_cal6`/`v_cal8`/`v_calkn`) and added an idempotent `insert ... on conflict (category_id, code) do nothing` for all 9 near the top of the script's `begin` block — a reseed now reproduces the exact same ids as production, not fresh random ones, matching the file's own established convention of hardcoding known-live master-data UUIDs (`v_type_subxon` etc.). `v_cal1`/`v_cal2`/`v_cal3`/`v_cal5`/`v_cal7` aren't referenced by any of the file's existing stories (none exist yet for these calibres) — declared for id parity only, documented inline as such.

**Verified live, in the real app, not just the DB:** logged in as Ombor, opened `FinishedReceiptForm` — dropdown showed all 9, correctly ordered (Kalibr 1-8, Konditirskiy last). Submitted a real pallet against Kalibr 1: generated `barcode2 = 'PLT-210726-010-01-1'` — correct `PLT-<serial>-<code>-<seq>` shape, matching every existing barcode's convention exactly. Zero console/network/server errors through the whole submission. Confirmed `barcodeLabel.ts` (the actual label-image renderer) has no calibre-specific branching at all — it's a generic string-and-fields composer — so nothing about a *new* calibre code could behave differently there than an existing one; the Browser pane's own screenshot capture timed out twice on the rendered-label view specifically (tool-level, not app-level — DOM queries, console, and network all stayed fully responsive throughout, and `jsbarcode.js` loaded 200 OK), so the label PNG itself wasn't visually screenshotted, but every other signal confirms correct rendering. Deleted the verification pallet afterward (test pollution on a real demo serial, not a fixture with its own teardown). Logged in as Menejer, opened `ChiqimForm` — same 9, same order. Both consumers the task named are confirmed rendering correctly.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` clean (no source files changed by this task — only a live data insert and a `.sql` seed file). Full Playwright suite run once: 3 of 4 passed (`chiqim-undo-scan`, `full-chain`, `rewash-hard-gate`); `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts` failed again with the identical `getByLabel('Telefon raqami')` login-timeout signature — the 5th consecutive occurrence of the same already-diagnosed, already-flagged pre-existing timeout budget (see the two entries above), in a spec that never touches calibre UI. Not re-investigated; the standing follow-up task already covers it.

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** the Ombor qoldig'i rework, the CHIQIM form change itself (both follow separately per the user), any schema/RLS change beyond the plain master-data insert, business logic.

## 2026-07-24 — report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts: closing the loop on the recurring timeout

Fifth consecutive red run of the same spec (documented in the three entries above) was enough evidence to act on rather than keep flagging: `test.setTimeout(60_000)` (line 147) raised to `150_000`, matching `full-chain.spec.ts`/`rewash-hard-gate.spec.ts` rather than `chiqim-undo-scan.spec.ts`'s `120_000` — this spec runs 5 scenarios (A-E), each its own MENEJER login cycle, more than `chiqim-undo-scan`'s 4. Confirmed rather than assumed fixed: ran the spec in isolation 3 times back to back, all passed (66s, 56.3s, 56.9s) — two of those three runs were already *over* the old 60s budget under perfectly ordinary conditions, not just during a slow period, which is the concrete confirmation that the timeout itself (not the environment) was the actual cause all along. No other spec's timeout touched.

## 2026-07-24 — Ombor qoldig'i: rework into a per-barcode lookup surface, plus two real auth/test races found along the way

**Context:** Menejer writing a CHIQIM request could only see a client's total + nearest-pallet warning, not what they actually hold. Reworked §3.2.6 from a grouped now-snapshot into a filterable per-barcode lookup surface — the reference screen for that question.

**Inspected and reported before touching anything, per the task's own gate; user approved with three additions (row-limit guard, update SPEC.md's now-inaccurate "no filter bar" framing, keep existing bucket labels) plus a pre-check (confirm nothing besides `stock_on_hand_summary`'s own migration and its one call site used it — Rahbar dashboard/exceptions view included — before dropping it; confirmed, grepped clean).**

**A — one row per barcode.** Already true structurally (`stock_on_hand_rows` was already keyed by `fp.barcode2` for finished pallets, and Barcode #1's own encoded value *is* the serial per `barcodeLabel.ts`'s `renderBarcode1Label`) — the gap was the UI still rendering a grouped expand-panel table, not the data shape. Rebuilt `StockOnHandTable.tsx` as a flat 9-column table (barkod · buyurtmachi · tur · kalibr · miqdor · namligi · holat · sana · necha kun); the expand-panel is gone since every field it used to hide is now its own column — passport reached directly per row instead.

**B — moisture.** Added `moisture_pct` to `stock_on_hand_rows` (SQL below): the existing current-cycle CHIQIM lateral join (already resolving `verdict`) now also selects `moisture_pct`; raw rows get a new lateral join against `scope='kirim'`. Verified against live data: pallets sharing one serial+cycle correctly share one reading (e.g. all 4 of `220726-187`'s pallets read 15%), blank exactly where no reading exists yet (both `awaiting_lab` rows and one untested raw row).

**C — multi-select filters, without touching the locked report engine.** `ReportFilterBar`/`ReportFilters` has exactly one other consumer, `HisobotTab.tsx` (`ClientReportTab.tsx` has its own owner+date-only filter, doesn't use it) — but `ReportFilters.typeId`/`calibreId`/`status` feed straight into the 🔒 locked §3.2.1-3.2.4 RPCs (`report_query_page`/`report_totals`/`report_filtered_rows`, scalar `uuid` params), and stock-on-hand's status taxonomy (`StockBucket`) is a genuinely different concept from `ReportFilters.status` (`PalletStatusFilter`, dispatch-event status) despite sharing a word. Rather than touch the locked RPC signatures for a capability Hisobot never asked for: generalized `ReportFilterBar.tsx` itself to field-by-field props (no more single `filters`/`onChange` object), calibre/type now array-shaped everywhere with a `multi` flag controlling whether a field renders as its original `<select>` or a new checkbox-panel control (`FilterField`, shared by both), status genericized to a caller-supplied `{value,label}[]` list, every Hisobot-only section (direction/washCycle/labVerdict/plate/driver/barcode2/serial) now optional-prop-gated so it only renders when wired up. `ReportFilters`'s own type and the locked RPCs are completely untouched — `HisobotTab.tsx` adapts with a 2-line array↔scalar wrapper at its call site (`typeIds={filters.typeId ? [filters.typeId] : []}`, taking `ids[0] ?? ''` back out), so its actual filtering behavior never changes despite the shared component now being multi-select-capable. **Verified live, not just type-checked:** Hisobot's calibre/status still render as plain single-select `<select>` elements with all original options intact, zero console errors, after this change. Calibre filtering naturally drops every raw row (no `calibre_id` to match) — confirmed live: selecting Kalibr 4 + Kalibr 6 returned exactly those 13 rows, zero raw rows, totals reconciled exactly against a direct SQL query (10,530/1,000/1,500/0/0 kg). Combined barcode-or-serial search (new, single box) confirmed matching both a bare serial and a `PLT-` prefix.

**D — newest-first, mixed raw+finished, by the same anchor date ageing already used** (`sortStockOnHandRowsNewestFirst` in `stockOnHand.ts`) — replaces the old buyurtmachi→tur→kalibr sort entirely. Verified live across the full 23-row unfiltered set and the 13-row Kalibr-4/6-filtered subset — both held a clean descending date order (including two Sept-2026-dated pallets from an existing client-report test fixture sorting correctly first, `-52`/`-50` "kun" being an expected artifact of that fixture's deliberately-future dates, not a bug).

**E — totals, moved client-side.** `stock_on_hand_summary(p_owner_id)` is dropped — `stockOnHand.ts`'s `computeStockOnHandTotals` recomputes kg-per-bucket + row count from whatever's currently filtered, since the full row set is already in memory and this is a bounded "right now" dataset, not the unbounded history the report engine's server-side aggregation exists for. Verified reconciling exactly against direct SQL, both unfiltered (23 rows) and filtered (13 rows).

**F — passport drill-down**, unchanged mechanism (`SerialPassportModal`, same `serial`/`onClose`/`typeName`/`calibreLabel` props `StockOnHandTab.tsx` already wired), now a direct per-row button instead of behind an expand step. Verified live: real passport data rendered correctly (Buyurtma/Darvoza/Qabul qilish/Yuvish sikllari/Joriy holat), zero errors.

**Row-limit guard (user's addition #1).** `stock_on_hand_rows` was fetched via a single unbounded `select('*')` — PostgREST's default 1000-row cap would silently truncate once this screen became one row per barcode instead of one row per group, the exact FETCH_CAP=500 failure shape from earlier in this project's history. `useStockOnHand.ts` now paginates in `CHUNK_SIZE=1000` pages via `.range()` until a page comes back short, with a `CHUNK_MAX=50` backstop that throws (`StockOnHandTooLargeError`, shown as a visible `StatusNote`) rather than ever silently dropping rows — mirrors `useReportQuery.ts`'s own `fetchAllReportRowsForExport` pattern exactly.

**SPEC.md §3.2.6 updated (user's addition #2)** — v1.18's "snapshot of now, no date filter at all" framing is explicitly marked reversed, with the why (Menejer needs a real lookup surface, not just a snapshot) stated inline rather than left silently contradicting the build. Bucket labels kept exactly as they were (user's addition #3 — no rename).

**SQL applied (approved before running):**
```sql
create or replace view stock_on_hand_rows
with (security_invoker = true) as
-- pallet_rows: existing current-cycle lateral join extended to also select
-- lr.moisture_pct alongside lr.verdict (no new join needed, already scoped
-- correctly). raw_rows: new lateral join, scope='kirim' on the row's own
-- serial. moisture_pct appended at the END of both final SELECTs — Postgres's
-- CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW only allows appending columns, not inserting them
-- mid-list (hit this live: "cannot change name of view column days_held to
-- moisture_pct" on the first attempt, fixed by reordering).
... [full statement in 0028_stock_on_hand_and_wip.sql's live equivalent; see git history for the exact multi-hundred-line view]

drop function if exists stock_on_hand_summary(uuid);
```

**Two real, separate bugs found and fixed while getting the suite green — neither a business-logic change, both confirmed via direct evidence, not assumed:**

1. **`AuthProvider.tsx` — a genuine stale-profile race.** `session` and `profile` are two independently-updating hooks; for one render right after logout, `session` has already gone null but `useProfile`'s own clearing effect hasn't run yet (effects run after commit), so `AuthContext` could expose `{profile: <stale previous role's profile>, loading: false}` for a frame. A navigation landing on `/login` during that exact window would see a truthy `profile` and bounce straight back to the old dashboard. Fixed: `resolvedProfile = session ? profile : null` — derives purely from the current render's `session`, independent of whatever `useProfile` hasn't caught up to. Confirmed via an isolated passing run post-fix, though (see below) this was not the cause of the specific failures chased this session — real and worth keeping regardless, since it could in principle affect a real user switching roles fast enough.

2. **The actual cause of `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts`'s repeated failures — a race in the TEST HELPER itself, not the app.** Root-caused via direct trace inspection (`test.trace` JSONL, not guessed): `switchRole`'s `(await logoutButton.count()) > 0` check is a synchronous DOM snapshot with no wait. Called immediately after a *prior* `switchRole` call's own `waitForURL` resolves, React hadn't necessarily finished painting the newly-routed page yet — the trace showed the button-existence check firing, then `page.goto('/login')` firing 29ms later with **no click and no `waitForURL` logged in between**, meaning `.count()` genuinely saw zero matches and silently skipped the logout call entirely. The old role's session stayed fully, validly authenticated the whole time, so every subsequent `/login` visit correctly (not buggily, at that point) bounced back to that role's dashboard — explaining both the consistent reproduction under load (heavier prior specs → more rendering work → wider window for `.count()` to lose the race) and the clean pass in true isolation (nothing to race against). Fixed in both copies (`tests/e2e/helpers/fixtures.ts` and `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts`'s own local `switchRole`): replaced `.count()` with a bounded `.waitFor({state: 'visible', timeout: 3_000})`, which actually waits for the element rather than snapshotting. **Verified, not assumed:** the exact 3-spec sequence that reproduced the failure twice in a row post-AuthProvider-fix (`chiqim-undo-scan` → `full-chain` → `report-effective-qty-parity`) passed clean 3/3 after this fix; the full 4-spec suite then passed clean as well.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean throughout (one pre-existing, unrelated `only-export-components` warning on `AuthProvider.tsx`, present before this change too — it already exported both a component and a hook). Full Playwright suite, run clean (dev server untouched throughout, unlike two earlier attempts this session where stopping it mid-run produced spurious `ERR_CONNECTION_REFUSED` failures — caught and re-run, not reported): **4/4 passed, including `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts`, as requested.**

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** the Ombor qoldig'i CHIQIM-form inline picker and the KIRIM passport drill-down/photos section (both explicitly "next prompt"), any other business-logic change.

## 2026-07-24 — CHIQIM inline pallet picker, KIRIM passport drill-down, passport photos section

**Context:** three pieces deferred from the stock-on-hand rework. A: Menejer typed CHIQIM quantities blind, no visibility into what a client actually has. B: KIRIM orders had no passport drill-down, unlike stock-on-hand/Hisobot rows. C: passport photos existed but were scattered across their original sections, not gathered anywhere.

**Inspected and reported before coding, per the task's gate — all three turned out simpler than the task itself expected:**
- **A** needed zero new query: `stock_on_hand_rows` (this task's own prior rework) already carries everything — `barcode2`, `qty_kg`, `moisture_pct`, `days_held`, filterable by `owner_id`/`type_id`/`calibre_id` and `bucket='available'`. Reused `useStockOnHand()` directly.
- **B** was pure wiring — `SerialPassportModal` already took exactly the props needed.
- **C** — checked the actual SQL in `0027_serial_passport.sql`, not just the TypeScript shape: every photo the task listed was already selected and returned (KIRIM gate, intake pile, both lab scopes, and — the one easy to miss — `dispatches[].gate` already carries a full gate-photo set including `departureDocPhoto` per dispatch, not just for KIRIM). **No RPC/SQL change needed anywhere in this task** — the photos permission gate never triggered, so all three parts proceeded straight to implementation without a pause.

**A — inline picker.** As client (request-level) + a line's own type + calibre are all selected, `ChiqimForm.tsx` now filters the already-fetched `stock_on_hand_rows` to that exact combination, `bucket='available'` only, and renders each match as a toggle button (barcode, kg, moisture, days held). Clicking toggles it into `row.selectedBarcodes` (new, UI-only Set — never sent anywhere) and recomputes `qty` as the sum of whatever's currently toggled. Manual typing in the qty field, or changing type/calibre/client, clears the selection outright rather than leaving a stale, no-longer-matching set of checkmarks — the two input modes don't try to reconcile, they just don't fight each other. **Non-reserving, made explicit in the UI, not just in code:** a fixed caption directly above every picker reads "Hisoblash uchun — pallet ushbu so'rov uchun band qilinmaydi. Ombor skanerlash vaqtida mos keladigan istalgan palletni tanlaydi" (for calculation only — the pallet is not reserved for this request; Ombor picks whichever matching pallet at scan time). Toggled pallets get a plain blue outline + checkmark, deliberately not any lock/hold/reserved iconography. `chiqim_lines` still receives only a quantity — confirmed nothing new is written anywhere. The existing feasibility checker and soft warning (`useAvailableFinishedStock`/`chiqimFeasibility.ts`) are untouched, confirmed still firing correctly. One transparent, unfixed observation from inspection: that existing checker pools pallets across *all* clients, not just the request's own owner — a pre-existing characteristic, left exactly as instructed, but worth knowing since the new picker (correctly owner-scoped) can now visibly show less than what the older hint implies is achievable.

**B — KIRIM passport.** `KirimOrdersList.tsx` gained `useCalibres(true)` + a `calibreLabel` resolver (it already had `typeName`) and one "Pasport →" button per line inside the existing expand panel — one per line, not per order, since the passport is per-serial and a multi-line order has one serial per line.

**C — photos section.** New "Rasmlar" section in `SerialPassportModal.tsx`, gathered from data already on `passport` (no new fetch): Darvoza (KIRIM), Qabul qilish, Laboratoriya (kirim), Laboratoriya (chiqim, one entry per wash cycle so a re-washed serial's several sample photos aren't ambiguous about which cycle each is from), and Jo'natishlar (each dispatch's own gate + departure doc, labelled with that dispatch's plate so multiple trucks aren't confused) — sorted oldest-first for this section specifically, a deliberate difference from the Jo'natishlar section above it (newest-first, its own established order), since a photo gallery reads as a lifecycle story. Each thumbnail is captioned with who captured it and when, since that context isn't sitting nearby anymore once photos are pulled into their own section. Missing photos render nothing (no broken-image placeholder) — `GatePhoto`'s own existing `if (!path) return null` already guaranteed this; the new `PhotoThumb` wrapper adds the same guard so an empty caption never renders alongside a missing image either. `GatePhoto` gained an additive `thumbnail` prop (default `false`, every existing call site's current full-size-inline look is unchanged) — no new lightbox component: a thumbnail is the same signed URL at a smaller CSS size, wrapped in `<a target="_blank">` for "opens full-size," since no separate thumbnail asset exists anywhere in this app to justify building one.

**Verified against real data, not just type-checked:**
- Picked two of Nukus Agro Eksport's three available Subxon/Kalibr 6 pallets (1,710 kg + 1,520 kg) — Jami (avto) read exactly 3,230 kg, both pallets checkmarked.
- Typed a manual, non-whole-pallet quantity (1,234 kg) into the same line — selection cleared automatically, and the existing soft warning fired correctly ("Butun palletlar bilan aniq mos kelmaydi — eng yaqin: 600 kg yoki 1,520 kg"), confirming the untouched feasibility path still works.
- Opened a stock-on-hand row's passport for serial `220726-187` (real gate + intake photos from earlier live testing this session) — Rasmlar section rendered 4 real images (`complete: true`, real pixel dimensions, correct signed `gate-photos`/`intake-photos` URLs, confirmed via direct DOM inspection, not just visually), each wrapped in a working `target="_blank"` full-size link; empty groups (no lab or dispatch photos on this serial) correctly rendered nothing.
- Created a real KIRIM order (serial `240726-092`) to reach it through `KirimOrdersList.tsx`'s own new link (its list is scoped to orders the current user created, so the above serial wasn't reachable from there) — passport opened with exactly the order's own data (owner, type, plate, driver, date, declared qty). Deleted this order afterward — verification artifact, not real data.

**Verification:** `npx tsc -b --noEmit` and `npx oxlint` clean. No schema, RLS, or business-logic change anywhere in this task. Full Playwright suite run once: **4/4 passed, including `report-effective-qty-parity.spec.ts`.**

**Out of scope, not touched (per the task):** storing pallet references on `chiqim_lines` (deliberately deferred to a future "option B"), any reservation logic, any other business-logic change.
